|----------------|-----------------------|----------------------------------|
| 溫度           | Hub / ArtiOS 規則處理 | Sync 空調指令、Act 控制、警報    |
| 濕度           | Hub / ArtiOS 規則處理 | 通風動作、警報、場景更新         |
| 光照           | Hub / ArtiOS 規則處理 | 照明場景、支援條件下窗簾相關動作 |
| 人在           | Hub / ArtiOS 規則處理 | 場景啟動、節能動作、警報         |
| 環境閾值       | Hub / ArtiOS 自動化   | Act / Sync / Panel / App 通知    |
| 感測器健康事件 | Runtime 健康更新      | 設備狀態更新、警報、日誌         |

## **8.7 Vision Event Flow**

## **8.7 視覺事件流**

**EN  
**Vision Event Flow defines how visual events from Artibird Vision enter
the system. Visual events may include motion events, visual alerts,
local recording status, security awareness signals, or room-state
signals where supported.

Visual events may be processed locally by Hub and ArtiOS, synchronized
with OceanAI Cloud where supported, or sent to OceanAI Edge for
AI-assisted visual interpretation where deployed. Vision data behavior
must follow privacy, storage, access, and validation boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**視覺事件流定義來自 Artibird Vision
的視覺事件如何進入系統。視覺事件可包括移動事件、視覺警報、本地錄影狀態、安全感知信號，或受支援條件下的房間狀態信號。

視覺事件可由 Hub 與 ArtiOS 本地處理，在支援條件下與 OceanAI Cloud
同步，或在部署條件下送至 OceanAI Edge 進行 AI 輔助視覺解讀。Vision
數據行為必須遵循隱私、儲存、存取與驗證邊界。

## **8.8 Cloud Command Flow**

## **8.8 雲端指令流**

**EN  
**Cloud Command Flow defines how remote commands from OceanAI Cloud
enter the local system. A cloud command may originate from Artibird App
remote access, account-based control, cloud automation, lifecycle
service, notification action, or multi-site management.

Cloud commands should be routed to Artibird Hub and then to Artibird
Gate or target devices where supported. Cloud command execution depends
on network availability, account binding, permissions, Hub availability,
device connectivity, and validation status.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端指令流定義來自 OceanAI Cloud
的遠端指令如何進入本地系統。雲端指令可來自 Artibird App
遠端存取、基於帳號的控制、雲端自動化、生命週期服務、通知動作或多站點管理。

雲端指令應在支援條件下路由至 Artibird Hub，再到 Artibird Gate
或目標設備。雲端指令執行取決於網路可用性、帳號綁定、權限、Hub
可用性、設備連接與驗證狀態。

## **8.9 Edge Intelligence Flow**

## **8.9 邊緣智慧流**

**EN  
**Edge Intelligence Flow defines how selected sensor data, visual
context, device state, or runtime information may be sent to OceanAI
Edge for AI-assisted interpretation where deployed.

OceanAI Edge may return interpretation, recommendation, classification,
or context signals to Hub and ArtiOS. These outputs may inform
automation, alerts, energy behavior, security response, or scene
behavior where supported. Edge-assisted output must remain within
runtime priority, safety, privacy, and validation boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**邊緣智慧流定義特定感測數據、視覺上下文、設備狀態或 Runtime
資訊如何在部署條件下送至 OceanAI Edge 進行 AI 輔助解讀。

OceanAI Edge 可向 Hub 與 ArtiOS
返回解讀、建議、分類或上下文信號。這些輸出可在支援條件下影響自動化、警報、能源行為、安全回應或場景行為。Edge
輔助輸出必須保持在 Runtime 優先級、安全、隱私與驗證邊界內。

## **8.10 Sync Flow**

## **8.10 同步流**

**EN  
**Sync Flow defines how selected state, configuration, lifecycle data,
logs, historical records, account information, and system status may
synchronize between Artibird Hub and OceanAI Cloud.

Synchronization may be continuous, scheduled, event-triggered, or manual
depending on system configuration. Sync behavior depends on network
availability, cloud availability, account binding, privacy policy,
storage limits, and validation conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**同步流定義特定狀態、配置、生命週期數據、日誌、歷史記錄、帳號資訊與系統狀態如何在
Artibird Hub 與 OceanAI Cloud 之間同步。

同步可依系統配置採用連續、定時、事件觸發或手動方式。同步行為取決於網路可用性、雲端可用性、帳號綁定、隱私政策、儲存限制與驗證條件。

## **English Table**

| **Sync Data Type** | **Direction** | **Description** |
|----|----|----|
| Device state | Hub ↔ Cloud | Selected device states may synchronize |
| Configuration | Hub ↔ Cloud | Device, room, scene, and automation configuration may synchronize |
| Lifecycle data | Hub ↔ Cloud | Firmware, software, and device lifecycle information may synchronize |
| Logs | Hub → Cloud | Selected runtime, diagnostic, and security logs may synchronize where supported |
| Historical records | Hub → Cloud | Historical data may synchronize where enabled |
| Account information | Cloud → Hub / App | User, role, and binding information may synchronize |
| Alerts | Hub / Cloud → App | Event alerts may be delivered through supported channels |

## **中文表**

| **同步數據類型** | **方向** | **說明** |
|----|----|----|
| 設備狀態 | Hub ↔ Cloud | 特定設備狀態可同步 |
| 配置 | Hub ↔ Cloud | 設備、房間、場景與自動化配置可同步 |
| 生命週期數據 | Hub ↔ Cloud | 韌體、軟體與設備生命週期資訊可同步 |
| 日誌 | Hub → Cloud | 支援條件下特定 Runtime、診斷與安全日誌可同步 |
| 歷史記錄 | Hub → Cloud | 啟用條件下歷史數據可同步 |
| 帳號資訊 | Cloud → Hub / App | 用戶、角色與綁定資訊可同步 |
| 警報 | Hub / Cloud → App | 事件警報可透過受支援通道傳送 |

## **8.11 Event Categories**

## **8.11 事件類型**

## **English Table**

| **Event Category** | **Example** |
|----|----|
| User event | Switch touch, Panel action, App command |
| Sensor event | Temperature threshold, light threshold, occupancy change |
| Vision event | Motion event, visual alert, room-state signal |
| Execution event | Relay on/off, plug state, Act response |
| Sync event | IR command sent, RF command sent, appliance action |
| System event | Device online/offline, firmware update, error state |
| Cloud event | Remote command, account sync, lifecycle update |
| Edge event | AI-assisted interpretation or recommendation |

## **中文表**

| **事件類型** | **示例**                            |
|--------------|-------------------------------------|
| 用戶事件     | Switch 觸控、Panel 操作、App 指令   |
| 感測事件     | 溫度閾值、光照閾值、人在變化        |
| 視覺事件     | 移動事件、視覺警報、房間狀態信號    |
| 執行事件     | 繼電器開 / 關、插座狀態、Act 回應   |
| 同步事件     | IR 指令發送、RF 指令發送、家電動作  |
| 系統事件     | 設備在線 / 離線、韌體更新、錯誤狀態 |
| 雲端事件     | 遠端指令、帳號同步、生命週期更新    |
| 邊緣事件     | AI 輔助解讀或建議                   |

## **8.12 Data Flow Boundary**

## **8.12 數據流邊界**

**EN  
**Data and event flow must be described according to supported product
type, device capability, firmware version, software version, network
condition, cloud availability, edge deployment status, privacy policy,
and validation evidence.

A defined flow does not imply that all data types, all devices, all
third-party services, all cloud behaviors, all edge models, or all
automation paths are supported.

**ZH-TW  
**數據與事件流必須依據受支援產品類型、設備能力、韌體版本、軟體版本、網路條件、雲端可用性、Edge
部署狀態、隱私政策與驗證證據進行描述。

已定義流程不表示支援所有數據類型、所有設備、所有第三方服務、所有雲端行為、所有
Edge 模型或所有自動化路徑。

## **8.13 Validation Requirements**

## **8.13 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any data or event flow that supports a performance, reliability,
capacity, security, privacy, AI, or commercial claim must be validated
under defined conditions.

Validation should include source component, target component,
communication path, message type, expected behavior, failure behavior,
latency where applicable, and synchronization behavior where applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**任何支援性能、可靠性、容量、安全、隱私、AI
或商業宣稱的數據或事件流，都必須在明確條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含來源組件、目標組件、通訊路徑、消息類型、預期行為、故障行為、適用時的延遲，以及適用時的同步行為。

## **8.14 Chapter Conclusion**

## **8.14 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the data and event flow of the OceanAI / Artibird
system. It explains how device events, user commands, sensor data,
visual events, cloud commands, edge-assisted interpretation,
synchronization data, and system events move through the supported
runtime system.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的數據與事件流。它說明設備事件、用戶指令、感測數據、視覺事件、雲端指令、Edge
輔助解讀、同步數據與系統事件如何在受支援 Runtime 系統中流動。

chap 9 連接與網路

# **chap 9 連接與網路**

# **9. Connectivity and Networking**

# **9. 連接與網路**

## **9.1 Purpose**

## **9.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section defines network technologies, topology, gateway roles,
local communication, cloud communication, and connectivity boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義網路技術、拓撲、網關角色、本地通訊、雲端通訊與連接邊界。

## **9.2 Connectivity and Networking Definition**

## **9.2 連接與網路定義**

**EN  
**Connectivity and networking define how supported OceanAI / Artibird
components communicate within the local environment and with cloud
services where supported.

The system may include Ethernet, Wi-Fi, BLE Mesh, Wi-Fi Mesh where
implemented and validated, local MQTT communication, App local
connection, cloud connection, gateway communication, and offline local
operation. Connectivity behavior must be defined according to supported
product variants, network conditions, firmware versions, deployment
models, and validation evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**連接與網路定義受支援 OceanAI / Artibird
組件如何在本地環境中通訊，以及在支援條件下如何與雲端服務通訊。

系統可包含 Ethernet、Wi-Fi、BLE Mesh、在已實作並驗證條件下的 Wi-Fi
Mesh、本地 MQTT 通訊、App
本地連接、雲端連接、網關通訊與離線本地運作。連接行為必須依據受支援產品版本、網路條件、韌體版本、部署模型與驗證證據進行定義。

## **9.3 Connectivity Table**

## **9.3 連接表**

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Connectivity** | **Notes** |
|----|----|----|
| Hub | Ethernet / Wi-Fi | Local runtime and MQTT services |
| Gate | Wi-Fi / Ethernet / BLE Mesh / Wi-Fi Mesh where supported | Device access and gateway communication |
| Switch | Wi-Fi / BLE Mesh depending on variant | Relay or event-node behavior |
| Panel | Wi-Fi / wired depending on variant | Room interface |
| Act | Wi-Fi / wired / variant-specific | Relay, plug, and energy execution |
| Sense | BLE / Wi-Fi / variant-specific | Sensor reporting |
| Sync | Wi-Fi / IR / RF | Appliance synchronization |
| Vision | Wi-Fi / Ethernet / variant-specific | Video and visual events |
| App | Local network / Cloud | Local and remote control |

## **中文表**

| **組件** | **連接方式** | **備註** |
|----|----|----|
| Hub | Ethernet / Wi-Fi | 本地 Runtime 與 MQTT 服務 |
| Gate | Wi-Fi / Ethernet / BLE Mesh / 支援條件下 Wi-Fi Mesh | 設備接入與網關通訊 |
| Switch | 依版本使用 Wi-Fi / BLE Mesh | 繼電器或事件節點行為 |
| Panel | 依版本使用 Wi-Fi / 有線 | 房間介面 |
| Act | Wi-Fi / 有線 / 依版本 | 繼電器、插座與能源執行 |
| Sense | BLE / Wi-Fi / 依版本 | 感測上報 |
| Sync | Wi-Fi / IR / RF | 家電同步 |
| Vision | Wi-Fi / Ethernet / 依版本 | 視頻與視覺事件 |
| App | 本地網路 / Cloud | 本地與遠端控制 |

## **9.4 Network Architecture Role**

## **9.4 網路架構角色**

**EN  
**The network architecture provides the communication foundation for
supported runtime behavior. It allows device events, user commands,
sensor data, visual events, execution responses, cloud commands, and
synchronization data to move between supported components.

Artibird Hub provides the local runtime service environment. Artibird
Gate provides supported device access and gateway communication.
Artibird App provides local and remote user access where supported.
OceanAI Cloud provides remote service connectivity. OceanAI Edge
participates through the supported local network path where deployed.

**ZH-TW  
**網路架構為受支援 Runtime
行為提供通訊基礎。它使設備事件、用戶指令、感測數據、視覺事件、執行回應、雲端指令與同步數據能夠在受支援組件之間流動。

Artibird Hub 提供本地 Runtime 服務環境。Artibird Gate
提供受支援設備接入與網關通訊。Artibird App
在支援條件下提供本地與遠端用戶存取。OceanAI Cloud
提供遠端服務連接。OceanAI Edge
在部署條件下透過受支援本地網路路徑參與系統。

## **9.5 Hub Connectivity**

## **9.5 Hub 連接**

**EN  
**Artibird Hub may use Ethernet or Wi-Fi depending on product
configuration and deployment model. Hub connectivity supports local
runtime services, MQTT services, web services, state management,
automation, synchronization, and communication with supported devices,
Gate, App, Cloud, and Edge.

Where reliability is required, Ethernet should be preferred when
available. Wi-Fi connectivity should be validated under defined network
conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**Artibird Hub 可依產品配置與部署模型使用 Ethernet 或 Wi-Fi。Hub
連接支援本地 Runtime 服務、MQTT 服務、Web
服務、狀態管理、自動化、同步，以及與受支援設備、Gate、App、Cloud 與 Edge
的通訊。

在需要較高可靠性的場景中，如條件允許，應優先使用 Ethernet。Wi-Fi
連接應在明確網路條件下完成驗證。

## **9.6 Gate Connectivity**

## **9.6 Gate 連接**

**EN  
**Artibird Gate provides device access and gateway communication for
supported Artibird devices. Depending on product variant and
implementation, Gate may support Wi-Fi, Ethernet, BLE Mesh, and Wi-Fi
Mesh where implemented and validated.

Artibird Gate is a system-level device access gateway. It should not be
described as a simple Wi-Fi accessory. Gate connectivity must be defined
according to supported protocols, device categories, firmware version,
network topology, and capacity validation.

**ZH-TW  
**Artibird Gate 為受支援 Artibird
設備提供設備接入與網關通訊。依產品版本與實作情況不同，Gate
可在已實作並驗證條件下支援 Wi-Fi、Ethernet、BLE Mesh 與 Wi-Fi Mesh。

Artibird Gate 是系統級設備接入網關，不應被描述為簡單 Wi-Fi 配件。Gate
連接能力必須依受支援協議、設備類別、韌體版本、網路拓撲與容量驗證進行定義。

## **English Table**

| **Gate Connectivity Mode** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Wi-Fi | Provides wireless local network participation where supported |
| Ethernet | Provides wired backhaul or wired local network access where supported |
| BLE Mesh | Provides access for supported BLE Mesh device categories |
| Wi-Fi Mesh | Supported only where implemented and validated |
| Gateway communication | Allows device events and commands to pass between devices and Hub / ArtiOS |
| Device onboarding | Supports device joining and registration where implemented |

## **中文表**

| **Gate 連接模式** | **說明**                                         |
|-------------------|--------------------------------------------------|
| Wi-Fi             | 在支援條件下提供無線本地網路參與                 |
| Ethernet          | 在支援條件下提供有線回程或有線本地網路接入       |
| BLE Mesh          | 為受支援 BLE Mesh 設備類別提供接入               |
| Wi-Fi Mesh        | 僅在已實作並驗證條件下支援                       |
| 網關通訊          | 使設備事件與指令可在設備與 Hub / ArtiOS 之間傳遞 |
| 設備入網          | 在已實作條件下支援設備加入與註冊                 |

## **9.7 Device Connectivity**

## **9.7 設備連接**

**EN  
**Supported Artibird devices may connect through different connectivity
paths depending on product type and product variant. Switch, Panel, Act,
Sense, Sync, and Vision may use Wi-Fi, BLE Mesh, wired communication, IR
/ RF, Ethernet, or variant-specific communication methods where
supported.

Device connectivity must be defined by product engineering
specifications and validated under defined deployment conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**受支援 Artibird
設備可依產品類型與產品版本透過不同連接路徑接入系統。Switch、Panel、Act、Sense、Sync
與 Vision 可在支援條件下使用 Wi-Fi、BLE Mesh、有線通訊、IR /
RF、Ethernet 或依版本定義的通訊方式。

設備連接能力必須由產品工程規格書定義，並在明確部署條件下完成驗證。

## **English Table**

| **Product Type** | **Possible Connectivity Path**                           |
|------------------|----------------------------------------------------------|
| Switch           | Wi-Fi / BLE Mesh depending on variant                    |
| Panel            | Wi-Fi / wired depending on variant                       |
| Act              | Wi-Fi / wired / variant-specific                         |
| Sense            | BLE / Wi-Fi / variant-specific                           |
| Sync             | Wi-Fi / IR / RF                                          |
| Vision           | Wi-Fi / Ethernet / variant-specific                      |
| Hub              | Ethernet / Wi-Fi                                         |
| Gate             | Wi-Fi / Ethernet / BLE Mesh / Wi-Fi Mesh where supported |

## **中文表**

| **產品類型** | **可能連接路徑**                                    |
|--------------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| Switch       | 依版本使用 Wi-Fi / BLE Mesh                         |
| Panel        | 依版本使用 Wi-Fi / 有線                             |
| Act          | Wi-Fi / 有線 / 依版本                               |
| Sense        | BLE / Wi-Fi / 依版本                                |
| Sync         | Wi-Fi / IR / RF                                     |
| Vision       | Wi-Fi / Ethernet / 依版本                           |
| Hub          | Ethernet / Wi-Fi                                    |
| Gate         | Wi-Fi / Ethernet / BLE Mesh / 支援條件下 Wi-Fi Mesh |

## **9.8 Local MQTT Communication**

## **9.8 本地 MQTT 通訊**

**EN  
**Local MQTT communication may be used by Artibird Hub and ArtiOS to
support local messaging, state reporting, event routing, device control,
automation, scene execution, and internal runtime communication where
implemented.

The MQTT broker location, topic structure, authentication method,
message format, Quality of Service behavior, retained messages, message
rate, and failure behavior must be defined in related technical
documents or implementation specifications.

**ZH-TW  
**本地 MQTT 通訊可在已實作條件下由 Artibird Hub 與 ArtiOS
用於支援本地消息、狀態上報、事件路由、設備控制、自動化、場景執行與內部
Runtime 通訊。

MQTT Broker 位置、Topic
結構、身份認證方式、消息格式、服務品質行為、保留消息、消息速率與故障行為，必須在相關技術文件或實作規格中定義。

## **English Table**

| **MQTT Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Broker location | Where the MQTT broker runs |
| Topic structure | Naming rules for device, room, state, command, event, and system topics |
| Authentication | How clients authenticate to the broker |
| Message format | Payload structure and supported message types |
| QoS behavior | Required quality of service level where applicable |
| Retained message policy | Which messages may be retained |
| Message rate | Supported throughput under defined conditions |
| Failure behavior | Behavior when broker, client, or network is unavailable |

## **中文表**

| **MQTT 項目** | **必須定義內容**                                  |
|---------------|---------------------------------------------------|
| Broker 位置   | MQTT Broker 運行位置                              |
| Topic 結構    | 設備、房間、狀態、指令、事件與系統 Topic 命名規則 |
| 身份認證      | 客戶端如何向 Broker 認證                          |
| 消息格式      | Payload 結構與受支援消息類型                      |
| QoS 行為      | 適用條件下所需服務品質等級                        |
| 保留消息策略  | 哪些消息可被保留                                  |
| 消息速率      | 明確條件下支援的吞吐量                            |
| 故障行為      | Broker、客戶端或網路不可用時的行為                |

## **9.9 App Local Connection**

## **9.9 App 本地連接**

**EN  
**Artibird App may connect to the local system through supported local
network paths where implemented. App local connection may support device
setup, local control, room management, scene control, automation
configuration, status viewing, and local runtime interaction.

App local connection depends on local network availability, discovery
method, Hub availability, user permission, device binding, and supported
App version.

**ZH-TW  
**Artibird App 可在已實作條件下透過受支援本地網路路徑連接至本地系統。App
本地連接可支援設備設定、本地控制、房間管理、場景控制、自動化配置、狀態查看與本地
Runtime 互動。

App 本地連接取決於本地網路可用性、發現方式、Hub
可用性、用戶權限、設備綁定與受支援 App 版本。

## **English Table**

| **App Local Function** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Local discovery | Detect supported Hub, Gate, or devices on the local network |
| Local setup | Configure supported devices or local services |
| Local control | Send supported commands within the local environment |
| Room management | Manage rooms, spaces, or zones where supported |
| Scene management | Create, edit, or execute supported scenes |
| Automation configuration | Configure supported local automation |
| Status viewing | View device state, health, and runtime status |
| Offline local access | Operate defined local functions without Internet where supported |

## **中文表**

| **App 本地功能** | **說明**                                       |
|------------------|------------------------------------------------|
| 本地發現         | 在本地網路中發現受支援 Hub、Gate 或設備        |
| 本地設定         | 配置受支援設備或本地服務                       |
| 本地控制         | 在本地環境內發送受支援指令                     |
| 房間管理         | 在支援條件下管理房間、空間或區域               |
| 場景管理         | 建立、編輯或執行受支援場景                     |
| 自動化配置       | 配置受支援本地自動化                           |
| 狀態查看         | 查看設備狀態、健康狀態與 Runtime 狀態          |
| 離線本地存取     | 在支援條件下，無 Internet 時操作已定義本地功能 |

## **9.10 Cloud Connection**

## **9.10 雲端連接**

**EN  
**Cloud connection defines how supported local components communicate
with OceanAI Cloud. Cloud connection may support remote access, account
binding, synchronization, lifecycle services, alerts, historical data,
multi-site management, and firmware or software update coordination
where supported.

Cloud connection depends on Internet availability, account binding,
permission rules, cloud service availability, security configuration,
and supported product or software versions.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端連接定義受支援本地組件如何與 OceanAI Cloud
通訊。雲端連接可在支援條件下支援遠端存取、帳號綁定、同步、生命週期服務、警報、歷史數據、多站點管理與韌體或軟體更新協調。

雲端連接取決於 Internet
可用性、帳號綁定、權限規則、雲端服務可用性、安全配置與受支援產品或軟體版本。

## **9.11 Offline Mode**

## **9.11 離線模式**

**EN  
**Offline mode defines which supported local functions can continue when
Internet or cloud access is unavailable. Local device control, supported
local scenes, supported local automation, device state handling, and
physical controls may continue where required local components are
present.

Remote control, cloud synchronization, cloud alerts, account updates,
historical cloud data, and multi-site management may be unavailable or
degraded during offline mode.

**ZH-TW  
**離線模式定義 Internet
或雲端存取不可用時，哪些受支援本地功能可以繼續。本地設備控制、受支援本地場景、受支援本地自動化、設備狀態處理與實體控制，可在所需本地元件具備時繼續運作。

在離線模式下，遠端控制、雲端同步、雲端警報、帳號更新、雲端歷史數據與多站點管理可能不可用或降級。

## **English Table**

| **Function** | **Offline Availability** |
|----|----|
| Local device control | Available where required local components are present |
| Local scene execution | Available where scenes are locally configured |
| Local automation | Available where automation is locally supported |
| Physical control | Available depending on device and power condition |
| Device state handling | Available locally where supported |
| Remote control | Not available without cloud / Internet |
| Cloud synchronization | Not available or delayed |
| Multi-site management | Not available or degraded |
| Cloud alerts | Not available or delayed |
| Historical cloud data | Not available or limited |

## **中文表**

| **功能**     | **離線可用性**             |
|--------------|----------------------------|
| 本地設備控制 | 所需本地元件具備時可用     |
| 本地場景執行 | 場景已本地配置時可用       |
| 本地自動化   | 本地支援自動化時可用       |
| 實體控制     | 依設備與供電條件可用       |
| 設備狀態處理 | 支援條件下可本地處理       |
| 遠端控制     | 無雲端 / Internet 時不可用 |
| 雲端同步     | 不可用或延遲               |
| 多站點管理   | 不可用或降級               |
| 雲端警報     | 不可用或延遲               |
| 雲端歷史數據 | 不可用或受限               |

## **9.12 Capacity and Connection Limits**

## **9.12 容量與連接限制**

**EN  
**Connectivity capacity must be defined according to validated test
conditions. Capacity-related statements may include max concurrent
device connections, max devices per Gate, max devices per Hub, message
throughput, event latency, local network load, cloud synchronization
load, and reconnection behavior.

Theoretical chip capability must not be used as a final system claim
unless validated under defined hardware, firmware, network, and
deployment conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**連接容量必須依已驗證測試條件定義。容量相關項目可包括最大併發設備連接數、每個
Gate 最大設備數、每個 Hub
最大設備數、消息吞吐量、事件延遲、本地網路負載、雲端同步負載與重新連接行為。

除非已在明確硬體、韌體、網路與部署條件下完成驗證，否則不得將理論晶片能力作為最終系統宣稱。

## **English Table**

| **Capacity Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Max concurrent device connections | Total active connections under validated conditions |
| Max devices per Gate | Supported count under defined protocol and network conditions |
| Max devices per Hub | Supported count under defined service and hardware load |
| MQTT throughput | Message rate and latency under defined load |
| Event latency | Time from event generation to runtime action |
| Reconnection behavior | How devices reconnect after failure or network interruption |
| Cloud sync load | Synchronization frequency, payload size, and failure handling |
| Offline load behavior | Behavior when local system operates without cloud access |

## **中文表**

| **容量項目**         | **必須定義內容**                   |
|----------------------|------------------------------------|
| 最大併發設備連接數   | 在已驗證條件下的總活躍連接數       |
| 每個 Gate 最大設備數 | 在明確協議與網路條件下的支援數量   |
| 每個 Hub 最大設備數  | 在明確服務與硬體負載下的支援數量   |
| MQTT 吞吐量          | 明確負載下的消息速率與延遲         |
| 事件延遲             | 從事件產生到 Runtime 動作的時間    |
| 重新連接行為         | 設備在故障或網路中斷後如何重新連接 |
| 雲端同步負載         | 同步頻率、負載大小與故障處理       |
| 離線負載行為         | 本地系統無雲端存取時的運作行為     |

## **9.13 Required Networking Topics**

## **9.13 必須包含網路主題**

## **English Table**

| **Topic** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Wi-Fi | Supported bands, device role, network dependency |
| Ethernet | Supported components and deployment models |
| BLE Mesh | Supported device categories and gateway behavior |
| Wi-Fi Mesh | Supported only where implemented and validated |
| Local MQTT | Topic structure, broker location, authentication, message flow |
| App local connection | Local discovery, connection path, offline behavior |
| Cloud connection | Remote access, sync, account binding |
| Offline mode | Local functions available without Internet |
| Capacity | Max concurrent device connections and tested limits |

## **中文表**

| **主題**     | **必須定義內容**                          |
|--------------|-------------------------------------------|
| Wi-Fi        | 支援頻段、設備角色、網路依賴              |
| Ethernet     | 支援組件與部署模型                        |
| BLE Mesh     | 受支援設備類別與網關行為                  |
| Wi-Fi Mesh   | 僅在已實作並驗證條件下支援                |
| 本地 MQTT    | Topic 結構、Broker 位置、身份認證、消息流 |
| App 本地連接 | 本地發現、連接路徑、離線行為              |
| 雲端連接     | 遠端存取、同步、帳號綁定                  |
| 離線模式     | 無 Internet 條件下可用的本地功能          |
| 容量         | 最大併發設備連接數與已測限制              |

## **9.14 Connectivity Boundary**

## **9.14 連接邊界**

**EN  
**Connectivity and networking behavior must be described according to
supported product type, firmware version, hardware version, network
topology, local network quality, cloud availability, gateway
availability, Hub availability, deployment model, and validation
evidence.

Defined connectivity does not imply support for all routers, all
networks, all third-party devices, all protocols, all cloud services, or
all deployment conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**連接與網路行為必須依受支援產品類型、韌體版本、硬體版本、網路拓撲、本地網路品質、雲端可用性、網關可用性、Hub
可用性、部署模型與驗證證據進行描述。

已定義的連接能力不表示支援所有路由器、所有網路、所有第三方設備、所有協議、所有雲端服務或所有部署條件。

## **9.15 Validation Requirements**

## **9.15 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any networking claim involving capacity, range, latency, reliability,
offline behavior, mesh performance, gateway behavior, cloud
synchronization, MQTT throughput, or concurrent connections must be
validated under defined test conditions.

Validation should include hardware version, firmware version, network
topology, device count, message rate, test duration, failure scenarios,
and environmental conditions where applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及容量、範圍、延遲、可靠性、離線行為、Mesh
性能、網關行為、雲端同步、MQTT
吞吐量或併發連接的網路宣稱，都必須在明確測試條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含硬體版本、韌體版本、網路拓撲、設備數量、消息速率、測試時長、故障場景，以及適用時的環境條件。

## **9.16 Chapter Conclusion**

## **9.16 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the connectivity and networking structure of the
OceanAI / Artibird system. It explains how Hub, Gate, devices, App,
Cloud, Edge, and local runtime services communicate through supported
network paths, gateway behavior, local MQTT, cloud connection, App local
access, offline mode, and validated capacity boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird 系統的連接與網路結構。它說明
Hub、Gate、設備、App、Cloud、Edge 與本地 Runtime
服務如何透過受支援網路路徑、網關行為、本地 MQTT、雲端連接、App
本地存取、離線模式與已驗證容量邊界進行通訊。

chap 10 本地優先、雲端增強模型

# **chap 10 本地優先、雲端增強模型**

# **10. Local-First, Cloud-Enhanced Model**

# **10. 本地優先、雲端增強模型**

## **10.1 Purpose**

## **10.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section defines what works locally, what requires cloud, and what
is enhanced by cloud.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義哪些功能可本地運作、哪些需要雲端，以及哪些由雲端增強。

## **10.2 Local-First, Cloud-Enhanced Definition**

## **10.2 本地優先、雲端增強定義**

**EN  
**The Local-First, Cloud-Enhanced Model defines the operating
relationship between local runtime services and OceanAI Cloud services.

In this model, core local behavior should be maintained by Artibird Hub,
ArtiOS, Artibird Gate, and supported local devices where required
components are present. OceanAI Cloud extends the system through remote
access, synchronization, account services, alerts, lifecycle management,
historical data, analytics, and multi-site management where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**本地優先、雲端增強模型定義本地 Runtime 服務與 OceanAI Cloud
服務之間的運作關係。

在此模型中，當所需元件具備時，核心本地行為應由 Artibird
Hub、ArtiOS、Artibird Gate 與受支援本地設備維持。OceanAI Cloud
則在支援條件下透過遠端存取、同步、帳號服務、警報、生命週期管理、歷史數據、分析與多站點管理擴展系統能力。

## **10.3 Operating Principle**

## **10.3 運作原則**

**EN  
**The system should avoid making every essential operation dependent on
cloud availability. Local device control, supported scenes, and
supported automations should operate locally when Hub, Gate, ArtiOS, and
required devices are available.

Cloud services should enhance the system but should not be treated as
the mandatory execution path for all local runtime behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**系統應避免讓所有關鍵操作完全依賴雲端可用性。在 Hub、Gate、ArtiOS
與所需設備具備時，本地設備控制、受支援場景與受支援自動化應可本地運作。

雲端服務應增強系統能力，但不應被視為所有本地 Runtime
行為的必要執行路徑。

## **10.4 Capability Table**

## **10.4 能力表**

## **English Table**

| **Capability**        | **Local**     | **Cloud-Enhanced** | **Cloud Required** |
|-----------------------|---------------|--------------------|--------------------|
| Local device control  | Yes           | Optional           | No                 |
| Scene execution       | Yes / Partial | Yes                | No / Partial       |
| Automation            | Yes / Partial | Yes                | No / Partial       |
| Remote control        | No            | Yes                | Yes                |
| Multi-site management | Limited       | Yes                | Yes                |
| Account binding       | Partial       | Yes                | Yes                |
| Firmware update       | Partial       | Yes                | Partial / Yes      |
| Historical analytics  | Limited       | Yes                | Yes                |
| Alerts                | Partial       | Yes                | Partial / Yes      |
| Lifecycle management  | Limited       | Yes                | Yes                |

## **中文表**

| **能力**     | **本地**  | **雲端增強** | **是否需要雲端** |
|--------------|-----------|--------------|------------------|
| 本地設備控制 | 是        | 可選         | 否               |
| 場景執行     | 是 / 部分 | 是           | 否 / 部分        |
| 自動化       | 是 / 部分 | 是           | 否 / 部分        |
| 遠端控制     | 否        | 是           | 是               |
| 多站點管理   | 有限      | 是           | 是               |
| 帳號綁定     | 部分      | 是           | 是               |
| 韌體更新     | 部分      | 是           | 部分 / 是        |
| 歷史分析     | 有限      | 是           | 是               |
| 警報         | 部分      | 是           | 部分 / 是        |
| 生命週期管理 | 有限      | 是           | 是               |

## **10.5 Local Device Control**

## **10.5 本地設備控制**

**EN  
**Local device control refers to supported device control within the
local environment without requiring cloud execution. This may include
switching, relay control, plug control, scene execution, panel
operation, local App control, and selected automation behavior.

Local device control depends on Hub availability, ArtiOS runtime
services, device connectivity, Gate availability where applicable, user
permission, and supported product capability.

**ZH-TW  
**本地設備控制指在不需要雲端執行的情況下，於本地環境內進行受支援設備控制。這可包括開關控制、繼電器控制、插座控制、場景執行、面板操作、App
本地控制與特定自動化行為。

本地設備控制取決於 Hub 可用性、ArtiOS Runtime 服務、設備連接、適用時
Gate 可用性、用戶權限與受支援產品能力。

## **English Table**

| **Local Function** | **Required Local Components** |
|----|----|
| Local switch control | Switch, target device, local communication path |
| Local panel control | Panel, Hub / ArtiOS, target device |
| Local App control | App, local network, Hub / ArtiOS, target device |
| Local scene execution | Hub / ArtiOS, configured scene, target devices |
| Local automation | Hub / ArtiOS, rule configuration, required input device, target device |
| Local status update | Device, Hub / ArtiOS, local communication path |

## **中文表**

| **本地功能** | **所需本地組件**                               |
|--------------|------------------------------------------------|
| 本地開關控制 | Switch、目標設備、本地通訊路徑                 |
| 本地面板控制 | Panel、Hub / ArtiOS、目標設備                  |
| App 本地控制 | App、本地網路、Hub / ArtiOS、目標設備          |
| 本地場景執行 | Hub / ArtiOS、已配置場景、目標設備             |
| 本地自動化   | Hub / ArtiOS、規則配置、所需輸入設備、目標設備 |
| 本地狀態更新 | 設備、Hub / ArtiOS、本地通訊路徑               |

## **10.6 Scene Execution**

## **10.6 場景執行**

**EN  
**Scene execution may operate locally where scenes are configured in the
local runtime and required devices are available. A scene may include
lighting control, plug control, relay control, IR / RF appliance
synchronization, panel display behavior, or other supported device
actions.

Cloud may enhance scene execution by synchronizing scene configuration,
allowing remote scene control, or supporting cross-site scene management
where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**在場景已配置於本地 Runtime
且所需設備可用時，場景執行可在本地運作。場景可包含照明控制、插座控制、繼電器控制、IR
/ RF 家電同步、面板顯示行為或其他受支援設備動作。

雲端可在支援條件下透過同步場景配置、允許遠端場景控制或支援跨站點場景管理來增強場景執行。

## **10.7 Automation**

## **10.7 自動化**

**EN  
**Automation may operate locally where automation rules, input devices,
target devices, and local runtime services are available. Local
automation may be triggered by time, device events, sensor values, state
changes, user actions, or supported runtime conditions.

Cloud may enhance automation by synchronizing rule configuration,
enabling remote management, storing history, delivering alerts, or
supporting multi-site visibility where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**當自動化規則、輸入設備、目標設備與本地 Runtime
服務可用時，自動化可在本地運作。本地自動化可由時間、設備事件、感測值、狀態變化、用戶動作或受支援
Runtime 條件觸發。

雲端可在支援條件下透過同步規則配置、啟用遠端管理、儲存歷史、推送警報或支援多站點可視化來增強自動化。

## **English Table**

| **Automation Type** | **Local Availability** | **Cloud Enhancement** |
|----|----|----|
| Time-based automation | Available where local schedule is supported | Remote schedule management where supported |
| Sensor-based automation | Available with local Sense / input device and runtime rules | Historical records and remote alerts where supported |
| Scene-based automation | Available with local scene configuration | Cloud synchronization of scene configuration |
| Device-state automation | Available with local state handling | Multi-site state visibility where supported |
| Vision-based automation | Partial / where supported | Cloud history or Edge-assisted enhancement where supported |
| Energy-aware automation | Partial / where supported | Reports, analytics, and remote monitoring where supported |

## **中文表**

| **自動化類型** | **本地可用性** | **雲端增強** |
|----|----|----|
| 基於時間的自動化 | 支援本地排程時可用 | 支援條件下遠端排程管理 |
| 基於感測的自動化 | 本地 Sense / 輸入設備與 Runtime 規則可用時可用 | 支援條件下歷史記錄與遠端警報 |
| 基於場景的自動化 | 本地場景配置可用時可用 | 場景配置雲端同步 |
| 基於設備狀態的自動化 | 本地狀態處理可用時可用 | 支援條件下多站點狀態可視化 |
| 基於 Vision 的自動化 | 部分 / 支援條件下可用 | 支援條件下雲端歷史或 Edge 輔助增強 |
| 能源感知自動化 | 部分 / 支援條件下可用 | 支援條件下報告、分析與遠端監測 |

## **10.8 Remote Control**

## **10.8 遠端控制**

**EN  
**Remote control requires cloud participation. It allows users to
control supported devices, scenes, automations, or sites through
Artibird App or supported remote interfaces when Internet access,
account binding, permissions, Hub availability, and cloud service
availability are present.

Remote control does not replace local control. It extends user access
beyond the local environment where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**遠端控制需要雲端參與。當 Internet 存取、帳號綁定、權限、Hub
可用性與雲端服務可用時，用戶可透過 Artibird App
或受支援遠端介面控制受支援設備、場景、自動化或站點。

遠端控制不取代本地控制，而是在支援條件下將用戶存取能力擴展至本地環境之外。

## **10.9 Multi-Site Management**

## **10.9 多站點管理**

**EN  
**Multi-site management is primarily a cloud-enhanced capability. It may
support multiple homes, classrooms, offices, buildings, campuses, or
infrastructure sites under one account or organization structure where
supported.

Local runtime services may manage local behavior within each site, while
OceanAI Cloud may provide cross-site visibility, account management,
reporting, alerts, synchronization, and lifecycle services.

**ZH-TW  
**多站點管理主要是雲端增強能力。它可在支援條件下，在同一帳號或組織結構下管理多住宅、教室、辦公室、建築、校園或基礎設施站點。

本地 Runtime 服務可管理每個站點內的本地行為，而 OceanAI Cloud
可提供跨站點可視化、帳號管理、報告、警報、同步與生命週期服務。

## **10.10 Account Binding**

## **10.10 帳號綁定**

**EN  
**Account binding associates users, devices, rooms, sites, permissions,
and cloud services. Some local setup or local device discovery may be
possible without full cloud dependency depending on implementation, but
account-based remote access, multi-site management, and cloud
synchronization generally require cloud participation.

Account binding must follow security, privacy, and permission rules.

**ZH-TW  
**帳號綁定將用戶、設備、房間、站點、權限與雲端服務關聯起來。依實作方式不同，部分本地設定或本地設備發現可不完全依賴雲端，但基於帳號的遠端存取、多站點管理與雲端同步通常需要雲端參與。

帳號綁定必須遵循安全、隱私與權限規則。

## **10.11 Firmware Update**

## **10.11 韌體更新**

**EN  
**Firmware update may be local, cloud-enhanced, or cloud-required
depending on product type and implementation. Cloud services may provide
firmware package delivery, update availability, version management,
update records, and lifecycle coordination where supported.

Firmware update behavior must define update source, device eligibility,
version compatibility, failure behavior, rollback behavior where
supported, and validation requirements.

**ZH-TW  
**依產品類型與實作方式不同，韌體更新可為本地、雲端增強或需要雲端。雲端服務可在支援條件下提供韌體包分發、更新可用性、版本管理、更新記錄與生命週期協調。

韌體更新行為必須定義更新來源、設備資格、版本相容性、失敗行為、支援條件下回滾行為與驗證要求。

## **10.12 Historical Analytics**

## **10.12 歷史分析**

**EN  
**Historical analytics is primarily cloud-enhanced. The local runtime
may maintain limited state, logs, and recent records, while OceanAI
Cloud may provide long-term history, trends, reports, energy analysis,
device usage records, and multi-site analytics where supported.

Historical analytics must follow storage, privacy, retention, and user
permission rules.

**ZH-TW  
**歷史分析主要由雲端增強。本地 Runtime
可維護有限狀態、日誌與近期記錄，而 OceanAI Cloud
可在支援條件下提供長期歷史、趨勢、報告、能源分析、設備使用記錄與多站點分析。

歷史分析必須遵循儲存、隱私、保留與用戶權限規則。

## **10.13 Alerts**

## **10.13 警報**

**EN  
**Alerts may be generated locally, cloud-enhanced, or cloud-delivered
depending on event type and deployment configuration. Local alerts may
be shown through Panel, App local access, device indicators, or local
runtime logs where supported.

Cloud-enhanced alerts may include push notifications, remote event
delivery, multi-site alerts, historical alert records, and account-based
notification rules where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**依事件類型與部署配置不同，警報可由本地生成、雲端增強或透過雲端傳送。本地警報可在支援條件下透過
Panel、App 本地存取、設備指示燈或本地 Runtime 日誌呈現。

雲端增強警報可在支援條件下包含推送通知、遠端事件傳送、多站點警報、歷史警報記錄與基於帳號的通知規則。

## **10.14 Lifecycle Management**

## **10.14 生命週期管理**

**EN  
**Lifecycle management includes device onboarding, binding,
configuration, firmware update, diagnostics, support records,
replacement, reset, decommissioning, and service history.

Local runtime may support selected lifecycle actions, while OceanAI
Cloud may enhance lifecycle management through account-based records,
update coordination, service history, diagnostics, and multi-site device
management where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**生命週期管理包括設備入網、綁定、配置、韌體更新、診斷、支援記錄、更換、重置、退役與服務歷史。

本地 Runtime 可支援特定生命週期動作，而 OceanAI Cloud
可在支援條件下透過基於帳號的記錄、更新協調、服務歷史、診斷與多站點設備管理增強生命週期管理。

## **10.15 Cloud Dependency Boundary**

## **10.15 雲端依賴邊界**

**EN  
**Cloud dependency must be clearly defined for each system capability. A
capability should not be described as fully local if it requires cloud
access. A capability should not be described as cloud-required if its
core behavior can operate locally with required local components.

Cloud dependency should be evaluated according to function type, device
type, account requirement, synchronization need, remote access
requirement, data storage requirement, and validation results.

**ZH-TW  
**每一項系統能力都必須清楚定義雲端依賴程度。如果某項能力需要雲端存取，不應描述為完全本地。如果某項能力在所需本地元件具備時可本地運作，則不應描述為必須依賴雲端。

雲端依賴應依功能類型、設備類型、帳號要求、同步需求、遠端存取需求、數據儲存需求與驗證結果進行評估。

## **English Table**

| **Dependency Type** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Local-only | Function operates without cloud where required local components are present |
| Local with cloud enhancement | Function operates locally and may be improved by cloud services |
| Cloud-required | Function requires cloud service availability |
| Cloud-degraded | Function partially operates but loses cloud-based capability |
| Cloud-unavailable | Function cannot operate without cloud |
| Hybrid | Function uses both local runtime and cloud services depending on configuration |

## **中文表**

| **依賴類型**       | **說明**                                   |
|--------------------|--------------------------------------------|
| 僅本地             | 所需本地元件具備時，功能不需要雲端即可運作 |
| 本地 + 雲端增強    | 功能可本地運作，並可由雲端服務增強         |
| 必須雲端           | 功能需要雲端服務可用                       |
| 雲端降級           | 功能可部分運作，但失去雲端能力             |
| 雲端不可用即不可用 | 無雲端時功能不可運作                       |
| 混合               | 功能依配置同時使用本地 Runtime 與雲端服務  |

## **10.16 Model Boundary**

## **10.16 模型邊界**

**EN  
**The Local-First, Cloud-Enhanced Model does not imply that every
function is fully local, nor does it imply that every function requires
cloud. Each capability must be classified according to supported
implementation, product type, deployment model, network condition, cloud
availability, user permission, and validation evidence.

This model must not be used to claim unlimited offline operation,
universal remote access, guaranteed cloud availability, or support for
unsupported devices and third-party platforms.

**ZH-TW  
**本地優先、雲端增強模型不表示所有功能都完全本地，也不表示所有功能都需要雲端。每一項能力都必須依受支援實作、產品類型、部署模型、網路條件、雲端可用性、用戶權限與驗證證據進行分類。

不得使用此模型宣稱無限制離線運作、通用遠端存取、保證雲端可用，或支援未支援設備與第三方平台。

## **10.17 Validation Requirements**

## **10.17 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any claim involving local operation, offline behavior, remote control,
cloud synchronization, cloud-enhanced analytics, firmware update,
alerts, lifecycle management, or multi-site management must be validated
under defined conditions.

Validation should include required local components, cloud availability,
network condition, user permissions, device count, firmware version,
software version, failure behavior, and expected recovery behavior where
applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及本地運作、離線行為、遠端控制、雲端同步、雲端增強分析、韌體更新、警報、生命週期管理或多站點管理的宣稱，都必須在明確條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含所需本地組件、雲端可用性、網路條件、用戶權限、設備數量、韌體版本、軟體版本、故障行為，以及適用時的預期恢復行為。

## **10.18 Chapter Conclusion**

## **10.18 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the Local-First, Cloud-Enhanced Model of the
OceanAI / Artibird system. It explains which capabilities may operate
locally, which capabilities require cloud, and which capabilities are
enhanced by cloud services under supported and validated conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的本地優先、雲端增強模型。它說明哪些能力可本地運作、哪些能力需要雲端，以及哪些能力在受支援與已驗證條件下由雲端服務增強。

chap 11 雲端架構

# **chap 11 雲端架構**

# **11. Cloud Architecture**

# **11. 雲端架構**

## **11.1 Purpose**

## **11.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section defines the cloud’s role without making the system
cloud-dependent for all core local behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**本章在不使所有核心本地行為依賴雲端的前提下，定義雲端角色。

## **11.2 Cloud Architecture Definition**

## **11.2 雲端架構定義**

**EN  
**Cloud Architecture defines how OceanAI Cloud participates in the
OceanAI / Artibird system. It provides remote services, account
management, synchronization, lifecycle services, historical data,
alerts, analytics, multi-site management, and commercial service support
where applicable.

OceanAI Cloud extends the system beyond the local environment. It should
enhance supported system behavior but should not be treated as the
required execution path for every core local function.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端架構定義 OceanAI Cloud 如何參與 OceanAI / Artibird
系統。它在適用條件下提供遠端服務、帳號管理、同步、生命週期服務、歷史數據、警報、分析、多站點管理與商業服務支援。

OceanAI Cloud
將系統能力擴展至本地環境之外。它應增強受支援系統行為，但不應被視為每一項核心本地功能的必要執行路徑。

## **11.3 Cloud Responsibilities**

## **11.3 雲端責任**

## **English Table**

| **Cloud Function** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Account management | User accounts, permissions, binding, identity |
| Device binding | Register and associate devices with accounts, homes, sites, or rooms |
| Remote access | Enable off-site device control and monitoring |
| Data synchronization | Sync state, configuration, logs, history, and lifecycle data |
| Firmware / software lifecycle | Manage OTA updates where supported |
| Historical data | Store and display historical records where enabled |
| Alerts | Send remote notifications and event alerts |
| Multi-site management | Manage multiple homes, classrooms, buildings, campuses, or sites |
| Commercial service plans | Enable paid service tiers where applicable |
| Cloud failure behavior | Define degraded operation when cloud is unavailable |

## **中文表**

| **雲端功能**        | **說明**                                 |
|---------------------|------------------------------------------|
| 帳號管理            | 用戶帳號、權限、綁定、身份               |
| 設備綁定            | 將設備註冊並關聯至帳號、住宅、站點或房間 |
| 遠端存取            | 啟用場外設備控制與監測                   |
| 數據同步            | 同步狀態、配置、日誌、歷史與生命週期數據 |
| 韌體 / 軟體生命週期 | 在支援條件下管理 OTA 更新                |
| 歷史數據            | 在啟用條件下儲存與顯示歷史記錄           |
| 警報                | 發送遠端通知與事件警報                   |
| 多站點管理          | 管理多住宅、教室、建築、校園或站點       |
| 商業服務方案        | 在適用時啟用付費服務層級                 |
| 雲端故障行為        | 定義雲端不可用時的降級運作               |

## **11.4 Account Management**

## **11.4 帳號管理**

**EN  
**Account management defines how users, roles, permissions,
organizations, homes, sites, rooms, and devices are associated within
OceanAI Cloud.

Account management may support owner, admin, user, installer, guest, or
organization-level roles where implemented. Account-based access must
follow authentication, authorization, privacy, and security
requirements.

**ZH-TW  
**帳號管理定義用戶、角色、權限、組織、住宅、站點、房間與設備如何在
OceanAI Cloud 中建立關聯。

帳號管理可在已實作條件下支援 Owner、Admin、User、Installer、Guest
或組織級角色。基於帳號的存取必須遵循身份認證、授權、隱私與安全要求。

## **English Table**

| **Account Item** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| User account | Represents a user identity within the cloud system |
| Role | Defines user permission level |
| Organization | Represents a company, school, institution, or managed group where supported |
| Home / Site | Represents a managed physical deployment location |
| Room / Space | Represents a space within a home, site, building, or campus |
| Device binding | Associates devices with accounts, spaces, and permissions |
| Permission rule | Defines what actions a user or role can perform |
| Access record | Records account-related access or change events where supported |

## **中文表**

| **帳號項目** | **說明**                                     |
|--------------|----------------------------------------------|
| 用戶帳號     | 表示雲端系統中的用戶身份                     |
| 角色         | 定義用戶權限等級                             |
| 組織         | 在支援條件下表示公司、學校、機構或受管理群組 |
| 住宅 / 站點  | 表示受管理實體部署位置                       |
| 房間 / 空間  | 表示住宅、站點、建築或校園中的空間           |
| 設備綁定     | 將設備與帳號、空間與權限建立關聯             |
| 權限規則     | 定義用戶或角色可執行的操作                   |
| 存取記錄     | 在支援條件下記錄帳號相關存取或變更事件       |

## **11.5 Device Binding**

## **11.5 設備綁定**

**EN  
**Device binding defines how supported devices are registered and
associated with a user account, home, site, room, organization, or
system deployment.

Device binding may be performed through Artibird App, Artibird Hub,
Artibird Gate, or supported cloud workflows depending on implementation.
Binding behavior must follow device identity, account permission,
security, and validation requirements.

**ZH-TW  
**設備綁定定義受支援設備如何被註冊並關聯至用戶帳號、住宅、站點、房間、組織或系統部署。

依實作方式不同，設備綁定可透過 Artibird App、Artibird Hub、Artibird Gate
或受支援雲端流程完成。綁定行為必須遵循設備身份、帳號權限、安全與驗證要求。

## **English Table**

| **Binding Item** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Device identity | Unique device identity used during binding |
| Account association | Links device to user or organization account |
| Site association | Links device to a home, site, building, classroom, or campus |
| Room assignment | Assigns device to a room, area, or zone |
| Permission check | Verifies user authority to bind or modify device |
| Security verification | Confirms trusted binding behavior where supported |
| Binding record | Stores binding result and lifecycle record where supported |

## **中文表**

| **綁定項目** | **說明**                                 |
|--------------|------------------------------------------|
| 設備身份     | 綁定時使用的唯一設備身份                 |
| 帳號關聯     | 將設備連結至用戶或組織帳號               |
| 站點關聯     | 將設備連結至住宅、站點、建築、教室或校園 |
| 房間分配     | 將設備分配至房間、區域或分區             |
| 權限檢查     | 驗證用戶是否具備綁定或修改設備的權限     |
| 安全驗證     | 在支援條件下確認可信綁定行為             |
| 綁定記錄     | 在支援條件下儲存綁定結果與生命週期記錄   |

## **11.6 Remote Access**

## **11.6 遠端存取**

**EN  
**Remote access allows users to monitor or control supported devices,
rooms, scenes, automations, or sites outside the local network where
cloud service, account binding, permission rules, and network conditions
are available.

Remote access should be treated as a cloud-enabled capability. It
extends user control beyond the local environment but does not replace
local runtime control where supported local components are present.

**ZH-TW  
**遠端存取允許用戶在雲端服務、帳號綁定、權限規則與網路條件可用時，於本地網路之外監測或控制受支援設備、房間、場景、自動化或站點。

遠端存取應被視為雲端啟用能力。它將用戶控制擴展至本地環境之外，但不取代所需本地元件具備時的本地
Runtime 控制。

## **English Table**

| **Remote Access Function** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Remote device control | Control supported devices outside the local network |
| Remote scene control | Execute supported scenes remotely |
| Remote status view | View device state, room state, or site status |
| Remote alert access | Receive alerts or notifications where supported |
| Remote configuration | Modify supported settings or rules where allowed |
| Multi-site access | Access multiple homes, classrooms, buildings, or campuses where supported |

## **中文表**

| **遠端存取功能** | **說明**                                 |
|------------------|------------------------------------------|
| 遠端設備控制     | 在本地網路之外控制受支援設備             |
| 遠端場景控制     | 遠端執行受支援場景                       |
| 遠端狀態查看     | 查看設備狀態、房間狀態或站點狀態         |
| 遠端警報存取     | 在支援條件下接收警報或通知               |
| 遠端配置         | 在允許條件下修改受支援設定或規則         |
| 多站點存取       | 在支援條件下存取多住宅、教室、建築或校園 |

## **11.7 Data Synchronization**

## **11.7 數據同步**

**EN  
**Data synchronization defines how selected state, configuration, logs,
lifecycle data, historical records, account data, and alert records may
synchronize between the local runtime system and OceanAI Cloud.

Synchronization may be continuous, scheduled, event-triggered, manual,
or delayed depending on implementation, network availability, privacy
rules, account binding, and cloud service availability.

**ZH-TW  
**數據同步定義特定狀態、配置、日誌、生命週期數據、歷史記錄、帳號數據與警報記錄如何在本地
Runtime 系統與 OceanAI Cloud 之間同步。

依實作方式、網路可用性、隱私規則、帳號綁定與雲端服務可用性不同，同步可採用連續、定時、事件觸發、手動或延遲方式。

## **English Table**

| **Sync Data Type** | **Direction** | **Description** |
|----|----|----|
| Device state | Hub ↔ Cloud | Selected device states may synchronize |
| Configuration | Hub ↔ Cloud | Device, room, scene, and automation configuration may synchronize |
| Lifecycle data | Hub ↔ Cloud | Firmware, software, and device lifecycle data may synchronize |
| Logs | Hub → Cloud | Runtime, diagnostic, security, or failure logs may synchronize where supported |
| Historical records | Hub → Cloud | Historical data may synchronize where enabled |
| Account data | Cloud → Hub / App | Account, role, and permission data may synchronize |
| Alert records | Hub / Cloud → App | Alert records may be delivered or stored where supported |

## **中文表**

| **同步數據類型** | **方向** | **說明** |
|----|----|----|
| 設備狀態 | Hub ↔ Cloud | 特定設備狀態可同步 |
| 配置 | Hub ↔ Cloud | 設備、房間、場景與自動化配置可同步 |
| 生命週期數據 | Hub ↔ Cloud | 韌體、軟體與設備生命週期數據可同步 |
| 日誌 | Hub → Cloud | 支援條件下 Runtime、診斷、安全或故障日誌可同步 |
| 歷史記錄 | Hub → Cloud | 啟用條件下歷史數據可同步 |
| 帳號數據 | Cloud → Hub / App | 帳號、角色與權限數據可同步 |
| 警報記錄 | Hub / Cloud → App | 警報記錄可在支援條件下傳送或儲存 |

## **11.8 Firmware / Software Lifecycle**

## **11.8 韌體 / 軟體生命週期**

**EN  
**OceanAI Cloud may support firmware and software lifecycle management
where implemented. This may include version availability, update
delivery, update status reporting, update history, rollback support
where available, and lifecycle records.

Firmware and software update behavior must be defined according to
product type, device eligibility, hardware version, firmware version,
software version, network condition, failure behavior, and validation
requirements.

**ZH-TW  
**OceanAI Cloud
可在已實作條件下支援韌體與軟體生命週期管理。這可包括版本可用性、更新分發、更新狀態回報、更新歷史、支援條件下的回滾，以及生命週期記錄。

韌體與軟體更新行為必須依產品類型、設備資格、硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、網路條件、失敗行為與驗證要求進行定義。

## **English Table**

| **Lifecycle Function** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Version availability | Identify available firmware or software versions |
| Update delivery | Deliver update packages where supported |
| Update status | Report update progress, success, or failure |
| Update history | Record previous update activity |
| Rollback behavior | Restore previous version where supported |
| Compatibility check | Verify version compatibility before update |
| Lifecycle record | Maintain firmware, software, and device lifecycle history |

## **中文表**

| **生命週期功能** | **說明**                         |
|------------------|----------------------------------|
| 版本可用性       | 識別可用韌體或軟體版本           |
| 更新分發         | 在支援條件下分發更新包           |
| 更新狀態         | 回報更新進度、成功或失敗         |
| 更新歷史         | 記錄過往更新活動                 |
| 回滾行為         | 在支援條件下恢復至先前版本       |
| 相容性檢查       | 更新前驗證版本相容性             |
| 生命週期記錄     | 維護韌體、軟體與設備生命週期歷史 |

## **11.9 Historical Data and Analytics**

## **11.9 歷史數據與分析**

**EN  
**Historical data and analytics may be provided by OceanAI Cloud where
enabled. This may include device history, event records, energy data,
usage patterns, runtime logs, alert history, system reports, and
multi-site analytics.

Historical data and analytics must follow data retention, privacy,
account permission, storage, and validation boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**在啟用條件下，歷史數據與分析可由 OceanAI Cloud
提供。這可包括設備歷史、事件記錄、能源數據、使用模式、Runtime
日誌、警報歷史、系統報告與多站點分析。

歷史數據與分析必須遵循數據保留、隱私、帳號權限、儲存與驗證邊界。

## **11.10 Alerts and Notifications**

## **11.10 警報與通知**

**EN  
**OceanAI Cloud may deliver remote alerts and notifications where
supported. Alerts may originate from device events, sensor thresholds,
vision events, execution failures, cloud service status, security
events, lifecycle events, or system failure conditions.

Alert delivery depends on cloud availability, App permission, account
binding, notification settings, event type, and validation status.

**ZH-TW  
**OceanAI Cloud
可在支援條件下傳送遠端警報與通知。警報可來自設備事件、感測閾值、視覺事件、執行失敗、雲端服務狀態、安全事件、生命週期事件或系統故障條件。

警報傳送取決於雲端可用性、App
權限、帳號綁定、通知設定、事件類型與驗證狀態。

## **English Table**

| **Alert Source** | **Example Alert** |
|----|----|
| Device event | Device offline, device error, relay failure |
| Sensor threshold | Temperature, humidity, light, occupancy threshold |
| Vision event | Motion alert, visual security event |
| Execution failure | Act failure, Sync command failure, relay command failure |
| Security event | Unauthorized access attempt, binding change, permission change |
| Lifecycle event | Firmware update available, update failed, device replacement |
| Cloud service event | Sync delayed, remote access unavailable, cloud service degraded |

## **中文表**

| **警報來源** | **警報示例**                            |
|--------------|-----------------------------------------|
| 設備事件     | 設備離線、設備錯誤、繼電器故障          |
| 感測閾值     | 溫度、濕度、光照、人在閾值              |
| 視覺事件     | 移動警報、視覺安全事件                  |
| 執行失敗     | Act 失敗、Sync 指令失敗、繼電器指令失敗 |
| 安全事件     | 未授權存取嘗試、綁定變更、權限變更      |
| 生命週期事件 | 韌體更新可用、更新失敗、設備更換        |
| 雲端服務事件 | 同步延遲、遠端存取不可用、雲端服務降級  |

## **11.11 Multi-Site Management**

## **11.11 多站點管理**

**EN  
**Multi-site management allows users or organizations to manage multiple
homes, classrooms, offices, buildings, campuses, infrastructure sites,
or other supported deployment environments under one account or
organization structure.

OceanAI Cloud may provide cross-site visibility, account management,
device grouping, remote monitoring, alert management, reporting,
configuration synchronization, and lifecycle management where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**多站點管理允許用戶或組織在同一帳號或組織結構下，管理多個住宅、教室、辦公室、建築、校園、基礎設施站點或其他受支援部署環境。

OceanAI Cloud
可在支援條件下提供跨站點可視化、帳號管理、設備分組、遠端監測、警報管理、報告、配置同步與生命週期管理。

## **11.12 Commercial Service Plans**

## **11.12 商業服務方案**

**EN  
**Commercial service plans may be enabled by OceanAI Cloud where
applicable. These plans may support enhanced remote services, historical
analytics, multi-site management, reporting, enterprise support,
lifecycle management, or other cloud-enhanced services.

Commercial service plans must remain aligned with actual cloud
capabilities, implemented service levels, privacy policy, data retention
rules, and validated system behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**在適用條件下，商業服務方案可由 OceanAI Cloud
啟用。這些方案可支援增強型遠端服務、歷史分析、多站點管理、報告、企業支援、生命週期管理或其他雲端增強服務。

商業服務方案必須與實際雲端能力、已實作服務等級、隱私政策、數據保留規則與已驗證系統行為保持一致。

## **11.13 Cloud Failure Behavior**

## **11.13 雲端故障行為**

**EN  
**Cloud failure behavior defines how the system behaves when OceanAI
Cloud is unavailable, degraded, delayed, or unreachable.

When cloud services are unavailable, supported local functions should
continue where required local components are present. Remote access,
cloud synchronization, cloud alerts, multi-site management, cloud
analytics, account updates, and cloud lifecycle services may be
unavailable, delayed, or degraded.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端故障行為定義 OceanAI Cloud
不可用、降級、延遲或無法連接時，系統如何運作。

當雲端服務不可用時，在所需本地元件具備條件下，受支援本地功能應繼續運作。遠端存取、雲端同步、雲端警報、多站點管理、雲端分析、帳號更新與雲端生命週期服務可能不可用、延遲或降級。

## **English Table**

| **Cloud Condition** | **Expected Behavior** |
|----|----|
| Cloud available | Remote access, synchronization, alerts, analytics, and lifecycle services operate where supported |
| Cloud delayed | Synchronization, alerts, and remote status may be delayed |
| Cloud unavailable | Supported local functions continue where local components are present |
| Internet unavailable | Remote access and cloud synchronization may stop; local runtime may continue |
| Account service unavailable | Account updates, binding changes, or role changes may be delayed |
| Cloud sync failure | Local data may queue, retry, or remain local depending on implementation |
| Cloud alert failure | Remote notifications may be delayed or unavailable |

## **中文表**

| **雲端狀態** | **預期行為** |
|----|----|
| 雲端可用 | 在支援條件下，遠端存取、同步、警報、分析與生命週期服務運作 |
| 雲端延遲 | 同步、警報與遠端狀態可能延遲 |
| 雲端不可用 | 本地元件具備時，受支援本地功能繼續 |
| Internet 不可用 | 遠端存取與雲端同步可能停止；本地 Runtime 可繼續 |
| 帳號服務不可用 | 帳號更新、綁定變更或角色變更可能延遲 |
| 雲端同步失敗 | 本地數據可依實作方式排隊、重試或保留本地 |
| 雲端警報失敗 | 遠端通知可能延遲或不可用 |

## **11.14 Cloud Security and Privacy Boundary**

## **11.14 雲端安全與隱私邊界**

**EN  
**Cloud services must follow defined security and privacy requirements.
These include account authentication, role-based access control, secure
communication, data retention, user permission, device binding security,
audit logging where supported, and privacy policy compliance.

Cloud participation must not be used to imply unlimited data collection,
unrestricted remote access, unsupported AI processing, or undefined
sharing of user data.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端服務必須遵循已定義安全與隱私要求。這包括帳號身份認證、角色權限控制、安全通訊、數據保留、用戶權限、設備綁定安全、支援條件下的審計日誌，以及隱私政策合規。

不得使用雲端參與來暗示無限制數據收集、不受限制遠端存取、未支援 AI
處理或未定義的用戶數據共享。

## **11.15 Cloud Boundary**

## **11.15 雲端邊界**

**EN  
**Cloud architecture must be described according to implemented cloud
services, supported products, software versions, account configuration,
network conditions, privacy policy, security requirements, and
validation evidence.

Cloud architecture does not imply that all functions require cloud, that
all functions operate without local components, that remote access is
always available, or that all third-party services are supported.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端架構必須依已實作雲端服務、受支援產品、軟體版本、帳號配置、網路條件、隱私政策、安全要求與驗證證據進行描述。

雲端架構不表示所有功能都需要雲端、不表示所有功能可以脫離本地元件運作、不表示遠端存取永遠可用，也不表示支援所有第三方服務。

## **11.16 Validation Requirements**

## **11.16 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any cloud claim involving remote access, synchronization, account
binding, alert delivery, historical analytics, multi-site management,
firmware lifecycle, security, privacy, reliability, or commercial
service plans must be validated under defined conditions.

Validation should include account status, user role, cloud availability,
Internet condition, Hub availability, device state, software version,
firmware version, expected behavior, failure behavior, and recovery
behavior where applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及遠端存取、同步、帳號綁定、警報傳送、歷史分析、多站點管理、韌體生命週期、安全、隱私、可靠性或商業服務方案的雲端宣稱，都必須在明確條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含帳號狀態、用戶角色、雲端可用性、Internet 條件、Hub
可用性、設備狀態、軟體版本、韌體版本、預期行為、故障行為，以及適用時的恢復行為。

## **11.17 Chapter Conclusion**

## **11.17 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the Cloud Architecture of the OceanAI / Artibird
system. It explains how OceanAI Cloud provides account management,
device binding, remote access, synchronization, lifecycle services,
historical data, alerts, multi-site management, commercial service
support, and cloud failure behavior while preserving the local-first
structure of the system.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird 系統的雲端架構。它說明 OceanAI Cloud
如何提供帳號管理、設備綁定、遠端存取、同步、生命週期服務、歷史數據、警報、多站點管理、商業服務支援與雲端故障行為，同時保留系統的本地優先結構。

chap 12 邊緣智慧架構

# **chap 12 邊緣智慧架構**

# **12. Edge Intelligence Architecture**

# **12. 邊緣智慧架構**

## **12.1 Purpose**

## **12.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section defines how OceanAI Edge participates in the system as an
AI-assisted local intelligence layer.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義 OceanAI Edge 如何作為 AI 輔助本地智慧層參與系統。

## **12.2 Edge Intelligence Architecture Definition**

## **12.2 邊緣智慧架構定義**

**EN  
**Edge Intelligence Architecture defines how OceanAI Edge participates
in the OceanAI / Artibird system through local AI-assisted inference,
visual understanding, sensor fusion, contextual interpretation, and
intelligent optimization where deployed.

OceanAI Edge is intended to enhance local runtime behavior by providing
AI-assisted interpretation. It should not replace deterministic runtime
behavior, safety rules, user permissions, validated control logic, or
defined system boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**邊緣智慧架構定義 OceanAI Edge 如何在部署條件下，透過本地 AI
輔助推理、視覺理解、感測融合、上下文解讀與智慧優化參與 OceanAI /
Artibird 系統。

OceanAI Edge 用於透過 AI 輔助解讀增強本地 Runtime
行為。它不應取代確定性的 Runtime
行為、安全規則、用戶權限、已驗證控制邏輯或已定義系統邊界。

## **12.3 Edge Responsibilities**

## **12.3 Edge 責任**

## **English Table**

| **Edge Function** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Local AI inference | Run AI models locally where deployed |
| SLM integration | Provide small language model-assisted reasoning where supported |
| VLM integration | Provide vision-language understanding where supported |
| Vision analysis | Interpret visual context from Vision devices |
| Sensor fusion | Combine Sense, Vision, state, and execution data |
| AI-assisted optimization | Suggest or inform automation, energy, comfort, or security behavior |
| Data boundary | Define what data remains local and what may sync |
| Privacy behavior | Support privacy-aware processing where configured |
| Failure behavior | Fall back to non-edge runtime behavior when Edge is unavailable |

## **中文表**

| **Edge 功能** | **說明**                                 |
|---------------|------------------------------------------|
| 本地 AI 推理  | 在部署條件下本地運行 AI 模型             |
| SLM 整合      | 在支援條件下提供小型語言模型輔助推理     |
| VLM 整合      | 在支援條件下提供視覺語言理解             |
| 視覺分析      | 解讀來自 Vision 設備的視覺上下文         |
| 感測融合      | 融合 Sense、Vision、狀態與執行數據       |
| AI 輔助優化   | 建議或影響自動化、能源、舒適度或安全行為 |
| 數據邊界      | 定義哪些數據保留本地，哪些可同步         |
| 隱私行為      | 在配置條件下支援隱私導向處理             |
| 故障行為      | Edge 不可用時回退至非 Edge Runtime 行為  |

## **12.4 Local AI Inference**

## **12.4 本地 AI 推理**

**EN  
**Local AI inference refers to AI model execution within the local
environment where OceanAI Edge is deployed. It may process supported
visual data, sensor data, state data, device events, or selected runtime
information.

Local AI inference should be used to support interpretation,
classification, recommendation, optimization, and context understanding.
It should not be described as unrestricted autonomous control unless
such behavior is explicitly implemented, validated, and bounded by
safety and permission rules.

**ZH-TW  
**本地 AI 推理指在部署 OceanAI Edge 的本地環境中執行 AI
模型。它可處理受支援視覺數據、感測數據、狀態數據、設備事件或特定 Runtime
資訊。

本地 AI
推理應用於支援解讀、分類、建議、優化與上下文理解。除非相關行為已明確實作、驗證，並受到安全與權限規則約束，否則不應描述為不受限制的自主控制。

## **English Table**

| **Inference Input** | **Possible Edge Output** |
|----|----|
| Vision data | Visual event interpretation, room-state signal, security context |
| Sense data | Environmental context, threshold interpretation, comfort signal |
| Device state | State pattern, abnormal condition, usage context |
| Runtime events | Event classification, recommendation, assisted action |
| Energy data where supported | Usage pattern, optimization suggestion, anomaly signal |
| User-configured context | Scenario-specific recommendation or interpretation |

## **中文表**

| **推理輸入**       | **可能 Edge 輸出**                     |
|--------------------|----------------------------------------|
| Vision 數據        | 視覺事件解讀、房間狀態信號、安全上下文 |
| Sense 數據         | 環境上下文、閾值解讀、舒適度信號       |
| 設備狀態           | 狀態模式、異常條件、使用上下文         |
| Runtime 事件       | 事件分類、建議、輔助動作               |
| 支援條件下能源數據 | 使用模式、優化建議、異常信號           |
| 用戶配置上下文     | 特定場景建議或解讀                     |

## **12.5 SLM Integration**

## **12.5 SLM 整合**

**EN  
**SLM integration refers to the use of small language model-assisted
reasoning within OceanAI Edge where supported. It may help interpret
system context, user intent, device state, scene relationships,
automation logic, diagnostic information, or local knowledge.

SLM-assisted output must be treated as assisted interpretation unless
explicitly validated for direct control. It must follow runtime
priority, user permission, security rules, and defined control
boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**SLM 整合指在支援條件下，於 OceanAI Edge
中使用小型語言模型輔助推理。它可幫助解讀系統上下文、用戶意圖、設備狀態、場景關係、自動化邏輯、診斷資訊或本地知識。

除非已明確驗證可用於直接控制，SLM 輔助輸出必須被視為輔助解讀。它必須遵循
Runtime 優先級、用戶權限、安全規則與已定義控制邊界。

## **12.6 VLM Integration**

## **12.6 VLM 整合**

**EN  
**VLM integration refers to the use of vision-language model-assisted
understanding within OceanAI Edge where supported. It may help interpret
visual context, room conditions, object presence, activity signals,
security events, or visual-state relationships.

VLM-assisted behavior depends on camera availability, Vision device
capability, model capability, local processing resources, privacy
configuration, and validation results.

**ZH-TW  
**VLM 整合指在支援條件下，於 OceanAI Edge
中使用視覺語言模型輔助理解。它可幫助解讀視覺上下文、房間條件、物體存在、活動信號、安全事件或視覺狀態關係。

VLM 輔助行為取決於攝像設備可用性、Vision
設備能力、模型能力、本地處理資源、隱私配置與驗證結果。

## **English Table**

| **VLM Input**                   | **Possible Use**                         |
|---------------------------------|------------------------------------------|
| Visual scene                    | Room-state interpretation                |
| Motion event                    | Security awareness or automation context |
| Object presence                 | Context signal where supported           |
| Activity pattern                | Assisted event classification            |
| Visual anomaly                  | Alert support or diagnostic context      |
| Combined visual and sensor data | Multi-modal context interpretation       |

## **中文表**

| **VLM 輸入**       | **可能用途**           |
|--------------------|------------------------|
| 視覺場景           | 房間狀態解讀           |
| 移動事件           | 安全感知或自動化上下文 |
| 物體存在           | 支援條件下的上下文信號 |
| 活動模式           | 輔助事件分類           |
| 視覺異常           | 警報支援或診斷上下文   |
| 視覺與感測融合數據 | 多模態上下文解讀       |

## **12.7 Vision Analysis**

## **12.7 視覺分析**

**EN  
**Vision analysis defines how OceanAI Edge may process visual context
from Artibird Vision devices. Vision analysis may support visual event
interpretation, motion analysis, room-state understanding, security
awareness, local alert support, and assisted automation.

Vision analysis must follow privacy requirements, storage boundaries,
user permission, local processing rules, and validation conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**視覺分析定義 OceanAI Edge 如何處理來自 Artibird Vision
設備的視覺上下文。視覺分析可支援視覺事件解讀、移動分析、房間狀態理解、安全感知、本地警報支援與輔助自動化。

視覺分析必須遵循隱私要求、儲存邊界、用戶權限、本地處理規則與驗證條件。

## **12.8 Sensor Fusion**

## **12.8 感測融合**

**EN  
**Sensor fusion defines how OceanAI Edge may combine data from Artibird
Sense, Artibird Vision, device state, execution state, and runtime
context to produce a more complete interpretation of the environment.

Sensor fusion may support comfort optimization, energy-aware behavior,
room-state understanding, security context, or automation suggestions
where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**感測融合定義 OceanAI Edge 如何融合來自 Artibird Sense、Artibird
Vision、設備狀態、執行狀態與 Runtime
上下文的數據，以形成更完整的環境解讀。

感測融合可在支援條件下支援舒適度優化、能源感知行為、房間狀態理解、安全上下文或自動化建議。

## **English Table**

| **Data Source** | **Contribution** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Sense | Temperature, humidity, light, occupancy, environmental data |
| Artibird Vision | Visual event, motion, room-state, security context |
| Device State | Current device condition and behavior |
| Execution State | Act, Sync, relay, or appliance action result |
| Runtime Context | Scene, automation, schedule, user action, or system event |
| Cloud Context where supported | Historical or multi-site context where available |

## **中文表**

| **數據來源**         | **貢獻**                               |
|----------------------|----------------------------------------|
| Artibird Sense       | 溫度、濕度、光照、人在、環境數據       |
| Artibird Vision      | 視覺事件、移動、房間狀態、安全上下文   |
| 設備狀態             | 當前設備條件與行為                     |
| 執行狀態             | Act、Sync、繼電器或家電動作結果        |
| Runtime 上下文       | 場景、自動化、排程、用戶動作或系統事件 |
| 支援條件下雲端上下文 | 可用條件下的歷史或多站點上下文         |

## **12.9 AI-Assisted Optimization**

## **12.9 AI 輔助優化**

**EN  
**AI-assisted optimization refers to the use of Edge interpretation to
suggest or inform supported automation, energy behavior, comfort
control, security response, or operational adjustment.

AI-assisted optimization should not be presented as guaranteed
optimization unless validated under defined conditions. It should be
described as assisted behavior based on supported input data, model
capability, runtime configuration, and validation results.

**ZH-TW  
**AI 輔助優化指利用 Edge
解讀來建議或影響受支援自動化、能源行為、舒適度控制、安全回應或運行調整。

除非已在明確條件下完成驗證，否則不應將 AI
輔助優化描述為保證優化。它應被描述為基於受支援輸入數據、模型能力、Runtime
配置與驗證結果的輔助行為。

## **English Table**

| **Optimization Area** | **Example** |
|----|----|
| Energy | Suggest load reduction or energy-aware automation where supported |
| Comfort | Inform climate, lighting, or scene behavior |
| Security | Assist visual event interpretation or alert prioritization |
| Automation | Suggest rule adjustment or assisted trigger behavior |
| Maintenance | Identify abnormal device patterns or diagnostic signals |
| Space usage | Interpret room usage patterns where supported |

## **中文表**

| **優化領域** | **示例**                                 |
|--------------|------------------------------------------|
| 能源         | 在支援條件下建議負載降低或能源感知自動化 |
| 舒適度       | 影響空調、照明或場景行為                 |
| 安全         | 輔助視覺事件解讀或警報優先級             |
| 自動化       | 建議規則調整或輔助觸發行為               |
| 維護         | 識別異常設備模式或診斷信號               |
| 空間使用     | 在支援條件下解讀房間使用模式             |

## **12.10 Data Boundary**

## **12.10 數據邊界**

**EN  
**Data boundary defines what data may be processed locally by OceanAI
Edge, what data may remain local, what data may synchronize with OceanAI
Cloud, and what data is restricted by privacy policy or user settings.

Edge processing should be described according to data type, user
permission, deployment configuration, storage policy, cloud
synchronization rule, and validation condition.

**ZH-TW  
**數據邊界定義哪些數據可由 OceanAI Edge
本地處理、哪些數據可保留本地、哪些數據可與 OceanAI Cloud
同步，以及哪些數據受到隱私政策或用戶設定限制。

Edge
處理應依據數據類型、用戶權限、部署配置、儲存政策、雲端同步規則與驗證條件進行描述。

## **English Table**

| **Data Type** | **Edge Processing** | **Cloud Sync** |
|----|----|----|
| Sensor data | May be processed locally where supported | May sync where enabled |
| Device state | May be processed locally | May sync where supported |
| Vision event metadata | May be processed locally | May sync where enabled |
| Video / image data | Local processing preferred where configured | Sync only where supported and permitted |
| AI interpretation result | May inform runtime behavior | May sync where enabled |
| Diagnostic data | May support local analysis | May sync where supported |
| User configuration | May guide Edge behavior | May sync with cloud where enabled |

## **中文表**

| **數據類型**    | **Edge 處理**          | **雲端同步**             |
|-----------------|------------------------|--------------------------|
| 感測數據        | 支援條件下可本地處理   | 啟用條件下可同步         |
| 設備狀態        | 可本地處理             | 支援條件下可同步         |
| 視覺事件元數據  | 可本地處理             | 啟用條件下可同步         |
| 視頻 / 圖像數據 | 配置條件下優先本地處理 | 僅在支援且允許條件下同步 |
| AI 解讀結果     | 可影響 Runtime 行為    | 啟用條件下可同步         |
| 診斷數據        | 可支援本地分析         | 支援條件下可同步         |
| 用戶配置        | 可引導 Edge 行為       | 啟用條件下可與雲端同步   |

## **12.11 Privacy Behavior**

## **12.11 隱私行為**

**EN  
**Privacy behavior defines how OceanAI Edge handles privacy-sensitive
data, especially visual data, sensor data, user configuration, and
locally processed AI inputs.

Where configured, privacy-sensitive processing should remain local. Any
synchronization to OceanAI Cloud must follow user permission, data
policy, storage policy, account settings, and applicable privacy
requirements.

**ZH-TW  
**隱私行為定義 OceanAI Edge
如何處理隱私敏感數據，尤其是視覺數據、感測數據、用戶配置與本地處理 AI
輸入。

在配置條件下，隱私敏感處理應保留於本地。任何同步至 OceanAI Cloud
的行為都必須遵循用戶權限、數據政策、儲存政策、帳號設定與適用隱私要求。

## **12.12 Failure Behavior**

## **12.12 故障行為**

**EN  
**Failure behavior defines how the system responds when OceanAI Edge is
unavailable, degraded, overloaded, disconnected, or unable to process
AI-assisted functions.

When OceanAI Edge is unavailable, supported non-edge local runtime
behavior should continue where required local components are present.
AI-assisted interpretation, VLM analysis, SLM reasoning, sensor fusion,
and Edge-assisted optimization may be unavailable or degraded.

**ZH-TW  
**故障行為定義 OceanAI Edge 不可用、降級、過載、斷開或無法處理 AI
輔助功能時，系統如何回應。

當 OceanAI Edge 不可用時，在所需本地元件具備條件下，受支援非 Edge 本地
Runtime 行為應繼續運作。AI 輔助解讀、VLM 分析、SLM 推理、感測融合與 Edge
輔助優化可能不可用或降級。

## **English Table**

| **Edge Condition** | **Expected Behavior** |
|----|----|
| Edge available | AI-assisted interpretation may support runtime behavior |
| Edge delayed | AI-assisted output may be delayed or ignored depending on runtime configuration |
| Edge unavailable | Non-edge local runtime behavior continues where supported |
| Edge overloaded | AI-assisted functions may degrade or stop |
| Edge disconnected | Hub / ArtiOS continue supported local runtime behavior |
| Model unavailable | Related AI-assisted function is unavailable |
| Privacy restriction enabled | Restricted data is not processed or not shared according to policy |

## **中文表**

| **Edge 狀態**  | **預期行為**                             |
|----------------|------------------------------------------|
| Edge 可用      | AI 輔助解讀可支援 Runtime 行為           |
| Edge 延遲      | AI 輔助輸出可依 Runtime 配置延遲或被忽略 |
| Edge 不可用    | 支援條件下非 Edge 本地 Runtime 行為繼續  |
| Edge 過載      | AI 輔助功能可能降級或停止                |
| Edge 斷開      | Hub / ArtiOS 繼續受支援本地 Runtime 行為 |
| 模型不可用     | 相關 AI 輔助功能不可用                   |
| 已啟用隱私限制 | 受限制數據依政策不被處理或不被共享       |

## **12.13 Edge Boundary**

## **12.13 Edge 邊界**

**EN  
**Edge Intelligence Architecture must be described according to deployed
hardware, supported model type, software version, device capability,
input data type, privacy configuration, local processing capacity,
runtime integration, and validation evidence.

Edge participation does not imply fully autonomous AI control,
guaranteed AI accuracy, unlimited model capability, universal visual
understanding, or support for all sensor and vision scenarios.

**ZH-TW  
**邊緣智慧架構必須依部署硬體、受支援模型類型、軟體版本、設備能力、輸入數據類型、隱私配置、本地處理能力、Runtime
整合與驗證證據進行描述。

Edge 參與不表示完全自主 AI 控制、不表示保證 AI
準確性、不表示無限制模型能力、不表示通用視覺理解，也不表示支援所有感測與視覺場景。

## **12.14 Validation Requirements**

## **12.14 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any Edge-related claim involving AI inference, SLM reasoning, VLM
understanding, vision analysis, sensor fusion, optimization, privacy
behavior, latency, reliability, or failure behavior must be validated
under defined conditions.

Validation should include hardware platform, model version, software
version, input data type, processing load, local network condition,
runtime integration path, expected output, failure behavior, and privacy
configuration where applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及 Edge 的宣稱，包括 AI 推理、SLM 推理、VLM
理解、視覺分析、感測融合、優化、隱私行為、延遲、可靠性或故障行為，都必須在明確條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含硬體平台、模型版本、軟體版本、輸入數據類型、處理負載、本地網路條件、Runtime
整合路徑、預期輸出、故障行為，以及適用時的隱私配置。

## **12.15 Chapter Conclusion**

## **12.15 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the Edge Intelligence Architecture of the OceanAI
/ Artibird system. It explains how OceanAI Edge provides local
AI-assisted inference, SLM / VLM integration, vision analysis, sensor
fusion, optimization, data boundary control, privacy behavior, and
failure behavior while remaining within defined runtime, safety,
privacy, and validation boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird 系統的邊緣智慧架構。它說明 OceanAI Edge
如何提供本地 AI 輔助推理、SLM / VLM
整合、視覺分析、感測融合、優化、數據邊界控制、隱私行為與故障行為，同時保持在已定義
Runtime、安全、隱私與驗證邊界內。

chap 13 安全與隱私

# **chap 13 安全與隱私**

# **13. Security and Privacy**

# **13. 安全與隱私**

## **13.1 Purpose**

## **13.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section defines security principles, authentication,
authorization, communication security, data protection, and privacy
boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義安全原則、身份認證、授權、通訊安全、數據保護與隱私邊界。

## **13.2 Security and Privacy Definition**

## **13.2 安全與隱私定義**

**EN  
**Security and Privacy define how the OceanAI / Artibird system protects
supported devices, user accounts, local runtime services, cloud
services, edge intelligence, data flow, remote access, and system
control behavior.

Security is responsible for device identity, user authentication, access
control, communication protection, firmware update protection, and
system operation integrity.

Privacy is responsible for defining how user data, device data, sensor
data, visual data, cloud data, edge-processed data, logs, and
account-related information are collected, stored, processed,
synchronized, retained, and accessed.

**ZH-TW  
**安全與隱私定義 OceanAI / Artibird
系統如何保護受支援設備、用戶帳號、本地 Runtime
服務、雲端服務、邊緣智慧、數據流、遠端存取與系統控制行為。

安全負責設備身份、用戶身份認證、存取控制、通訊保護、韌體更新保護與系統運作完整性。

隱私負責定義用戶數據、設備數據、感測數據、視覺數據、雲端數據、Edge
處理數據、日誌與帳號相關資訊如何被收集、儲存、處理、同步、保留與存取。

## **13.3 Required Topics**

## **13.3 必須包含主題**

## **English Table**

| **Topic** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Device identity | Unique device identity and authentication |
| Account binding | Secure association between device and user / site |
| Local access control | Local permission and role rules |
| Remote access control | Cloud permission and account-based access |
| Secure MQTT | Authentication and encrypted communication where implemented |
| Firmware update security | Signed updates, version control, rollback handling where supported |
| Data retention | Define what data is stored and for how long |
| Vision data privacy | Define recording, access, storage, and processing behavior |
| Cloud data policies | Define cloud storage, use, and access rules |
| Edge processing boundary | Define local AI processing and data sharing boundaries |
| Role-based access control | Owner, admin, user, installer, guest roles |
| Audit logs | Security-sensitive event logging where supported |

## **中文表**

| **主題**        | **說明**                                   |
|-----------------|--------------------------------------------|
| 設備身份        | 唯一設備身份與身份認證                     |
| 帳號綁定        | 設備與用戶 / 站點之間的安全關聯            |
| 本地存取控制    | 本地權限與角色規則                         |
| 遠端存取控制    | 雲端權限與基於帳號的存取                   |
| 安全 MQTT       | 在已實作條件下的身份認證與加密通訊         |
| 韌體更新安全    | 在支援條件下的簽名更新、版本控制與回滾處理 |
| 數據保留        | 定義儲存哪些數據以及保留多久               |
| Vision 數據隱私 | 定義錄影、存取、儲存與處理行為             |
| 雲端數據政策    | 定義雲端儲存、使用與存取規則               |
| Edge 處理邊界   | 定義本地 AI 處理與數據共享邊界             |
| 角色權限控制    | Owner、Admin、User、Installer、Guest 角色  |
| 審計日誌        | 在支援條件下記錄安全敏感事件               |

## **13.4 Device Identity**

## **13.4 設備身份**

**EN  
**Device identity defines how each supported device is uniquely
identified and authenticated within the OceanAI / Artibird system.
Device identity may include Device ID, product type, model number,
hardware version, firmware version, security credential, account binding
status, and trusted registration status.

Device identity is required for device onboarding, access control,
