command routing, cloud synchronization, firmware update, security
logging, and system validation.

**ZH-TW  
**設備身份定義每個受支援設備如何在 OceanAI / Artibird
系統中被唯一識別與身份認證。設備身份可包括 Device
ID、產品類型、型號、硬體版本、韌體版本、安全憑證、帳號綁定狀態與可信註冊狀態。

設備身份對於設備入網、存取控制、指令路由、雲端同步、韌體更新、安全日誌與系統驗證都是必要的。

## **English Table**

| **Device Identity Item** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Device ID | Unique identifier for the device |
| Product Type | Hub, Gate, Switch, Panel, Act, Sense, Sync, Vision |
| Model Number | Product model identification |
| Hardware Version | Hardware revision |
| Firmware Version | Current firmware version |
| Security Credential | Credential used for authentication where implemented |
| Account Binding Status | Bound, unbound, pending, or reset state |
| Trusted Registration Status | Indicates whether the device is trusted by the system |

## **中文表**

| **設備身份項目** | **說明** |
|----|----|
| Device ID | 設備唯一識別碼 |
| Product Type | Hub、Gate、Switch、Panel、Act、Sense、Sync、Vision |
| Model Number | 產品型號識別 |
| Hardware Version | 硬體修訂版本 |
| Firmware Version | 當前韌體版本 |
| Security Credential | 在已實作條件下用於身份認證的憑證 |
| Account Binding Status | 已綁定、未綁定、待處理或重置狀態 |
| Trusted Registration Status | 表示設備是否被系統信任 |

## **13.5 Account Binding**

## **13.5 帳號綁定**

**EN  
**Account binding defines the secure association between a supported
device and a user account, home, site, organization, room, or system
deployment.

Account binding must verify device identity, user permission, ownership
status, site assignment, and security status where supported. Binding
behavior should prevent unauthorized device takeover, invalid
re-binding, unsafe migration, and unsupported system participation.

**ZH-TW  
**帳號綁定定義受支援設備與用戶帳號、住宅、站點、組織、房間或系統部署之間的安全關聯。

帳號綁定必須在支援條件下驗證設備身份、用戶權限、所有權狀態、站點分配與安全狀態。綁定行為應防止未授權設備接管、無效重新綁定、不安全遷移與未支援系統參與。

## **13.6 Local Access Control**

## **13.6 本地存取控制**

**EN  
**Local access control defines how users, devices, App interfaces,
Panels, Switches, Hub services, Gate services, and local runtime
components are permitted to interact within the local environment.

Local access control may include user roles, local permissions, device
permissions, local network access, command authorization, scene
permissions, automation permissions, and local configuration permissions
where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**本地存取控制定義用戶、設備、App 介面、Panel、Switch、Hub 服務、Gate
服務與本地 Runtime 組件如何在本地環境內被允許互動。

本地存取控制可在支援條件下包括用戶角色、本地權限、設備權限、本地網路存取、指令授權、場景權限、自動化權限與本地配置權限。

## **English Table**

| **Local Access Item** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Local user permission | Determines what a user can control locally |
| Device permission | Determines whether a device can participate in local runtime |
| Command authorization | Determines whether a command is allowed |
| Scene permission | Determines whether a user or device can trigger a scene |
| Automation permission | Determines whether automation can be configured or executed |
| Local configuration permission | Determines whether local settings may be modified |
| Network access condition | Determines whether the local path is trusted or allowed |

## **中文表**

| **本地存取項目** | **說明**                       |
|------------------|--------------------------------|
| 本地用戶權限     | 決定用戶可在本地控制哪些內容   |
| 設備權限         | 決定設備是否可參與本地 Runtime |
| 指令授權         | 決定指令是否被允許             |
| 場景權限         | 決定用戶或設備是否可觸發場景   |
| 自動化權限       | 決定自動化是否可被配置或執行   |
| 本地配置權限     | 決定本地設定是否可被修改       |
| 網路存取條件     | 決定本地路徑是否可信或被允許   |

## **13.7 Remote Access Control**

## **13.7 遠端存取控制**

**EN  
**Remote access control defines how users access supported devices,
rooms, scenes, automations, sites, and cloud services outside the local
environment.

Remote access control must follow account authentication, account
binding, role-based permission, cloud service availability, device
availability, secure communication, and validation requirements.

**ZH-TW  
**遠端存取控制定義用戶如何在本地環境之外存取受支援設備、房間、場景、自動化、站點與雲端服務。

遠端存取控制必須遵循帳號身份認證、帳號綁定、角色權限、雲端服務可用性、設備可用性、安全通訊與驗證要求。

## **English Table**

| **Remote Access Item** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Account authentication | Verifies user identity |
| Role permission | Defines what the user can access |
| Device availability | Determines whether the target device can be reached |
| Cloud availability | Determines whether remote service is available |
| Secure communication | Protects remote access path where implemented |
| Access logging | Records access events where supported |
| Remote restriction | Limits remote access according to policy or configuration |

## **中文表**

| **遠端存取項目** | **說明**                       |
|------------------|--------------------------------|
| 帳號身份認證     | 驗證用戶身份                   |
| 角色權限         | 定義用戶可存取內容             |
| 設備可用性       | 決定目標設備是否可達           |
| 雲端可用性       | 決定遠端服務是否可用           |
| 安全通訊         | 在已實作條件下保護遠端存取路徑 |
| 存取日誌         | 在支援條件下記錄存取事件       |
| 遠端限制         | 依政策或配置限制遠端存取       |

## **13.8 Secure MQTT**

## **13.8 安全 MQTT**

**EN  
**Secure MQTT defines how local MQTT communication is authenticated and
protected where implemented. This may include broker authentication,
client authentication, encrypted communication, topic permission,
message validation, retained message policy, and failure handling.

Secure MQTT behavior must be defined in related technical documents or
implementation specifications.

**ZH-TW  
**安全 MQTT 定義在已實作條件下，本地 MQTT
通訊如何完成身份認證與保護。這可包括 Broker
認證、客戶端認證、加密通訊、Topic
權限、消息驗證、保留消息策略與故障處理。

安全 MQTT 行為必須在相關技術文件或實作規格中定義。

## **English Table**

| **Secure MQTT Item** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Broker authentication | Verifies connection to the correct broker |
| Client authentication | Verifies device or service identity |
| Encrypted communication | Protects MQTT messages where implemented |
| Topic permission | Controls which client may publish or subscribe |
| Message validation | Checks message format and expected behavior |
| Retained message policy | Defines which messages may be retained |
| Failure handling | Defines behavior when broker or client authentication fails |

## **中文表**

| **安全 MQTT 項目** | **說明**                             |
|--------------------|--------------------------------------|
| Broker 認證        | 驗證是否連接至正確 Broker            |
| 客戶端認證         | 驗證設備或服務身份                   |
| 加密通訊           | 在已實作條件下保護 MQTT 消息         |
| Topic 權限         | 控制哪些客戶端可發布或訂閱           |
| 消息驗證           | 檢查消息格式與預期行為               |
| 保留消息策略       | 定義哪些消息可被保留                 |
| 故障處理           | 定義 Broker 或客戶端認證失敗時的行為 |

## **13.9 Firmware Update Security**

## **13.9 韌體更新安全**

**EN  
**Firmware update security defines how firmware updates are protected
from unauthorized modification, invalid installation, incompatible
versions, interrupted updates, or rollback failure.

Where supported, firmware update security may include signed updates,
version control, compatibility check, update authorization, failure
recovery, rollback handling, update logging, and lifecycle records.

**ZH-TW  
**韌體更新安全定義如何防止韌體更新遭未授權修改、無效安裝、版本不相容、更新中斷或回滾失敗。

在支援條件下，韌體更新安全可包括簽名更新、版本控制、相容性檢查、更新授權、失敗恢復、回滾處理、更新日誌與生命週期記錄。

## **English Table**

| **Firmware Security Item** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Signed update | Verifies firmware authenticity where supported |
| Version control | Prevents invalid or incompatible versions |
| Compatibility check | Confirms device eligibility before update |
| Update authorization | Confirms that update is allowed |
| Failure recovery | Defines behavior after interrupted or failed update |
| Rollback handling | Restores prior version where supported |
| Update logging | Records update activity |
| Lifecycle record | Maintains firmware history |

## **中文表**

| **韌體安全項目** | **說明**                   |
|------------------|----------------------------|
| 簽名更新         | 在支援條件下驗證韌體真實性 |
| 版本控制         | 防止無效或不相容版本       |
| 相容性檢查       | 更新前確認設備資格         |
| 更新授權         | 確認更新是否被允許         |
| 失敗恢復         | 定義更新中斷或失敗後行為   |
| 回滾處理         | 在支援條件下恢復先前版本   |
| 更新日誌         | 記錄更新活動               |
| 生命週期記錄     | 維護韌體歷史               |

## **13.10 Data Retention**

## **13.10 數據保留**

**EN  
**Data retention defines what data is stored, where it is stored, how
long it is retained, who may access it, and how it may be deleted or
overwritten.

Data retention may apply to device states, configuration, logs, event
records, alert records, historical data, cloud data, Edge processing
results, Vision metadata, and account-related information.

**ZH-TW  
**數據保留定義哪些數據被儲存、儲存在何處、保留多久、誰可以存取，以及如何刪除或覆寫。

數據保留可適用於設備狀態、配置、日誌、事件記錄、警報記錄、歷史數據、雲端數據、Edge
處理結果、Vision 元數據與帳號相關資訊。

## **English Table**

| **Data Type**      | **Retention Consideration**                           |
|--------------------|-------------------------------------------------------|
| Device state       | Stored locally or synchronized where supported        |
| Configuration      | Stored for system operation                           |
| Runtime logs       | Stored for diagnostics and validation where supported |
| Security logs      | Stored for access and security review where supported |
| Alert records      | Stored where alerts are enabled                       |
| Historical data    | Stored where cloud analytics or reports are enabled   |
| Vision metadata    | Stored according to privacy and configuration         |
| Video / image data | Stored only where supported and permitted             |
| Edge output        | Stored or discarded according to configuration        |
| Account data       | Stored according to account and privacy policy        |

## **中文表**

| **數據類型**    | **保留考量**                   |
|-----------------|--------------------------------|
| 設備狀態        | 在支援條件下本地儲存或同步     |
| 配置            | 為系統運作而儲存               |
| Runtime 日誌    | 在支援條件下用於診斷與驗證     |
| 安全日誌        | 在支援條件下用於存取與安全審查 |
| 警報記錄        | 在啟用警報時儲存               |
| 歷史數據        | 在啟用雲端分析或報告時儲存     |
| Vision 元數據   | 依隱私與配置儲存               |
| 視頻 / 圖像數據 | 僅在支援且允許條件下儲存       |
| Edge 輸出       | 依配置儲存或丟棄               |
| 帳號數據        | 依帳號與隱私政策儲存           |

## **13.11 Vision Data Privacy**

## **13.11 Vision 數據隱私**

**EN  
**Vision data privacy defines how Artibird Vision data is recorded,
processed, accessed, stored, synchronized, retained, or deleted.

Vision data may include video, images, motion events, visual metadata,
local recording status, security alerts, room-state signals, and
AI-assisted interpretation results. Vision data behavior must follow
user permission, privacy settings, storage rules, cloud synchronization
rules, and validation requirements.

**ZH-TW  
**Vision 數據隱私定義 Artibird Vision
數據如何被錄製、處理、存取、儲存、同步、保留或刪除。

Vision
數據可包括視頻、圖像、移動事件、視覺元數據、本地錄影狀態、安全警報、房間狀態信號與
AI 輔助解讀結果。Vision
數據行為必須遵循用戶權限、隱私設定、儲存規則、雲端同步規則與驗證要求。

## **English Table**

| **Vision Data Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Recording behavior | When and how recording occurs where supported |
| Local storage | Whether data is stored locally and for how long |
| Cloud sync | Whether data or metadata syncs with cloud |
| Access permission | Who can view or manage Vision data |
| Processing path | Whether processing occurs locally, on Edge, or in Cloud |
| Retention rule | How long data is retained |
| Deletion rule | How data may be deleted |
| Alert behavior | How visual alerts are generated and delivered |

## **中文表**

| **Vision 數據項目** | **必須定義內容**              |
|---------------------|-------------------------------|
| 錄影行為            | 在支援條件下何時與如何錄影    |
| 本地儲存            | 數據是否本地儲存以及保留多久  |
| 雲端同步            | 數據或元數據是否與雲端同步    |
| 存取權限            | 誰可以查看或管理 Vision 數據  |
| 處理路徑            | 處理發生於本地、Edge 或 Cloud |
| 保留規則            | 數據保留多久                  |
| 刪除規則            | 數據如何被刪除                |
| 警報行為            | 視覺警報如何生成與傳送        |

## **13.12 Cloud Data Policies**

## **13.12 雲端數據政策**

**EN  
**Cloud data policies define how OceanAI Cloud stores, uses,
synchronizes, protects, retains, accesses, and deletes data.

Cloud data policies must cover account data, device data, configuration,
logs, alerts, historical records, lifecycle data, remote access data,
multi-site data, and any supported analytics data.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端數據政策定義 OceanAI Cloud
如何儲存、使用、同步、保護、保留、存取與刪除數據。

雲端數據政策必須涵蓋帳號數據、設備數據、配置、日誌、警報、歷史記錄、生命週期數據、遠端存取數據、多站點數據，以及任何受支援分析數據。

## **English Table**

| **Cloud Data Policy Item** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Storage location | Where cloud data is stored where applicable |
| Data use | How data is used for supported services |
| Access rule | Who may access cloud data |
| Retention rule | How long cloud data is retained |
| Deletion rule | How data may be deleted or removed |
| Synchronization rule | What data syncs between local and cloud |
| Sharing rule | Whether data may be shared and under what condition |
| Security rule | How cloud data is protected |

## **中文表**

| **雲端數據政策項目** | **說明**                     |
|----------------------|------------------------------|
| 儲存位置             | 適用時雲端數據儲存位置       |
| 數據使用             | 數據如何用於受支援服務       |
| 存取規則             | 誰可以存取雲端數據           |
| 保留規則             | 雲端數據保留多久             |
| 刪除規則             | 數據如何被刪除或移除         |
| 同步規則             | 哪些數據在本地與雲端之間同步 |
| 共享規則             | 數據是否可被共享以及條件     |
| 安全規則             | 雲端數據如何被保護           |

## **13.13 Edge Processing Boundary**

## **13.13 Edge 處理邊界**

**EN  
**Edge processing boundary defines what data may be processed by OceanAI
Edge, what data remains local, what data may synchronize with OceanAI
Cloud, and what data is restricted by privacy configuration.

Edge processing may include Vision data, Sense data, device state,
runtime context, AI-assisted interpretation, diagnostic data, and
optimization signals where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**Edge 處理邊界定義哪些數據可由 OceanAI Edge
處理、哪些數據保留本地、哪些數據可與 OceanAI Cloud
同步，以及哪些數據受到隱私配置限制。

Edge 處理可在支援條件下包括 Vision 數據、Sense 數據、設備狀態、Runtime
上下文、AI 輔助解讀、診斷數據與優化信號。

## **English Table**

| **Edge Data Type** | **Processing Boundary**                               |
|--------------------|-------------------------------------------------------|
| Sense data         | May be processed locally where supported              |
| Vision data        | Must follow privacy and storage rules                 |
| Device state       | May support local analysis                            |
| Runtime context    | May support interpretation and recommendation         |
| AI output          | May inform runtime behavior within defined boundaries |
| Diagnostic data    | May support local troubleshooting                     |
| Cloud sync data    | May synchronize only where permitted and supported    |

## **中文表**

| **Edge 數據類型** | **處理邊界**                      |
|-------------------|-----------------------------------|
| Sense 數據        | 在支援條件下可本地處理            |
| Vision 數據       | 必須遵循隱私與儲存規則            |
| 設備狀態          | 可支援本地分析                    |
| Runtime 上下文    | 可支援解讀與建議                  |
| AI 輸出           | 可在已定義邊界內影響 Runtime 行為 |
| 診斷數據          | 可支援本地故障排查                |
| 雲端同步數據      | 僅在允許且支援條件下同步          |

## **13.14 Role-Based Access Control**

## **13.14 角色權限控制**

**EN  
**Role-based access control defines what different users may view,
configure, control, or manage within the system.

Supported roles may include owner, admin, user, installer, guest, or
organization-level roles where implemented. Each role should have
defined permissions for device control, configuration, remote access,
scene management, automation management, user management, data access,
and system maintenance.

**ZH-TW  
**角色權限控制定義不同用戶在系統中可查看、配置、控制或管理哪些內容。

受支援角色可在已實作條件下包括 Owner、Admin、User、Installer、Guest
或組織級角色。每個角色都應定義其在設備控制、配置、遠端存取、場景管理、自動化管理、用戶管理、數據存取與系統維護方面的權限。

## **English Table**

| **Role** | **Typical Permission Scope** |
|----|----|
| Owner | Full control, binding, configuration, user management |
| Admin | Broad management rights except selected ownership functions |
| User | Device control and selected scene / automation use |
| Installer | Setup and deployment-related access where permitted |
| Guest | Limited temporary access where supported |
| Organization Role | Site or multi-site access where supported |

## **中文表**

| **角色**          | **典型權限範圍**                     |
|-------------------|--------------------------------------|
| Owner             | 完整控制、綁定、配置、用戶管理       |
| Admin             | 廣泛管理權限，但不包含特定所有權功能 |
| User              | 設備控制與特定場景 / 自動化使用      |
| Installer         | 在允許條件下具備設定與部署相關存取   |
| Guest             | 支援條件下的有限臨時存取             |
| Organization Role | 支援條件下的站點或多站點存取         |

## **13.15 Audit Logs**

## **13.15 審計日誌**

**EN  
**Audit logs record security-sensitive, access-related,
configuration-related, lifecycle-related, and failure-related system
events where supported.

Audit logs may be used for diagnostics, security review, validation,
account management, troubleshooting, and compliance-related review where
applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**審計日誌在支援條件下記錄安全敏感、存取相關、配置相關、生命週期相關與故障相關系統事件。

審計日誌可在適用條件下用於診斷、安全審查、驗證、帳號管理、故障排查與合規相關審查。

## **English Table**

| **Audit Log Type** | **Example** |
|----|----|
| Access log | User login, remote access, local access |
| Binding log | Device bind, unbind, reset, migration |
| Permission log | Role change, permission update |
| Configuration log | Scene change, automation change, device setting change |
| Security log | Failed authentication, suspicious access, lockout |
| Lifecycle log | Firmware update, update failure, device replacement |
| Failure log | Cloud failure, Hub failure, Gate failure, device offline |

## **中文表**

| **審計日誌類型** | **示例**                                |
|------------------|-----------------------------------------|
| 存取日誌         | 用戶登入、遠端存取、本地存取            |
| 綁定日誌         | 設備綁定、解除綁定、重置、遷移          |
| 權限日誌         | 角色變更、權限更新                      |
| 配置日誌         | 場景變更、自動化變更、設備設定變更      |
| 安全日誌         | 身份認證失敗、可疑存取、鎖定            |
| 生命週期日誌     | 韌體更新、更新失敗、設備更換            |
| 故障日誌         | 雲端故障、Hub 故障、Gate 故障、設備離線 |

## **13.16 Security and Privacy Boundary**

## **13.16 安全與隱私邊界**

**EN  
**Security and privacy behavior must be described according to
implemented features, supported devices, software version, firmware
version, account configuration, local network condition, cloud
availability, Edge deployment status, privacy settings, and validation
evidence.

Security and privacy definitions do not imply absolute security,
unlimited privacy protection, unrestricted remote access, unsupported
encryption, unsupported local AI privacy behavior, or compliance with
every external regulatory requirement unless explicitly verified.

**ZH-TW  
**安全與隱私行為必須依已實作功能、受支援設備、軟體版本、韌體版本、帳號配置、本地網路條件、雲端可用性、Edge
部署狀態、隱私設定與驗證證據進行描述。

安全與隱私定義不表示絕對安全、不表示無限制隱私保護、不表示不受限制遠端存取、不表示支援未實作加密、不表示支援未定義本地
AI 隱私行為，也不表示符合所有外部法規要求，除非已明確驗證。

## **13.17 Validation Requirements**

## **13.17 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any security or privacy claim involving device identity, account
binding, access control, secure MQTT, firmware update security, data
retention, Vision privacy, cloud data policy, Edge processing boundary,
role-based access control, or audit logs must be validated under defined
conditions.

Validation should include product type, firmware version, software
version, account role, access path, network condition, cloud
availability, local runtime availability, Edge deployment status,
expected behavior, failure behavior, and privacy configuration where
applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及設備身份、帳號綁定、存取控制、安全
MQTT、韌體更新安全、數據保留、Vision 隱私、雲端數據政策、Edge
處理邊界、角色權限控制或審計日誌的安全或隱私宣稱，都必須在明確條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含產品類型、韌體版本、軟體版本、帳號角色、存取路徑、網路條件、雲端可用性、本地
Runtime 可用性、Edge
部署狀態、預期行為、故障行為，以及適用時的隱私配置。

## **13.18 Chapter Conclusion**

## **13.18 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the Security and Privacy structure of the OceanAI
/ Artibird system. It explains how device identity, account binding,
local and remote access control, secure MQTT, firmware update security,
data retention, Vision data privacy, cloud data policies, Edge
processing boundaries, role-based access control, and audit logs protect
the supported system within defined implementation and validation
boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的安全與隱私結構。它說明設備身份、帳號綁定、本地與遠端存取控制、安全
MQTT、韌體更新安全、數據保留、Vision 數據隱私、雲端數據政策、Edge
處理邊界、角色權限控制與審計日誌如何在已定義實作與驗證邊界內保護受支援系統。

chap 14 可靠性與故障行為

# **chap 14 可靠性與故障行為**

# **14. Reliability and Failure Behavior**

# **14. 可靠性與故障行為**

## **14.1 Purpose**

## **14.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section defines how the system behaves under failure, degraded,
offline, and recovery conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義系統在故障、降級、離線與恢復條件下如何運作。

## **14.2 Reliability and Failure Behavior Definition**

## **14.2 可靠性與故障行為定義**

**EN  
**Reliability and Failure Behavior defines how the OceanAI / Artibird
system maintains supported operation when cloud services, Internet
connection, local runtime services, gateway access, devices, App access,
Edge services, or network conditions become unavailable, degraded,
delayed, or interrupted.

The system should maintain supported local behavior where required local
components are present. When a component is unavailable, the system
should enter a defined degraded state, report status where supported,
and recover according to the expected behavior defined by product type,
deployment condition, and validation result.

**ZH-TW  
**可靠性與故障行為定義當雲端服務、Internet 連接、本地 Runtime
服務、網關接入、設備、App 存取、Edge
服務或網路條件不可用、降級、延遲或中斷時，OceanAI / Artibird
系統如何維持受支援運作。

當所需本地元件具備時，系統應維持受支援本地行為。當某一組件不可用時，系統應進入已定義降級狀態，在支援條件下回報狀態，並依產品類型、部署條件與驗證結果所定義的預期行為恢復。

## **14.3 Failure Behavior Table**

## **14.3 故障行為表**

## **English Table**

| **Failure Scenario** | **Expected Behavior** |
|----|----|
| Cloud unavailable | Local supported functions continue where local components are present |
| Internet unavailable | Local network functions continue where configured |
| Hub unavailable | Device-level behavior may degrade; local runtime functions may stop |
| Gate unavailable | Connected device access may degrade |
| Device offline | Device marked offline; commands queued or rejected depending on design |
| Edge unavailable | Edge-assisted functions stop; basic local runtime continues |
| App unavailable | Physical controls and local automation continue where configured |
| Power failure | Recovery depends on device and Hub startup behavior |
| Network congestion | System may degrade; capacity limits apply |

## **中文表**

| **故障場景**    | **預期行為**                                  |
|-----------------|-----------------------------------------------|
| 雲端不可用      | 所需本地元件具備時，受支援本地功能繼續運作    |
| Internet 不可用 | 已配置條件下，本地網路功能繼續運作            |
| Hub 不可用      | 設備級行為可能降級；本地 Runtime 功能可能停止 |
| Gate 不可用     | 已接入設備連接可能降級                        |
| 設備離線        | 設備標記為離線；指令依設計排隊或拒絕          |
| Edge 不可用     | Edge 輔助功能停止；基本本地 Runtime 繼續      |
| App 不可用      | 配置條件下，實體控制與本地自動化繼續          |
| 電力故障        | 恢復取決於設備與 Hub 啟動行為                 |
| 網路擁塞        | 系統可能降級；容量限制適用                    |

## **14.4 Cloud Unavailable**

## **14.4 雲端不可用**

**EN  
**Cloud unavailable means OceanAI Cloud cannot be reached, is degraded,
or cannot provide expected cloud services. In this condition, supported
local functions should continue where required local components are
present.

Remote access, cloud synchronization, cloud alerts, account updates,
historical cloud data, multi-site management, cloud analytics, and cloud
lifecycle services may be unavailable, delayed, or degraded.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端不可用指 OceanAI Cloud
無法連接、處於降級狀態，或無法提供預期雲端服務。在此條件下，當所需本地元件具備時，受支援本地功能應繼續運作。

遠端存取、雲端同步、雲端警報、帳號更新、雲端歷史數據、多站點管理、雲端分析與雲端生命週期服務可能不可用、延遲或降級。

## **English Table**

| **Cloud-Dependent Function** | **Behavior When Cloud Is Unavailable** |
|----|----|
| Remote control | Unavailable or degraded |
| Cloud synchronization | Delayed, queued, retried, or stopped depending on implementation |
| Cloud alerts | Delayed or unavailable |
| Account update | Unavailable or delayed |
| Multi-site management | Unavailable or degraded |
| Historical cloud data | Unavailable or limited |
| Local device control | Continues where local components are present |
| Local scene execution | Continues where locally configured and supported |
| Local automation | Continues where locally configured and supported |

## **中文表**

| **雲端依賴功能** | **雲端不可用時行為**             |
|------------------|----------------------------------|
| 遠端控制         | 不可用或降級                     |
| 雲端同步         | 依實作方式延遲、排隊、重試或停止 |
| 雲端警報         | 延遲或不可用                     |
| 帳號更新         | 不可用或延遲                     |
| 多站點管理       | 不可用或降級                     |
| 雲端歷史數據     | 不可用或受限                     |
| 本地設備控制     | 本地元件具備時繼續               |
| 本地場景執行     | 本地已配置且支援時繼續           |
| 本地自動化       | 本地已配置且支援時繼續           |

## **14.5 Internet Unavailable**

## **14.5 Internet 不可用**

**EN  
**Internet unavailable means the local environment has no external
network access. In this condition, local network functions may continue
where the local network, Hub, Gate, ArtiOS, and required devices are
available.

Remote control, cloud synchronization, cloud alerts, account updates,
cloud analytics, and cloud lifecycle services may stop or become delayed
until Internet access is restored.

**ZH-TW  
**Internet
不可用指本地環境無外部網路存取。在此條件下，若本地網路、Hub、Gate、ArtiOS
與所需設備可用，本地網路功能可繼續運作。

遠端控制、雲端同步、雲端警報、帳號更新、雲端分析與雲端生命週期服務可能停止或延遲，直到
Internet 存取恢復。

## **14.6 Hub Unavailable**

## **14.6 Hub 不可用**

**EN  
**Hub unavailable means Artibird Hub cannot provide local runtime
services. In this condition, local runtime functions such as scene
execution, automation processing, MQTT services, local state management,
web services, or command routing may stop or degrade.

Some device-level behavior may continue depending on the device type,
firmware behavior, local direct control capability, power condition, and
product design. Any claim regarding behavior without Hub must be
validated.

**ZH-TW  
**Hub 不可用指 Artibird Hub 無法提供本地 Runtime
服務。在此條件下，場景執行、自動化處理、MQTT 服務、本地狀態管理、Web
服務或指令路由等本地 Runtime 功能可能停止或降級。

依設備類型、韌體行為、本地直接控制能力、供電條件與產品設計不同，部分設備級行為可能繼續。任何關於無
Hub 條件下行為的宣稱都必須完成驗證。

## **English Table**

| **Hub-Dependent Function** | **Behavior When Hub Is Unavailable** |
|----|----|
| Local scene execution | May stop or degrade |
| Local automation | May stop or degrade |
| Local MQTT service | Unavailable if hosted on Hub |
| Local state management | May stop or degrade |
| App local access through Hub | Unavailable or degraded |
| Gate-to-runtime routing | May stop or degrade |
| Device direct behavior | Depends on product type and firmware design |
| Physical control | May continue where device supports it directly |

## **中文表**

| **Hub 依賴功能**       | **Hub 不可用時行為**     |
|------------------------|--------------------------|
| 本地場景執行           | 可能停止或降級           |
| 本地自動化             | 可能停止或降級           |
| 本地 MQTT 服務         | 若由 Hub 承載，則不可用  |
| 本地狀態管理           | 可能停止或降級           |
| 經 Hub 的 App 本地存取 | 不可用或降級             |
| Gate 至 Runtime 路由   | 可能停止或降級           |
| 設備直接行為           | 取決於產品類型與韌體設計 |
| 實體控制               | 設備直接支援時可繼續     |

## **14.7 Gate Unavailable**

## **14.7 Gate 不可用**

**EN  
**Gate unavailable means Artibird Gate cannot provide device access,
onboarding, gateway communication, or supported protocol access. In this
condition, devices that depend on Gate for communication may become
unreachable or degraded.

Devices that use other supported local communication paths may continue
depending on deployment configuration. Gate failure behavior must be
described according to device category, network path, protocol
dependency, and validation result.

**ZH-TW  
**Gate 不可用指 Artibird Gate
無法提供設備接入、設備入網、網關通訊或受支援協議接入。在此條件下，依賴
Gate 通訊的設備可能不可達或降級。

使用其他受支援本地通訊路徑的設備，可依部署配置繼續運作。Gate
故障行為必須依設備類別、網路路徑、協議依賴與驗證結果進行描述。

## **14.8 Device Offline**

## **14.8 設備離線**

**EN  
**Device offline means a supported device cannot be reached by the local
runtime system, cloud service, gateway, App, or supported communication
path. The system should mark the device as offline where supported.

Commands to an offline device may be rejected, queued, retried, or
delayed depending on implementation. Offline behavior depends on product
type, communication path, power condition, firmware behavior, and
runtime configuration.

**ZH-TW  
**設備離線指受支援設備無法被本地 Runtime 系統、雲端服務、網關、App
或受支援通訊路徑連接。在支援條件下，系統應將設備標記為離線。

發送至離線設備的指令可依實作方式被拒絕、排隊、重試或延遲。離線行為取決於產品類型、通訊路徑、供電條件、韌體行為與
Runtime 配置。

## **English Table**

| **Offline Device Behavior** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Mark offline | Device status is updated to offline where supported |
| Reject command | Command is rejected when device cannot be reached |
| Queue command | Command is stored for later execution where supported |
| Retry command | System retries communication according to implementation |
| Degraded state | Device remains visible but with limited capability |
| Alert generation | Offline event may generate alert where enabled |
| Log record | Offline condition may be logged where supported |

## **中文表**

| **設備離線行為** | **說明**                         |
|------------------|----------------------------------|
| 標記離線         | 在支援條件下將設備狀態更新為離線 |
| 拒絕指令         | 設備不可達時拒絕指令             |
| 指令排隊         | 在支援條件下儲存指令以待後續執行 |
| 重試指令         | 系統依實作方式重試通訊           |
| 降級狀態         | 設備仍可見，但能力受限           |
| 生成警報         | 啟用條件下離線事件可生成警報     |
| 日誌記錄         | 支援條件下可記錄離線狀態         |

## **14.9 Edge Unavailable**

## **14.9 Edge 不可用**

**EN  
**Edge unavailable means OceanAI Edge cannot provide AI-assisted
analysis, local inference, SLM / VLM-assisted interpretation, sensor
fusion, or optimization behavior.

When Edge is unavailable, supported non-edge local runtime behavior
should continue where Hub, ArtiOS, Gate, and required devices are
available. Edge-assisted functions may stop, degrade, or become
unavailable.

**ZH-TW  
**Edge 不可用指 OceanAI Edge 無法提供 AI 輔助分析、本地推理、SLM / VLM
輔助解讀、感測融合或優化行為。

當 Edge 不可用時，在 Hub、ArtiOS、Gate 與所需設備可用條件下，受支援非
Edge 本地 Runtime 行為應繼續。Edge 輔助功能可能停止、降級或不可用。

## **English Table**

| **Edge Function**          | **Behavior When Edge Is Unavailable**        |
|----------------------------|----------------------------------------------|
| AI-assisted interpretation | Unavailable or degraded                      |
| Vision analysis            | Unavailable or reduced to non-edge behavior  |
| Sensor fusion              | Unavailable or degraded                      |
| SLM-assisted reasoning     | Unavailable                                  |
| VLM-assisted understanding | Unavailable                                  |
| AI-assisted optimization   | Unavailable or disabled                      |
| Local scene execution      | Continues where non-edge runtime supports it |
| Local automation           | Continues where non-edge runtime supports it |

## **中文表**

| **Edge 功能** | **Edge 不可用時行為**      |
|---------------|----------------------------|
| AI 輔助解讀   | 不可用或降級               |
| 視覺分析      | 不可用或降級為非 Edge 行為 |
| 感測融合      | 不可用或降級               |
| SLM 輔助推理  | 不可用                     |
| VLM 輔助理解  | 不可用                     |
| AI 輔助優化   | 不可用或停用               |
| 本地場景執行  | 非 Edge Runtime 支援時繼續 |
| 本地自動化    | 非 Edge Runtime 支援時繼續 |

## **14.10 App Unavailable**

## **14.10 App 不可用**

**EN  
**App unavailable means Artibird App cannot access the system locally or
remotely. In this condition, supported physical controls, local scenes,
local automations, device-level behavior, and runtime services may
continue where required components are present.

App unavailable may prevent user configuration, remote control, device
management, scene editing, automation editing, status viewing, or
account management until App access is restored.

**ZH-TW  
**App 不可用指 Artibird App
無法在本地或遠端存取系統。在此條件下，當所需元件具備時，受支援實體控制、本地場景、本地自動化、設備級行為與
Runtime 服務可繼續運作。

App
不可用可能導致用戶無法進行配置、遠端控制、設備管理、場景編輯、自動化編輯、狀態查看或帳號管理，直到
App 存取恢復。

## **14.11 Power Failure**

## **14.11 電力故障**

**EN  
**Power failure defines how the system behaves when power is interrupted
for Hub, Gate, devices, local network equipment, Edge, or related
infrastructure.

Recovery depends on device power design, Hub startup behavior, Gate
startup behavior, network restoration, firmware state recovery, retained
configuration, and local runtime recovery. Battery-powered devices may
behave differently from mains-powered devices.

**ZH-TW  
**電力故障定義 Hub、Gate、設備、本地網路設備、Edge
或相關基礎設施供電中斷時，系統如何運作。

恢復取決於設備供電設計、Hub 啟動行為、Gate
啟動行為、網路恢復、韌體狀態恢復、保留配置與本地 Runtime
恢復。電池供電設備與市電供電設備可能具有不同表現。

## **English Table**

| **Power Failure Area** | **Expected Consideration** |
|----|----|
| Hub power failure | Local runtime may stop until Hub restarts |
| Gate power failure | Device access through Gate may stop until Gate restarts |
| Device power failure | Device becomes unavailable until power is restored |
| Network equipment power failure | Local and cloud communication may stop |
| Edge power failure | Edge-assisted functions become unavailable |
| Battery-powered device | May continue depending on battery condition |
| Mains-powered device | Depends on power restoration and firmware recovery |
| Configuration recovery | Depends on retained configuration and startup behavior |

## **中文表**

| **電力故障區域** | **預期考量**                                   |
|------------------|------------------------------------------------|
| Hub 斷電         | 本地 Runtime 可能停止，直到 Hub 重新啟動       |
| Gate 斷電        | 經 Gate 的設備接入可能停止，直到 Gate 重新啟動 |
| 設備斷電         | 設備不可用，直到電力恢復                       |
| 網路設備斷電     | 本地與雲端通訊可能停止                         |
| Edge 斷電        | Edge 輔助功能不可用                            |
| 電池供電設備     | 依電池狀態可繼續                               |
| 市電供電設備     | 取決於電力恢復與韌體恢復行為                   |
| 配置恢復         | 取決於保留配置與啟動行為                       |

## **14.12 Network Congestion**

## **14.12 網路擁塞**

**EN  
**Network congestion means local or cloud communication quality is
reduced by high traffic, interference, poor signal quality, message
overload, device count, gateway load, Hub load, or external network
conditions.

In network congestion conditions, system behavior may become delayed,
degraded, or temporarily unavailable. Capacity limits, message priority,
retry behavior, timeout behavior, and degradation rules should apply
where implemented.

**ZH-TW  
**網路擁塞指本地或雲端通訊品質因高流量、干擾、信號品質差、消息過載、設備數量、網關負載、Hub
負載或外部網路條件而降低。

在網路擁塞條件下，系統行為可能延遲、降級或暫時不可用。在已實作條件下，應適用容量限制、消息優先級、重試行為、超時行為與降級規則。

## **14.13 Degraded Operation**

## **14.13 降級運作**

**EN  
**Degraded operation means the system remains partially functional while
one or more components, services, or communication paths are unavailable
or limited.

A degraded state should be visible where supported. The system should
identify which capabilities remain available, which capabilities are
unavailable, and which capabilities may recover when the affected
component or service becomes available again.

**ZH-TW  
**降級運作指在一個或多個組件、服務或通訊路徑不可用或受限時，系統仍保持部分功能可用。

在支援條件下，降級狀態應可見。系統應識別哪些能力仍可用、哪些能力不可用，以及受影響組件或服務恢復後哪些能力可恢復。

## **English Table**

| **Degraded Condition** | **Available Behavior** | **Unavailable / Degraded Behavior** |
|----|----|----|
| Cloud unavailable | Local control, local scenes, local automation where supported | Remote access, cloud sync, cloud alerts |
| Edge unavailable | Non-edge runtime behavior | AI-assisted interpretation and optimization |
| Gate unavailable | Devices not dependent on Gate may continue | Gate-dependent device access |
| Hub unavailable | Device-level behavior where supported | Local runtime, scenes, automation |
| App unavailable | Physical controls and local automation where supported | User configuration and App control |
| Internet unavailable | Local network behavior where supported | Remote services and cloud sync |

## **中文表**

| **降級條件** | **可用行為** | **不可用 / 降級行為** |
|----|----|----|
| 雲端不可用 | 支援條件下本地控制、本地場景、本地自動化 | 遠端存取、雲端同步、雲端警報 |
| Edge 不可用 | 非 Edge Runtime 行為 | AI 輔助解讀與優化 |
| Gate 不可用 | 不依賴 Gate 的設備可繼續 | 依賴 Gate 的設備接入 |
| Hub 不可用 | 支援條件下設備級行為 | 本地 Runtime、場景、自動化 |
| App 不可用 | 支援條件下實體控制與本地自動化 | 用戶配置與 App 控制 |
| Internet 不可用 | 支援條件下本地網路行為 | 遠端服務與雲端同步 |

## **14.14 Recovery Behavior**

## **14.14 恢復行為**

**EN  
**Recovery behavior defines how the system returns from failure or
degraded state to normal operation. Recovery may include reconnecting
devices, restarting services, restoring state, synchronizing delayed
data, retrying commands, updating health status, clearing alerts, or
resuming cloud and edge participation.

Recovery behavior depends on the affected component, failure duration,
retained configuration, last known state, network condition, and
implementation design.

**ZH-TW  
**恢復行為定義系統如何從故障或降級狀態回到正常運作。恢復可包括重新連接設備、重啟服務、恢復狀態、同步延遲數據、重試指令、更新健康狀態、清除警報，或恢復雲端與
Edge 參與。

恢復行為取決於受影響組件、故障持續時間、保留配置、最後已知狀態、網路條件與實作設計。

## **English Table**

| **Recovery Item** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Device reconnection | Device reconnects after network or power recovery |
| Hub service restart | Local runtime services restart after Hub recovery |
| Gate reconnection | Gate restores device access path |
| Cloud resynchronization | Delayed data sync resumes when cloud is available |
| Edge reconnection | Edge-assisted functions resume when Edge is available |
| State restoration | Last known or retained state is restored where supported |
| Command retry | Pending commands may retry where supported |
| Alert clearing | Alerts may clear after recovery condition is verified |

## **中文表**

| **恢復項目**  | **說明**                         |
|---------------|----------------------------------|
| 設備重新連接  | 網路或電力恢復後設備重新連接     |
| Hub 服務重啟  | Hub 恢復後本地 Runtime 服務重啟  |
| Gate 重新連接 | Gate 恢復設備接入路徑            |
| 雲端重新同步  | 雲端可用後延遲數據同步恢復       |
| Edge 重新連接 | Edge 可用後 Edge 輔助功能恢復    |
| 狀態恢復      | 支援條件下恢復最後已知或保留狀態 |
| 指令重試      | 支援條件下待處理指令可重試       |
| 警報清除      | 恢復條件確認後警報可清除         |

## **14.15 Reliability Boundary**

## **14.15 可靠性邊界**

**EN  
**Reliability and failure behavior must be described according to
supported components, product type, hardware version, firmware version,
software version, local network condition, cloud availability, edge
deployment status, power condition, device count, deployment model, and
validation evidence.

Reliability definitions do not imply uninterrupted operation, guaranteed
cloud availability, universal offline operation, unlimited capacity, or
failure-free behavior under all conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**可靠性與故障行為必須依據受支援組件、產品類型、硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、本地網路條件、雲端可用性、Edge
部署狀態、供電條件、設備數量、部署模型與驗證證據進行描述。

可靠性定義不表示不間斷運作、不表示保證雲端可用、不表示通用離線運作、不表示無限制容量，也不表示所有條件下無故障行為。

## **14.16 Validation Requirements**

## **14.16 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any reliability claim involving cloud failure, Internet failure, Hub
failure, Gate failure, device offline behavior, Edge failure, App
unavailability, power failure, network congestion, degraded operation,
or recovery behavior must be validated under defined conditions.

Validation should include product type, hardware version, firmware
version, software version, network topology, device count, power
condition, cloud condition, edge condition, failure duration, expected
behavior, recovery behavior, and observed result.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及雲端故障、Internet 故障、Hub 故障、Gate
故障、設備離線行為、Edge 故障、App
不可用、電力故障、網路擁塞、降級運作或恢復行為的可靠性宣稱，都必須在明確條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含產品類型、硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、網路拓撲、設備數量、供電條件、雲端條件、Edge
條件、故障持續時間、預期行為、恢復行為與觀察結果。

## **14.17 Chapter Conclusion**

## **14.17 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the reliability and failure behavior of the
OceanAI / Artibird system. It explains how the system behaves when
cloud, Internet, Hub, Gate, devices, Edge, App, power, or network
conditions become unavailable or degraded, and how supported local
functions, degraded operation, and recovery behavior should be handled
within validated boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的可靠性與故障行為。它說明當雲端、Internet、Hub、Gate、設備、Edge、App、電力或網路條件不可用或降級時，系統如何運作，以及受支援本地功能、降級運作與恢復行為應如何在已驗證邊界內處理。

chap 15 部署模型

# **chap 15 部署模型**

# **15. Deployment Models**

# **15. 部署模型**

## **15.1 Purpose**

## **15.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section defines how the system can be deployed across homes,
classrooms, offices, campuses, buildings, energy systems, vision-aware
security, agriculture, and infrastructure scenarios.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義系統如何部署於住宅、教室、辦公、校園、建築、能源系統、視覺感知安全、農業與基礎設施場景。

## **15.2 Deployment Model Definition**

## **15.2 部署模型定義**

**EN  
**Deployment Models define how the OceanAI / Artibird system is
organized and installed within supported physical environments. A
deployment model describes the required components, system role, local
runtime structure, cloud participation, edge participation, device
categories, network requirements, and validation boundaries for a
specific scenario.

A deployment model does not imply that every component is required in
every scenario. Each deployment should be defined according to the
actual environment, required functions, supported products, network
condition, local runtime requirement, cloud requirement, edge
requirement, and validation evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**部署模型定義 OceanAI / Artibird
系統如何在受支援實體環境中組織與安裝。部署模型描述特定場景所需組件、系統角色、本地
Runtime 結構、雲端參與、Edge 參與、設備類別、網路要求與驗證邊界。

部署模型不表示每個場景都必須使用所有組件。每個部署都應依實際環境、所需功能、受支援產品、網路條件、本地
Runtime 要求、雲端要求、Edge 要求與驗證證據進行定義。

## **15.3 Deployment Model Table**

## **15.3 部署模型表**

## **English Table**

| **Deployment Model** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Residential Local System | Home-based Hub + Gate + device deployment |
| Smart Classroom | Classroom control, energy, climate, and AV synchronization |
| Smart Office | Meeting room, workspace, shared area coordination |
| Smart Building | Multi-room / multi-zone deployment |
| Smart Campus | Multi-building / multi-site deployment |
| Energy Management | Act-E, Sense, Cloud, analytics |
| Vision-Aware Security | Vision, Edge, Cloud, local alerts |
| Agriculture / Infrastructure | Sense, Act, Gate, Cloud, outdoor constraints |

## **中文表**

| **部署模型**    | **說明**                          |
|-----------------|-----------------------------------|
| 住宅本地系統    | 基於家庭的 Hub + Gate + 設備部署  |
| 智慧教室        | 教室控制、能源、空調與影音同步    |
| 智慧辦公        | 會議室、工位區與共享區域協同      |
| 智慧建築        | 多房間 / 多區域部署               |
| 智慧校園        | 多建築 / 多站點部署               |
| 能源管理        | Act-E、Sense、Cloud、分析         |
| 視覺感知安全    | Vision、Edge、Cloud、本地警報     |
| 農業 / 基礎設施 | Sense、Act、Gate、Cloud、戶外限制 |

## **15.4 Residential Local System**

## **15.4 住宅本地系統**

**EN  
**Residential Local System refers to a home-based deployment using
Artibird Hub, Artibird Gate, and supported Artibird devices. It may
include Switch, Panel, Act, Sense, Sync, Vision, and Artibird App
depending on the required functions.

This deployment model focuses on local device control, room-level
interaction, scenes, automation, appliance synchronization,
environmental sensing, and optional cloud-enhanced remote control.

**ZH-TW  
**住宅本地系統指基於家庭環境，使用 Artibird Hub、Artibird Gate 與受支援
Artibird 設備的部署方式。依所需功能不同，可包含
Switch、Panel、Act、Sense、Sync、Vision 與 Artibird App。

此部署模型重點在於本地設備控制、房間級互動、場景、自動化、家電同步、環境感知，以及可選的雲端增強遠端控制。

## **English Table**

| **Residential Component** | **Role** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | Local runtime center |
| Artibird Gate | Device access gateway |
| Artibird Switch | Local interaction, scene trigger, relay control by variant |
| Artibird Panel | Room-level control interface |
| Artibird Act | Electrical execution, plug or relay control |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental context |
| Artibird Sync | IR / RF appliance synchronization |
| Artibird Vision | Visual event and security awareness where supported |
| Artibird App | Setup, local control, remote control where supported |
| OceanAI Cloud | Remote access, synchronization, lifecycle services where supported |

## **中文表**

| **住宅組件**    | **角色**                                 |
|-----------------|------------------------------------------|
| Artibird Hub    | 本地 Runtime 中心                        |
| Artibird Gate   | 設備接入網關                             |
| Artibird Switch | 本地互動、場景觸發，依版本支援繼電器控制 |
| Artibird Panel  | 房間級控制介面                           |
| Artibird Act    | 電力執行、插座或繼電器控制               |
| Artibird Sense  | 環境上下文                               |
| Artibird Sync   | IR / RF 家電同步                         |
| Artibird Vision | 支援條件下視覺事件與安全感知             |
| Artibird App    | 設定、本地控制、支援條件下遠端控制       |
| OceanAI Cloud   | 支援條件下遠端存取、同步、生命週期服務   |

## **15.5 Smart Classroom**

## **15.5 智慧教室**

**EN  
**Smart Classroom refers to a classroom deployment for coordinated
control of lighting, climate, power, audiovisual equipment, sensing,
panel interaction, automation, and selected visual awareness.

This deployment model may use Artibird Hub, Artibird Gate, Artibird
Panel, Artibird Switch, Artibird Sense, Artibird Act, Artibird Sync,
Artibird Vision, Artibird App, OceanAI Cloud, and OceanAI Edge where
supported.

**ZH-TW  
**智慧教室指面向教室環境，用於協同控制照明、空調、電力、影音設備、感知、面板互動、自動化與特定視覺感知的部署方式。

此部署模型可在支援條件下使用 Artibird Hub、Artibird Gate、Artibird
Panel、Artibird Switch、Artibird Sense、Artibird Act、Artibird
Sync、Artibird Vision、Artibird App、OceanAI Cloud 與 OceanAI Edge。

## **English Table**

| **Classroom Function** | **Possible Components**            |
|------------------------|------------------------------------|
| Lighting control       | Switch, Panel, Act                 |
| Climate coordination   | Sense, Sync, Act                   |
| Power control          | Act, Switch relay variant          |
| AV synchronization     | Sync, Panel, Hub                   |
| Teacher interface      | Panel, App                         |
| Environmental sensing  | Sense                              |
| Visual awareness       | Vision, Edge where supported       |
| Local automation       | Hub, ArtiOS                        |
| Remote management      | OceanAI Cloud where supported      |
| Energy reporting       | Act-E, Cloud, Edge where supported |

## **中文表**

| **教室功能** | **可能組件**                  |
|--------------|-------------------------------|
| 照明控制     | Switch、Panel、Act            |
| 空調協同     | Sense、Sync、Act              |
| 電力控制     | Act、Switch 繼電器版本        |
| 影音同步     | Sync、Panel、Hub              |
| 教師介面     | Panel、App                    |
| 環境感知     | Sense                         |
| 視覺感知     | 支援條件下 Vision、Edge       |
| 本地自動化   | Hub、ArtiOS                   |
| 遠端管理     | 支援條件下 OceanAI Cloud      |
| 能源報告     | 支援條件下 Act-E、Cloud、Edge |

## **15.6 Smart Office**

## **15.6 智慧辦公**

**EN  
**Smart Office refers to an office-based deployment for meeting rooms,
workspaces, shared areas, reception areas, and facility zones. It may
support room control, scene execution, environmental sensing, power
control, appliance synchronization, and remote monitoring where
supported.

This deployment model may use Artibird Hub, Artibird Panel, Artibird
Switch, Artibird Sense, Artibird Act, Artibird Sync, Artibird App, and
OceanAI Cloud depending on the required deployment scale.

**ZH-TW  
**智慧辦公指面向辦公室、會議室、工位區、共享區域、接待區與設施區域的部署方式。它可在支援條件下支援房間控制、場景執行、環境感知、電力控制、家電同步與遠端監測。

此部署模型可依所需部署規模使用 Artibird Hub、Artibird Panel、Artibird
Switch、Artibird Sense、Artibird Act、Artibird Sync、Artibird App 與
OceanAI Cloud。

## **English Table**

| **Office Area** | **Possible System Behavior** |
|----|----|
| Meeting room | Scene control, AV sync, climate control, lighting control |
| Workspace | Lighting, plug control, occupancy-based automation |
| Shared area | Environmental sensing, scene control, power management |
| Reception area | Panel interaction, lighting scene, visual awareness where supported |
| Facility zone | Energy control, equipment monitoring, alert behavior |
| Remote office management | Cloud-supported monitoring and configuration where supported |

## **中文表**

| **辦公區域** | **可能系統行為**                       |
|--------------|----------------------------------------|
| 會議室       | 場景控制、影音同步、空調控制、照明控制 |
| 工位區       | 照明、插座控制、基於人在的自動化       |
| 共享區域     | 環境感知、場景控制、電力管理           |
| 接待區       | 面板互動、照明場景、支援條件下視覺感知 |
| 設施區域     | 能源控制、設備監測、警報行為           |
| 遠端辦公管理 | 支援條件下雲端監測與配置               |

## **15.7 Smart Building**

## **15.7 智慧建築**

**EN  
**Smart Building refers to a multi-room or multi-zone deployment within
a building. It may include lighting control, power control,
environmental sensing, room-level interface, gateway access, local
runtime coordination, cloud-enhanced monitoring, and selected visual
awareness.

This deployment model requires clear zoning, component placement,
network planning, capacity planning, local runtime planning, and
validation of device count, message flow, and failure behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**智慧建築指建築內多房間或多區域部署方式。它可包含照明控制、電力控制、環境感知、房間級介面、網關接入、本地
Runtime 協同、雲端增強監測與特定視覺感知。

此部署模型需要明確分區、組件佈置、網路規劃、容量規劃、本地 Runtime
規劃，以及設備數量、消息流與故障行為驗證。

## **English Table**

| **Building Deployment Item** | **Required Consideration** |
|----|----|
| Zone definition | Rooms, floors, areas, functional zones |
| Hub placement | Local runtime coverage and reliability |
| Gate placement | Device access coverage and protocol support |
| Network topology | Ethernet, Wi-Fi, BLE Mesh, local network, cloud connection |
| Device density | Number of devices per room, zone, Gate, and Hub |
| Scene scope | Room-level, floor-level, or building-level scenes |
| Automation scope | Local rules, zone rules, building rules |
| Failure behavior | Cloud, Hub, Gate, device, and network failure behavior |
| Validation | Capacity, latency, reliability, and deployment testing |

## **中文表**

| **建築部署項目** | **必須考量**                                  |
|------------------|-----------------------------------------------|
| 分區定義         | 房間、樓層、區域、功能分區                    |
| Hub 佈置         | 本地 Runtime 覆蓋與可靠性                     |
| Gate 佈置        | 設備接入覆蓋與協議支援                        |
| 網路拓撲         | Ethernet、Wi-Fi、BLE Mesh、本地網路、雲端連接 |
| 設備密度         | 每房間、區域、Gate 與 Hub 的設備數量          |
| 場景範圍         | 房間級、樓層級或建築級場景                    |
| 自動化範圍       | 本地規則、區域規則、建築規則                  |
| 故障行為         | 雲端、Hub、Gate、設備與網路故障行為           |
| 驗證             | 容量、延遲、可靠性與部署測試                  |

## **15.8 Smart Campus**

## **15.8 智慧校園**

**EN  
**Smart Campus refers to a multi-building or multi-site deployment
across classrooms, offices, public areas, outdoor areas, energy systems,
and security-related spaces. It may require multiple Hubs, multiple
Gates, distributed devices, cloud-enhanced management, and optional Edge
intelligence.

This deployment model should define local control within each building
or area while allowing OceanAI Cloud to support multi-site visibility,
account management, reporting, alert delivery, and lifecycle services
where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**智慧校園指跨教室、辦公區、公共區域、戶外區域、能源系統與安全相關空間的多建築或多站點部署方式。它可能需要多個
Hub、多個 Gate、分布式設備、雲端增強管理與可選 Edge 智慧。

此部署模型應定義每棟建築或區域內的本地控制，同時允許 OceanAI Cloud
在支援條件下提供多站點可視化、帳號管理、報告、警報傳送與生命週期服務。

## **English Table**

| **Campus Area** | **Possible Components** |
|----|----|
| Classroom building | Hub, Gate, Panel, Switch, Sense, Act, Sync, Vision |
| Office building | Hub, Panel, Switch, Sense, Act, Cloud |
| Public area | Sense, Vision, Act, Gate, Cloud |
| Energy zone | Act-E, Sense, Hub, Cloud, Edge where supported |
| Outdoor area | Sense, Act, Gate, Cloud, outdoor-rated devices where supported |
| Security-related area | Vision, Edge, Hub, Cloud, local alerts |
| Central management | Cloud, App, multi-site dashboard where supported |

## **中文表**

| **校園區域** | **可能組件**                                       |
|--------------|----------------------------------------------------|
| 教學樓       | Hub、Gate、Panel、Switch、Sense、Act、Sync、Vision |
| 辦公樓       | Hub、Panel、Switch、Sense、Act、Cloud              |
| 公共區域     | Sense、Vision、Act、Gate、Cloud                    |
| 能源區域     | 支援條件下 Act-E、Sense、Hub、Cloud、Edge          |
| 戶外區域     | 支援條件下 Sense、Act、Gate、Cloud、戶外等級設備   |
| 安全相關區域 | Vision、Edge、Hub、Cloud、本地警報                 |
| 中央管理     | 支援條件下 Cloud、App、多站點儀表板                |

## **15.9 Energy Management**

## **15.9 能源管理**

**EN  
**Energy Management refers to deployments that use supported execution
nodes, sensing nodes, cloud services, and optional Edge intelligence to
monitor, control, report, or optimize energy-related behavior.

This deployment model may include Artibird Act-E, Artibird Sense,
Artibird Hub, OceanAI Cloud, OceanAI Edge, and Artibird App where
supported. Energy-related claims must be validated and should not be
described as guaranteed savings unless supported by defined evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**能源管理指使用受支援執行節點、感知節點、雲端服務與可選 Edge
智慧，對能源相關行為進行監測、控制、報告或優化的部署方式。

此部署模型可在支援條件下包含 Artibird Act-E、Artibird Sense、Artibird
Hub、OceanAI Cloud、OceanAI Edge 與 Artibird
App。能源相關宣稱必須完成驗證，且除非有明確證據支援，不應描述為保證節能。

## **English Table**

| **Energy Function**     | **Possible Components**   |
|-------------------------|---------------------------|
| Load control            | Act, Switch relay variant |
| Energy measurement      | Act-E where supported     |
| Environmental input     | Sense                     |
| Local automation        | Hub, ArtiOS               |
| Energy reporting        | Cloud where supported     |
| Optimization suggestion | Edge where supported      |
| Remote monitoring       | App, Cloud                |
| Alerts                  | Hub, Cloud, App           |

## **中文表**

| **能源功能** | **可能組件**           |
|--------------|------------------------|
| 負載控制     | Act、Switch 繼電器版本 |
| 電能計量     | 支援條件下 Act-E       |
| 環境輸入     | Sense                  |
| 本地自動化   | Hub、ArtiOS            |
| 能源報告     | 支援條件下 Cloud       |
| 優化建議     | 支援條件下 Edge        |
| 遠端監測     | App、Cloud             |
| 警報         | Hub、Cloud、App        |

## **15.10 Vision-Aware Security**

## **15.10 視覺感知安全**

**EN  
**Vision-Aware Security refers to deployments that use Artibird Vision,
OceanAI Edge, OceanAI Cloud, Artibird Hub, and supported alerts to
provide visual event awareness, local recording, AI-assisted
interpretation, and remote notification where supported.

Vision-aware security must be described within privacy, storage, access,
retention, and validation boundaries. It should not be described as
perfect detection, guaranteed security, or unrestricted surveillance.

**ZH-TW  
**視覺感知安全指使用 Artibird Vision、OceanAI Edge、OceanAI
Cloud、Artibird Hub
與受支援警報，在支援條件下提供視覺事件感知、本地錄影、AI
輔助解讀與遠端通知的部署方式。

視覺感知安全必須在隱私、儲存、存取、保留與驗證邊界內描述。不應描述為完美偵測、保證安全或不受限制監控。

## **English Table**

| **Vision Security Function** | **Required Consideration** |
|----|----|
| Visual event detection | Supported Vision capability and validation |
| Local recording | Storage, retention, and access policy |
| Edge interpretation | Edge availability, model capability, privacy configuration |
| Cloud notification | Cloud availability, account permission, alert settings |
| Remote viewing | User permission and supported remote access |
| Privacy control | User consent, data policy, local processing preference |
| Failure behavior | Vision, Edge, Cloud, network, and storage failure behavior |

## **中文表**

| **視覺安全功能** | **必須考量**                            |
|------------------|-----------------------------------------|
| 視覺事件偵測     | 受支援 Vision 能力與驗證                |
| 本地錄影         | 儲存、保留與存取政策                    |
| Edge 解讀        | Edge 可用性、模型能力、隱私配置         |
| 雲端通知         | 雲端可用性、帳號權限、警報設定          |
| 遠端查看         | 用戶權限與受支援遠端存取                |
| 隱私控制         | 用戶同意、數據政策、本地處理優先        |
| 故障行為         | Vision、Edge、Cloud、網路與儲存故障行為 |

## **15.11 Agriculture / Infrastructure**

## **15.11 農業 / 基礎設施**

**EN  
**Agriculture / Infrastructure refers to deployments in outdoor,
semi-outdoor, facility, irrigation, monitoring, or infrastructure
environments. It may include environmental sensing, controlled
execution, irrigation control, power control, alerts, remote monitoring,
and cloud-enhanced reporting.

This deployment model must account for outdoor constraints, power
availability, network range, environmental protection, device placement,
communication reliability, and validation under real deployment
conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**農業 /
基礎設施指部署於戶外、半戶外、設施、灌溉、監測或基礎設施環境中的系統。它可包含環境感知、受控執行、灌溉控制、電力控制、警報、遠端監測與雲端增強報告。

此部署模型必須考量戶外限制、供電可用性、網路範圍、環境防護、設備佈置、通訊可靠性，以及真實部署條件下的驗證。

## **English Table**

| **Agriculture / Infrastructure Function** | **Possible Components** |
|----|----|
| Environmental sensing | Sense |
| Irrigation control | Act |
| Power control | Act, Switch relay variant where supported |
| Gateway access | Gate |
| Local coordination | Hub, ArtiOS |
| Remote monitoring | Cloud, App |
| Edge-assisted interpretation | Edge where supported |
| Alerts | Sense, Hub, Cloud, App |
| Outdoor deployment | Outdoor-rated devices where supported |

## **中文表**

| **農業 / 基礎設施功能** | **可能組件**                      |
|-------------------------|-----------------------------------|
| 環境感知                | Sense                             |
| 灌溉控制                | Act                               |
| 電力控制                | 支援條件下 Act、Switch 繼電器版本 |
| 網關接入                | Gate                              |
| 本地協同                | Hub、ArtiOS                       |
| 遠端監測                | Cloud、App                        |
| Edge 輔助解讀           | 支援條件下 Edge                   |
| 警報                    | Sense、Hub、Cloud、App            |
| 戶外部署                | 支援條件下戶外等級設備            |

## **15.12 Deployment Planning Requirements**

## **15.12 部署規劃要求**

**EN  
**Each deployment should define required components, component
placement, network topology, local runtime requirements, cloud
requirements, edge requirements, device count, room or zone structure,
power requirements, safety requirements, security requirements, privacy
requirements, and validation requirements.

Deployment planning should be completed before system claims,
installation materials, commercial proposals, or final system
acceptance.

**ZH-TW  
**每個部署都應定義所需組件、組件佈置、網路拓撲、本地 Runtime
要求、雲端要求、Edge
要求、設備數量、房間或區域結構、供電要求、安全要求、隱私要求與驗證要求。

部署規劃應在系統宣稱、安裝材料、商業方案或最終系統驗收之前完成。

## **English Table**

| **Planning Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Required components | Hub, Gate, devices, Cloud, Edge, App where applicable |
| Component placement | Physical placement and coverage requirement |
| Network topology | Ethernet, Wi-Fi, BLE Mesh, local network, cloud path |
| Local runtime requirement | Required Hub and ArtiOS functions |
| Cloud requirement | Remote access, sync, alerts, analytics, multi-site support |
| Edge requirement | AI-assisted analysis, Vision, sensor fusion, optimization |
| Device count | Number of devices per room, zone, Gate, Hub, or site |
| Power requirement | Power source, outage behavior, backup condition |
| Security requirement | Access control, binding, secure communication |
| Privacy requirement | Vision, cloud, Edge, data retention, user permission |
| Validation requirement | Functional, capacity, reliability, security, privacy testing |

## **中文表**

| **規劃項目**      | **必須定義內容**                              |
|-------------------|-----------------------------------------------|
| 所需組件          | 適用時 Hub、Gate、設備、Cloud、Edge、App      |
| 組件佈置          | 實體位置與覆蓋要求                            |
| 網路拓撲          | Ethernet、Wi-Fi、BLE Mesh、本地網路、雲端路徑 |
| 本地 Runtime 要求 | 所需 Hub 與 ArtiOS 功能                       |
| 雲端要求          | 遠端存取、同步、警報、分析、多站點支援        |
| Edge 要求         | AI 輔助分析、Vision、感測融合、優化           |
| 設備數量          | 每房間、區域、Gate、Hub 或站點設備數          |
| 供電要求          | 電源來源、斷電行為、備援條件                  |
| 安全要求          | 存取控制、綁定、安全通訊                      |
| 隱私要求          | Vision、Cloud、Edge、數據保留、用戶權限       |
| 驗證要求          | 功能、容量、可靠性、安全、隱私測試            |

## **15.13 Deployment Boundary**

## **15.13 部署邊界**

**EN  
**Deployment models must be described according to actual site
conditions, supported products, validated network conditions, power
conditions, device placement, environmental conditions, cloud
availability, edge deployment status, and system capacity limits.

A deployment model does not imply universal compatibility, unlimited
device count, guaranteed network coverage, guaranteed energy savings,
perfect AI vision detection, or support for all building, campus,
agriculture, or infrastructure environments.

**ZH-TW  
**部署模型必須依實際場地條件、受支援產品、已驗證網路條件、供電條件、設備佈置、環境條件、雲端可用性、Edge
部署狀態與系統容量限制進行描述。

部署模型不表示通用相容、不表示無限制設備數量、不表示保證網路覆蓋、不表示保證節能、不表示完美
AI 視覺偵測，也不表示支援所有建築、校園、農業或基礎設施環境。

## **15.14 Validation Requirements**

## **15.14 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any deployment claim involving supported scenario, device count,
network coverage, local operation, cloud-enhanced management,
edge-assisted behavior, energy management, vision-aware security,
outdoor use, or multi-site management must be validated under defined
deployment conditions.

Validation should include site type, product type, hardware version,
firmware version, software version, device count, network topology,
power condition, cloud condition, Edge condition, environmental
condition, expected behavior, failure behavior, and observed result.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及受支援場景、設備數量、網路覆蓋、本地運作、雲端增強管理、Edge
輔助行為、能源管理、視覺感知安全、戶外使用或多站點管理的部署宣稱，都必須在明確部署條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含場地類型、產品類型、硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、設備數量、網路拓撲、供電條件、雲端條件、Edge
條件、環境條件、預期行為、故障行為與觀察結果。

## **15.15 Chapter Conclusion**

## **15.15 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the deployment models of the OceanAI / Artibird
system. It explains how the system may be deployed across residential,
classroom, office, building, campus, energy, vision-aware security,
agriculture, and infrastructure scenarios while maintaining supported
component requirements, deployment boundaries, and validation
requirements.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的部署模型。它說明系統如何部署於住宅、教室、辦公、建築、校園、能源、視覺感知安全、農業與基礎設施場景，同時保持受支援組件要求、部署邊界與驗證要求。

chap 16 系統容量與工程邊界

# **chap 16 系統容量與工程邊界**

# **16. System Capacity and Engineering Boundaries**

# **16. 系統容量與工程邊界**

## **16.1 Purpose**

## **16.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section defines measurable system limits and validation
requirements.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義可量測的系統限制與驗證要求。

## **16.2 System Capacity and Engineering Boundaries Definition**

## **16.2 系統容量與工程邊界定義**

**EN  
**System Capacity and Engineering Boundaries define the measurable
limits of the OceanAI / Artibird system under supported hardware,
firmware, software, network, cloud, edge, and deployment conditions.

Capacity boundaries may include concurrent device connections, devices
per Gate, devices per Hub, scenes, automations, rooms, users, sites,
MQTT throughput, event latency, storage limits, Vision stream limits,
and Edge processing limits.

Engineering boundaries prevent unsupported claims and ensure that system
behavior is described according to validated test evidence rather than
theoretical capability.

**ZH-TW  
**系統容量與工程邊界定義 OceanAI / Artibird
系統在受支援硬體、韌體、軟體、網路、雲端、Edge
與部署條件下的可量測限制。

容量邊界可包括併發設備連接數、每個 Gate 支援設備數、每個 Hub
支援設備數、場景數、自動化數、房間數、用戶數、站點數、MQTT
吞吐量、事件延遲、儲存限制、Vision 視頻流限制與 Edge 處理限制。

工程邊界用於防止未支援宣稱，並確保系統行為依據已驗證測試證據描述，而不是依據理論能力描述。

## **16.3 Required Capacity Items**

## **16.3 必須定義容量項目**

## **English Table**

| **Capacity Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Max concurrent device connections | Total concurrent active devices under validated conditions |
| Max devices per Gate | Supported device count per Gate under tested network conditions |
| Max devices per Hub | Supported device count per Hub under defined hardware and service load |
| Max scenes | Supported scene count |
| Max automations | Supported automation count |
| Max rooms / spaces | Supported spatial organization scale |
| Max users | Supported user count and role model |
| Max sites | Supported site count under cloud account structure |
| MQTT throughput | Message throughput and latency under defined conditions |
| Event latency | Time from event generation to action execution |
| Storage limits | Local and cloud storage boundaries |
| Vision stream limits | Supported video streams and recording limits |
| Edge processing limits | Supported AI processing load and model boundaries |

## **中文表**

| **容量項目**         | **必須定義內容**                              |
|----------------------|-----------------------------------------------|
| 最大併發設備連接數   | 在已驗證條件下的總併發活躍設備數              |
| 每個 Gate 最大設備數 | 在已測網路條件下，每個 Gate 支援的設備數      |
| 每個 Hub 最大設備數  | 在明確硬體與服務負載下，每個 Hub 支援的設備數 |
| 最大場景數           | 支援的場景數量                                |
| 最大自動化數         | 支援的自動化數量                              |
| 最大房間 / 空間數    | 支援的空間組織規模                            |
| 最大用戶數           | 支援的用戶數與角色模型                        |
| 最大站點數           | 雲端帳號結構下支援的站點數                    |
| MQTT 吞吐量          | 明確條件下的消息吞吐與延遲                    |
| 事件延遲             | 從事件產生到動作執行的時間                    |
| 儲存限制             | 本地與雲端儲存邊界                            |
| Vision 視頻流限制    | 支援的視頻流與錄影限制                        |
| Edge 處理限制        | 支援的 AI 處理負載與模型邊界                  |

## **16.4 Max Concurrent Device Connections**

## **16.4 最大併發設備連接數**

**EN  
**Max concurrent device connections define the total number of supported
active devices that may participate in the system at the same time under
validated conditions.

This capacity must be measured according to product type, network
topology, Gate configuration, Hub configuration, protocol type, message
rate, firmware version, software version, and deployment model.

Theoretical chip capability must not be used as the final system claim
unless the complete system has been tested under defined conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**最大併發設備連接數定義在已驗證條件下，可同時參與系統的受支援活躍設備總數。

此容量必須依產品類型、網路拓撲、Gate 配置、Hub
配置、協議類型、消息速率、韌體版本、軟體版本與部署模型進行量測。

除非完整系統已在明確條件下完成測試，否則不得將理論晶片能力作為最終系統宣稱。

## **English Table**

| **Validation Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Device count | Number of active devices under test |
| Product mix | Hub, Gate, Switch, Panel, Act, Sense, Sync, Vision mix |
| Network topology | Ethernet, Wi-Fi, BLE Mesh, local network, cloud path |
| Message rate | Event, command, telemetry, and synchronization rate |
| Runtime load | Scene, automation, state, and command processing load |
| Test duration | Duration of concurrent connection test |
| Failure condition | Behavior under disconnect, reconnect, congestion, or overload |
| Acceptance criteria | Required stability, latency, and error threshold |

## **中文表**

| **驗證項目** | **必須定義內容**                                        |
|--------------|---------------------------------------------------------|
| 設備數量     | 測試中的活躍設備數                                      |
| 產品組合     | Hub、Gate、Switch、Panel、Act、Sense、Sync、Vision 組合 |
| 網路拓撲     | Ethernet、Wi-Fi、BLE Mesh、本地網路、雲端路徑           |
| 消息速率     | 事件、指令、遙測與同步速率                              |
| Runtime 負載 | 場景、自動化、狀態與指令處理負載                        |
| 測試時長     | 併發連接測試持續時間                                    |
| 故障條件     | 斷線、重連、擁塞或過載時行為                            |
| 驗收標準     | 所需穩定性、延遲與錯誤閾值                              |

## **16.5 Max Devices per Gate**

## **16.5 每個 Gate 最大設備數**

**EN  
**Max devices per Gate defines the supported number of devices that may
connect through one Artibird Gate under tested network conditions.

This boundary depends on Gate hardware version, firmware version,
supported protocol, Wi-Fi condition, BLE Mesh condition, Wi-Fi Mesh
implementation where supported, device type, message frequency, and
deployment environment.

The capacity of Artibird Gate must be validated as a system-level
boundary, not only as a chipset-level capability.

**ZH-TW  
**每個 Gate 最大設備數定義在已測網路條件下，可透過一個 Artibird Gate
接入的受支援設備數量。

此邊界取決於 Gate 硬體版本、韌體版本、受支援協議、Wi-Fi 條件、BLE Mesh
條件、支援條件下 Wi-Fi Mesh 實作、設備類型、消息頻率與部署環境。

Artibird Gate 的容量必須作為系統級邊界進行驗證，而不僅是晶片級能力。

## **English Table**

| **Gate Capacity Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Gate model | Gate product model and hardware version |
| Firmware version | Firmware version used during validation |
| Protocol type | Wi-Fi, Ethernet, BLE Mesh, Wi-Fi Mesh where supported |
| Device type | Switch, Sense, Act, Panel, Vision, Sync, or mixed devices |
| Device count | Number of devices connected through one Gate |
| Event frequency | Average and peak event frequency |
| Gateway load | CPU, memory, message handling, connection handling where available |
| Failure behavior | Behavior when device count exceeds validated capacity |

## **中文表**

| **Gate 容量項目** | **必須定義內容**                                   |
|-------------------|----------------------------------------------------|
| Gate 型號         | Gate 產品型號與硬體版本                            |
| 韌體版本          | 驗證時使用的韌體版本                               |
| 協議類型          | Wi-Fi、Ethernet、BLE Mesh、支援條件下 Wi-Fi Mesh   |
| 設備類型          | Switch、Sense、Act、Panel、Vision、Sync 或混合設備 |
| 設備數量          | 經由一個 Gate 接入的設備數                         |
| 事件頻率          | 平均與峰值事件頻率                                 |
| 網關負載          | 可用條件下 CPU、記憶體、消息處理與連接處理         |
| 故障行為          | 設備數超過已驗證容量時的行為                       |

## **16.6 Max Devices per Hub**

## **16.6 每個 Hub 最大設備數**

**EN  
**Max devices per Hub defines the supported number of devices that may
be managed by one Artibird Hub under defined hardware and service load.

This capacity depends on Hub hardware platform, local runtime services,
MQTT broker load, state management load, automation count, scene count,
device count, message rate, local storage, network topology, and cloud
synchronization behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**每個 Hub 最大設備數定義在明確硬體與服務負載下，一個 Artibird Hub
可管理的受支援設備數量。

此容量取決於 Hub 硬體平台、本地 Runtime 服務、MQTT Broker
負載、狀態管理負載、自動化數量、場景數量、設備數量、消息速率、本地儲存、網路拓撲與雲端同步行為。

## **English Table**

| **Hub Capacity Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Hub hardware | Hardware platform and configuration |
| Local runtime load | ArtiOS services, automation, scenes, state management |
| MQTT load | Message rate, retained messages, topic count where applicable |
| Device count | Total devices managed by one Hub |
| Gate count | Number of connected or associated Gates |
| Cloud sync load | Synchronization frequency and payload size |
| Storage use | Local log, state, configuration, and history use |
| Recovery behavior | Behavior after restart, overload, or network failure |

## **中文表**

| **Hub 容量項目**  | **必須定義內容**                     |
|-------------------|--------------------------------------|
| Hub 硬體          | 硬體平台與配置                       |
| 本地 Runtime 負載 | ArtiOS 服務、自動化、場景、狀態管理  |
| MQTT 負載         | 適用時消息速率、保留消息、Topic 數量 |
| 設備數量          | 一個 Hub 管理的總設備數              |
| Gate 數量         | 已連接或關聯的 Gate 數量             |
| 雲端同步負載      | 同步頻率與負載大小                   |
| 儲存使用          | 本地日誌、狀態、配置與歷史使用       |
| 恢復行為          | 重啟、過載或網路故障後行為           |

## **16.7 Max Scenes and Automations**

## **16.7 最大場景數與自動化數**

**EN  
**Max scenes and automations define how many configured scene behaviors
and automation rules the system can support under defined runtime
conditions.

This boundary depends on Hub performance, ArtiOS runtime structure,
device count, rule complexity, event frequency, storage use, local
processing load, cloud synchronization behavior, and validation
evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**最大場景數與自動化數定義系統在明確 Runtime
條件下可支援多少已配置場景行為與自動化規則。

此邊界取決於 Hub 性能、ArtiOS Runtime
結構、設備數量、規則複雜度、事件頻率、儲存使用、本地處理負載、雲端同步行為與驗證證據。

## **English Table**

| **Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Max scenes | Number of supported configured scenes |
| Max automations | Number of supported configured automation rules |
| Rule complexity | Number of conditions, triggers, and actions per automation |
| Scene complexity | Number of devices and actions per scene |
| Trigger frequency | Average and peak automation trigger rate |
| Execution latency | Time from trigger to execution |
| Failure behavior | Behavior when rule count or scene count exceeds boundary |

## **中文表**

| **項目**     | **必須定義內容**               |
|--------------|--------------------------------|
| 最大場景數   | 支援的已配置場景數量           |
| 最大自動化數 | 支援的已配置自動化規則數量     |
| 規則複雜度   | 每條自動化的條件、觸發與動作數 |
| 場景複雜度   | 每個場景的設備數與動作數       |
| 觸發頻率     | 平均與峰值自動化觸發速率       |
| 執行延遲     | 從觸發到執行的時間             |
| 故障行為     | 規則數或場景數超出邊界時的行為 |

## **16.8 Max Rooms / Spaces, Users, and Sites**

## **16.8 最大房間 / 空間數、用戶數與站點數**

**EN  
**Max rooms / spaces, users, and sites define the supported organization
scale of the system.

Rooms and spaces define the local physical or logical structure. Users
define account and role capacity. Sites define the number of homes,
classrooms, buildings, campuses, or managed locations supported under
the cloud account structure where applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**最大房間 / 空間數、用戶數與站點數定義系統支援的組織規模。

房間與空間定義本地實體或邏輯結構。用戶定義帳號與角色容量。站點定義在適用雲端帳號結構下支援的住宅、教室、建築、校園或受管理位置數量。

## **English Table**

| **Organization Capacity** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Max rooms / spaces | Number of supported rooms, zones, or areas |
| Max users | Number of supported users per home, site, or organization |
| Max roles | Supported role types and role assignments |
| Max sites | Number of supported homes, classrooms, buildings, campuses, or locations |
| Permission load | Impact of user and role count on access control |
| Cloud account structure | Account, organization, site, and room hierarchy |
| Sync behavior | Synchronization behavior across users, spaces, and sites |

## **中文表**

| **組織容量**      | **必須定義內容**                       |
|-------------------|----------------------------------------|
| 最大房間 / 空間數 | 支援的房間、分區或區域數量             |
| 最大用戶數        | 每住宅、站點或組織支援的用戶數         |
| 最大角色數        | 受支援角色類型與角色分配               |
| 最大站點數        | 支援的住宅、教室、建築、校園或位置數量 |
| 權限負載          | 用戶與角色數量對存取控制的影響         |
| 雲端帳號結構      | 帳號、組織、站點與房間層級             |
| 同步行為          | 跨用戶、空間與站點的同步行為           |

## **16.9 MQTT Throughput**

## **16.9 MQTT 吞吐量**

**EN  
**MQTT throughput defines the supported message handling capacity of the
local MQTT communication structure where implemented.

Throughput should be measured by message rate, payload size, topic
count, client count, retained message behavior, QoS behavior, broker
load, runtime processing load, and event latency under defined
conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**MQTT 吞吐量定義在已實作條件下，本地 MQTT 通訊結構支援的消息處理能力。

吞吐量應依消息速率、負載大小、Topic 數量、客戶端數量、保留消息行為、QoS
行為、Broker 負載、Runtime 處理負載與明確條件下的事件延遲進行量測。

## **English Table**

| **MQTT Capacity Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Message rate | Messages per second under defined load |
| Payload size | Average and maximum payload size |
| Topic count | Number of active topics |
| Client count | Number of connected MQTT clients |
| QoS behavior | Supported QoS level and impact |
| Retained messages | Number and behavior of retained messages where supported |
| Broker load | CPU, memory, and message queue behavior where available |
| Failure behavior | Behavior during overload, disconnect, or broker failure |

## **中文表**

| **MQTT 容量項目** | **必須定義內容**                     |
|-------------------|--------------------------------------|
| 消息速率          | 明確負載下每秒消息數                 |
| 負載大小          | 平均與最大 Payload 大小              |
| Topic 數量        | 活躍 Topic 數量                      |
| 客戶端數量        | 已連接 MQTT 客戶端數                 |
| QoS 行為          | 支援的 QoS 等級與影響                |
| 保留消息          | 支援條件下保留消息數量與行為         |
| Broker 負載       | 可用條件下 CPU、記憶體與消息隊列行為 |
| 故障行為          | 過載、斷線或 Broker 故障時行為       |

## **16.10 Event Latency**

## **16.10 事件延遲**

**EN  
**Event latency defines the time from event generation to expected
system action. Events may originate from Switch, Panel, App, Sense,
Vision, Act, Sync, Gate, Cloud, or Edge where supported.

Latency must be measured according to source, target, network path,
runtime load, device count, protocol type, cloud condition, edge
condition, and expected behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**事件延遲定義從事件產生到預期系統動作之間的時間。事件可在支援條件下來自
Switch、Panel、App、Sense、Vision、Act、Sync、Gate、Cloud 或 Edge。

延遲必須依來源、目標、網路路徑、Runtime
負載、設備數量、協議類型、雲端條件、Edge 條件與預期行為進行量測。

## **English Table**

| **Event Type** | **Latency Measurement** |
|----|----|
| Switch event | Time from touch event to runtime action |
| Panel event | Time from panel action to device or scene response |
| App local command | Time from local App command to device response |
| App remote command | Time from remote command to device response where supported |
| Sensor event | Time from sensor reading to automation action |
| Vision event | Time from visual event to alert or runtime action |
| Cloud command | Time from cloud command to local execution |
| Edge interpretation | Time from input data to Edge-assisted output |

## **中文表**

| **事件類型** | **延遲量測**                          |
|--------------|---------------------------------------|
| Switch 事件  | 從觸控事件到 Runtime 動作的時間       |
| Panel 事件   | 從面板操作到設備或場景回應的時間      |
| App 本地指令 | 從 App 本地指令到設備回應的時間       |
| App 遠端指令 | 支援條件下從遠端指令到設備回應的時間  |
| 感測事件     | 從感測讀數到自動化動作的時間          |
| Vision 事件  | 從視覺事件到警報或 Runtime 動作的時間 |
| 雲端指令     | 從雲端指令到本地執行的時間            |
| Edge 解讀    | 從輸入數據到 Edge 輔助輸出的時間      |

## **16.11 Storage Limits**

## **16.11 儲存限制**

**EN  
**Storage limits define the local and cloud storage boundaries for
configuration, state, logs, historical records, alerts, Vision data,
diagnostic records, lifecycle data, and Edge output where supported.

Storage behavior should include capacity, retention period, overwrite
behavior, deletion behavior, synchronization behavior, and failure
behavior when storage is full or unavailable.

**ZH-TW  
**儲存限制定義配置、狀態、日誌、歷史記錄、警報、Vision
數據、診斷記錄、生命週期數據與支援條件下 Edge 輸出的本地與雲端儲存邊界。

儲存行為應包含容量、保留時間、覆寫行為、刪除行為、同步行為，以及儲存已滿或不可用時的故障行為。

## **English Table**

| **Storage Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Configuration storage | Space for device, room, scene, and automation configuration |
| State storage | Current and recent device or system state |
| Runtime logs | Local or cloud runtime records |
| Security logs | Access, binding, permission, and security-related records |
| Historical records | Long-term data where supported |
| Vision storage | Video, image, or metadata storage where supported |
| Lifecycle records | Firmware, software, device replacement, and update history |
| Storage full behavior | Overwrite, reject, delete, queue, or alert behavior |

## **中文表**

| **儲存項目** | **必須定義內容**                 |
|--------------|----------------------------------|
| 配置儲存     | 設備、房間、場景與自動化配置空間 |
| 狀態儲存     | 當前與近期設備或系統狀態         |
| Runtime 日誌 | 本地或雲端 Runtime 記錄          |
| 安全日誌     | 存取、綁定、權限與安全相關記錄   |
| 歷史記錄     | 支援條件下長期數據               |
| Vision 儲存  | 支援條件下視頻、圖像或元數據儲存 |
| 生命週期記錄 | 韌體、軟體、設備更換與更新歷史   |
| 儲存已滿行為 | 覆寫、拒絕、刪除、排隊或警報行為 |

## **16.12 Vision Stream Limits**

## **16.12 Vision 視頻流限制**

**EN  
**Vision stream limits define the supported number of visual streams,
recording channels, event streams, metadata streams, and remote viewing
sessions where Artibird Vision is deployed.

Vision limits depend on Vision device capability, local network
condition, Hub capability, Edge processing load, cloud synchronization
behavior, storage capacity, privacy configuration, and validation
evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**Vision 視頻流限制定義部署 Artibird Vision
時，支援的視覺流、錄影通道、事件流、元數據流與遠端查看 Session 數量。

Vision 限制取決於 Vision 設備能力、本地網路條件、Hub 能力、Edge
處理負載、雲端同步行為、儲存容量、隱私配置與驗證證據。

## **English Table**

| **Vision Capacity Item** | **Required Definition**                       |
|--------------------------|-----------------------------------------------|
| Max Vision devices       | Number of supported Vision devices            |
| Max live streams         | Number of simultaneous live viewing streams   |
| Max recording channels   | Number of recording channels where supported  |
| Event stream rate        | Number and frequency of visual events         |
| Metadata throughput      | Visual metadata rate where supported          |
| Storage capacity         | Local or cloud video / metadata storage       |
| Edge processing load     | Vision analysis load on OceanAI Edge          |
| Privacy restriction      | Impact of privacy settings on Vision behavior |

## **中文表**
