| **Vision 容量項目** | **必須定義內容**              |
|---------------------|-------------------------------|
| 最大 Vision 設備數  | 支援的 Vision 設備數量        |
| 最大即時視頻流      | 同時即時查看視頻流數量        |
| 最大錄影通道        | 支援條件下錄影通道數量        |
| 事件流速率          | 視覺事件數量與頻率            |
| 元數據吞吐量        | 支援條件下視覺元數據速率      |
| 儲存容量            | 本地或雲端視頻 / 元數據儲存   |
| Edge 處理負載       | OceanAI Edge 上的視覺分析負載 |
| 隱私限制            | 隱私設定對 Vision 行為的影響  |

## **16.13 Edge Processing Limits**

## **16.13 Edge 處理限制**

**EN  
**Edge processing limits define the supported AI processing load and
model boundaries of OceanAI Edge where deployed.

These limits depend on hardware platform, model type, model version,
input data type, sensor and Vision data rate, inference frequency, local
network condition, runtime integration, memory load, compute load,
latency requirement, and validation evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**Edge 處理限制定義部署 OceanAI Edge 時，受支援 AI 處理負載與模型邊界。

這些限制取決於硬體平台、模型類型、模型版本、輸入數據類型、感測與 Vision
數據速率、推理頻率、本地網路條件、Runtime
整合、記憶體負載、運算負載、延遲要求與驗證證據。

## **English Table**

| **Edge Capacity Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Model type | SLM, VLM, vision model, sensor fusion model where supported |
| Model version | Specific validated model version |
| Input rate | Sensor, Vision, state, or runtime input rate |
| Inference frequency | Number of inferences under defined load |
| Processing latency | Time from input to AI-assisted output |
| Compute load | CPU, GPU, NPU, memory, or platform load where available |
| Concurrent tasks | Number of simultaneous AI-assisted tasks |
| Failure behavior | Behavior during overload, model failure, or Edge unavailability |

## **中文表**

| **Edge 容量項目** | **必須定義內容**                            |
|-------------------|---------------------------------------------|
| 模型類型          | 支援條件下 SLM、VLM、視覺模型、感測融合模型 |
| 模型版本          | 具體已驗證模型版本                          |
| 輸入速率          | 感測、Vision、狀態或 Runtime 輸入速率       |
| 推理頻率          | 明確負載下的推理次數                        |
| 處理延遲          | 從輸入到 AI 輔助輸出的時間                  |
| 運算負載          | 可用條件下 CPU、GPU、NPU、記憶體或平台負載  |
| 併發任務          | 同時 AI 輔助任務數量                        |
| 故障行為          | 過載、模型故障或 Edge 不可用時行為          |

## **16.14 Engineering Boundary**

## **16.14 工程邊界**

**EN  
**Engineering boundaries define what the OceanAI / Artibird system
supports under validated conditions and what remains outside supported
behavior.

Engineering boundaries must be applied to product capabilities,
connectivity, capacity, latency, reliability, offline behavior, cloud
participation, Edge participation, AI-assisted behavior, security
behavior, privacy behavior, and deployment scenarios.

**ZH-TW  
**工程邊界定義 OceanAI / Artibird
系統在已驗證條件下支援哪些能力，以及哪些行為不屬於受支援範圍。

工程邊界必須適用於產品能力、連接、容量、延遲、可靠性、離線行為、雲端參與、Edge
參與、AI 輔助行為、安全行為、隱私行為與部署場景。

## **English Table**

| **Boundary Area** | **Boundary Principle** |
|----|----|
| Product capability | Defined by product engineering specifications |
| Connectivity | Defined by supported protocol and validated network condition |
| Capacity | Defined by test evidence under known load |
| Latency | Defined by measured source-to-action behavior |
| Reliability | Defined by failure and recovery testing |
| Offline behavior | Defined by required local components and validated scenarios |
| Cloud participation | Defined by implemented cloud services and network availability |
| Edge participation | Defined by deployed hardware, models, and validated input conditions |
| Security | Defined by implemented authentication, authorization, and protection behavior |
| Privacy | Defined by data policy, user permission, storage, and processing rules |
| Deployment | Defined by actual site conditions and supported components |

## **中文表**

| **邊界領域** | **邊界原則**                             |
|--------------|------------------------------------------|
| 產品能力     | 由產品工程規格書定義                     |
| 連接         | 由受支援協議與已驗證網路條件定義         |
| 容量         | 由已知負載下測試證據定義                 |
| 延遲         | 由來源至動作的量測行為定義               |
| 可靠性       | 由故障與恢復測試定義                     |
| 離線行為     | 由所需本地元件與已驗證場景定義           |
| 雲端參與     | 由已實作雲端服務與網路可用性定義         |
| Edge 參與    | 由部署硬體、模型與已驗證輸入條件定義     |
| 安全         | 由已實作身份認證、授權與保護行為定義     |
| 隱私         | 由數據政策、用戶權限、儲存與處理規則定義 |
| 部署         | 由實際場地條件與受支援組件定義           |

## **16.15 Mandatory Statement**

## **16.15 強制聲明**

**EN  
**All capacity and performance claims must be based on validated test
reports under defined hardware, firmware, network, and deployment
conditions.

Theoretical chipset specifications, prototype-only observations, limited
internal tests, or uncontrolled demonstrations must not be used as final
system claims unless validated as part of the complete OceanAI /
Artibird system.

**ZH-TW  
**所有容量與性能宣稱必須基於明確硬體、韌體、網路與部署條件下的已驗證測試報告。

理論晶片規格、僅原型觀察、有限內部測試或未受控演示，不得作為最終系統宣稱，除非已作為完整
OceanAI / Artibird 系統的一部分完成驗證。

## **16.16 Validation Requirements**

## **16.16 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any claim involving capacity, performance, latency, throughput,
connection count, device count, scene count, automation count, storage,
Vision streams, Edge processing, cloud synchronization, offline
behavior, or reliability must be validated under defined conditions.

Validation should include hardware version, firmware version, software
version, network topology, device count, product mix, message rate, test
duration, cloud condition, Edge condition, failure scenario, expected
behavior, observed result, and acceptance criteria.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及容量、性能、延遲、吞吐量、連接數、設備數、場景數、自動化數、儲存、Vision
視頻流、Edge
處理、雲端同步、離線行為或可靠性的宣稱，都必須在明確條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、網路拓撲、設備數量、產品組合、消息速率、測試時長、雲端條件、Edge
條件、故障場景、預期行為、觀察結果與驗收標準。

## **16.17 Chapter Conclusion**

## **16.17 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the system capacity and engineering boundaries of
the OceanAI / Artibird system. It explains how concurrent connections,
devices per Gate, devices per Hub, scenes, automations, rooms, users,
sites, MQTT throughput, event latency, storage, Vision streams, and Edge
processing must be described according to validated conditions and
engineering evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的系統容量與工程邊界。它說明併發連接、每個 Gate 設備數、每個 Hub
設備數、場景、自動化、房間、用戶、站點、MQTT
吞吐量、事件延遲、儲存、Vision 視頻流與 Edge
處理，必須如何依已驗證條件與工程證據進行描述。

chap 17 測試與驗證

# **chap 17 測試與驗證**

# **17. Testing and Validation**

# **17. 測試與驗證**

## **17.1 Purpose**

## **17.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section defines system-level testing requirements and validation
categories.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義系統級測試要求與驗證類別。

## **17.2 Testing and Validation Definition**

## **17.2 測試與驗證定義**

**EN  
**Testing and Validation define how the OceanAI / Artibird system is
verified under defined hardware, firmware, software, network, cloud,
edge, runtime, deployment, and environmental conditions.

Testing confirms whether supported functions operate as expected.
Validation confirms whether system claims, capacity limits, reliability
behavior, security behavior, privacy behavior, cloud participation, edge
participation, and deployment models are supported by evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**測試與驗證定義 OceanAI / Artibird
系統如何在明確硬體、韌體、軟體、網路、雲端、Edge、Runtime、部署與環境條件下完成確認。

測試用於確認受支援功能是否按預期運作。驗證用於確認系統宣稱、容量限制、可靠性行為、安全行為、隱私行為、雲端參與、Edge
參與與部署模型是否具備證據支持。

## **17.3 Testing Categories**

## **17.3 測試類別**

## **English Table**

| **Test Category** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| Functional Test | Verify core system functions |
| Runtime Test | Verify local runtime behavior |
| Connectivity Test | Verify network and gateway communication |
| Capacity Test | Verify device and event limits |
| Stress Test | Verify long-duration operation |
| Failover Test | Verify cloud, network, Hub, Gate, and Edge failure behavior |
| Security Test | Verify access control, authentication, and communication security |
| Privacy Test | Verify data behavior, especially Vision and Cloud |
| Compatibility Test | Verify device and version interoperability |
| Deployment Test | Verify scenario-specific deployments |

## **中文表**

| **測試類別** | **說明**                                   |
|--------------|--------------------------------------------|
| 功能測試     | 驗證核心系統功能                           |
| Runtime 測試 | 驗證本地 Runtime 行為                      |
| 連接測試     | 驗證網路與網關通訊                         |
| 容量測試     | 驗證設備與事件限制                         |
| 壓力測試     | 驗證長時間運作                             |
| 故障切換測試 | 驗證雲端、網路、Hub、Gate 與 Edge 故障行為 |
| 安全測試     | 驗證存取控制、身份認證與通訊安全           |
| 隱私測試     | 驗證數據行為，尤其是 Vision 與 Cloud       |
| 相容性測試   | 驗證設備與版本互操作性                     |
| 部署測試     | 驗證特定場景部署                           |

## **17.4 Functional Test**

## **17.4 功能測試**

**EN  
**Functional Test verifies whether the core system functions operate as
expected. It should cover device onboarding, local control, remote
control where supported, scene execution, automation execution, sensor
reporting, Vision event reporting, Act execution, Sync command behavior,
App interaction, Hub services, Gate communication, Cloud participation,
and Edge participation where applicable.

Functional testing must be performed according to supported product
type, firmware version, software version, deployment model, and expected
system behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**功能測試驗證核心系統功能是否按預期運作。它應涵蓋設備入網、本地控制、支援條件下遠端控制、場景執行、自動化執行、感測上報、Vision
事件上報、Act 執行、Sync 指令行為、App 互動、Hub 服務、Gate 通訊、Cloud
參與，以及適用時 Edge 參與。

功能測試必須依受支援產品類型、韌體版本、軟體版本、部署模型與預期系統行為進行。

## **English Table**

| **Functional Test Item** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Device onboarding | Device can be discovered, registered, and assigned |
| Local control | Supported local commands execute correctly |
| Remote control | Supported remote commands execute under cloud conditions |
| Scene execution | Configured scenes execute expected device actions |
| Automation execution | Rules trigger and execute as configured |
| Sensor reporting | Sense data reports correctly |
| Vision event reporting | Vision events report correctly where supported |
| Act execution | Relay, plug, or load control executes correctly |
| Sync command behavior | IR / RF command behavior works where supported |
| App interaction | Setup, control, configuration, and status display operate correctly |

## **中文表**

| **功能測試項目** | **預期驗證**                       |
|------------------|------------------------------------|
| 設備入網         | 設備可被發現、註冊與分配           |
| 本地控制         | 受支援本地指令正確執行             |
| 遠端控制         | 在雲端條件下受支援遠端指令正確執行 |
| 場景執行         | 已配置場景執行預期設備動作         |
| 自動化執行       | 規則按配置觸發與執行               |
| 感測上報         | Sense 數據正確上報                 |
| Vision 事件上報  | 支援條件下 Vision 事件正確上報     |
| Act 執行         | 繼電器、插座或負載控制正確執行     |
| Sync 指令行為    | 支援條件下 IR / RF 指令行為正常    |
| App 互動         | 設定、控制、配置與狀態顯示正常運作 |

## **17.5 Runtime Test**

## **17.5 Runtime 測試**

**EN  
**Runtime Test verifies local runtime behavior managed by Artibird Hub
and ArtiOS. It should cover local service hosting, event handling, state
management, command routing, scene execution, automation execution, data
synchronization, offline behavior, and Edge participation where
deployed.

Runtime testing must verify that the system follows defined priority
rules, permission rules, supported device capability, and expected
failure behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**Runtime 測試驗證由 Artibird Hub 與 ArtiOS 管理的本地 Runtime
行為。它應涵蓋本地服務承載、事件處理、狀態管理、指令路由、場景執行、自動化執行、數據同步、離線行為，以及部署條件下
Edge 參與。

Runtime
測試必須驗證系統是否遵循已定義優先級規則、權限規則、受支援設備能力與預期故障行為。

## **English Table**

| **Runtime Test Item** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Local service hosting | Hub services and ArtiOS modules operate correctly |
| Event handling | Events are processed by runtime logic |
| State management | Device and system states update correctly |
| Command routing | Commands reach intended targets |
| Scene execution | Runtime executes multi-device scenes correctly |
| Automation execution | Runtime executes configured rules correctly |
| Priority handling | Safety, manual control, automation, Edge, Cloud, and background priorities apply |
| Offline behavior | Supported local functions continue under defined offline conditions |
| Edge participation | Edge-assisted output informs runtime only within defined boundaries |

## **中文表**

| **Runtime 測試項目** | **預期驗證** |
|----|----|
| 本地服務承載 | Hub 服務與 ArtiOS 模組正常運作 |
| 事件處理 | 事件由 Runtime 邏輯正確處理 |
| 狀態管理 | 設備與系統狀態正確更新 |
| 指令路由 | 指令到達預期目標 |
| 場景執行 | Runtime 正確執行多設備場景 |
| 自動化執行 | Runtime 正確執行已配置規則 |
| 優先級處理 | 安全、手動控制、自動化、Edge、Cloud 與背景優先級正確適用 |
| 離線行為 | 在明確離線條件下受支援本地功能繼續 |
| Edge 參與 | Edge 輔助輸出僅在已定義邊界內影響 Runtime |

## **17.6 Connectivity Test**

## **17.6 連接測試**

**EN  
**Connectivity Test verifies network and gateway communication among
Hub, Gate, supported devices, App, Cloud, and Edge. It should cover
Ethernet, Wi-Fi, BLE Mesh, Wi-Fi Mesh where implemented, local MQTT, App
local connection, cloud connection, gateway communication, and offline
local behavior.

Connectivity testing must define network topology, device count,
firmware version, hardware version, signal condition, message rate, and
expected communication behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**連接測試驗證 Hub、Gate、受支援設備、App、Cloud 與 Edge
之間的網路與網關通訊。它應涵蓋 Ethernet、Wi-Fi、BLE Mesh、已實作條件下
Wi-Fi Mesh、本地 MQTT、App 本地連接、雲端連接、網關通訊與離線本地行為。

連接測試必須定義網路拓撲、設備數量、韌體版本、硬體版本、信號條件、消息速率與預期通訊行為。

## **English Table**

| **Connectivity Test Item** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Ethernet connection | Wired connection operates where supported |
| Wi-Fi connection | Wireless connection operates under defined conditions |
| BLE Mesh behavior | Supported BLE Mesh devices communicate correctly |
| Wi-Fi Mesh behavior | Wi-Fi Mesh operates only where implemented and validated |
| Local MQTT | Broker, topics, messages, authentication, and routing operate correctly |
| App local connection | App discovers and controls local system where supported |
| Cloud connection | Cloud access and synchronization operate under defined conditions |
| Gate communication | Gate passes supported device events and commands correctly |
| Offline local network | Local network behavior continues without Internet where supported |

## **中文表**

| **連接測試項目** | **預期驗證**                                |
|------------------|---------------------------------------------|
| Ethernet 連接    | 支援條件下有線連接正常運作                  |
| Wi-Fi 連接       | 在明確條件下無線連接正常運作                |
| BLE Mesh 行為    | 受支援 BLE Mesh 設備正確通訊                |
| Wi-Fi Mesh 行為  | Wi-Fi Mesh 僅在已實作與驗證條件下運作       |
| 本地 MQTT        | Broker、Topic、消息、身份認證與路由正常運作 |
| App 本地連接     | App 在支援條件下發現並控制本地系統          |
| 雲端連接         | 雲端存取與同步在明確條件下正常運作          |
| Gate 通訊        | Gate 正確傳遞受支援設備事件與指令           |
| 離線本地網路     | 無 Internet 時支援的本地網路行為繼續        |

## **17.7 Capacity Test**

## **17.7 容量測試**

**EN  
**Capacity Test verifies measurable system limits. It should validate
max concurrent device connections, max devices per Gate, max devices per
Hub, max scenes, max automations, max rooms / spaces, max users, max
sites, MQTT throughput, event latency, storage limits, Vision stream
limits, and Edge processing limits.

Capacity testing must be performed under defined hardware, firmware,
software, network, cloud, edge, runtime load, and deployment conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**容量測試驗證可量測系統限制。它應驗證最大併發設備連接數、每個 Gate
最大設備數、每個 Hub 最大設備數、最大場景數、最大自動化數、最大房間 /
空間數、最大用戶數、最大站點數、MQTT 吞吐量、事件延遲、儲存限制、Vision
視頻流限制與 Edge 處理限制。

容量測試必須在明確硬體、韌體、軟體、網路、雲端、Edge、Runtime
負載與部署條件下執行。

## **English Table**

| **Capacity Test Item** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Max concurrent device connections | Total active devices remain stable under defined load |
| Max devices per Gate | Gate maintains communication within validated capacity |
| Max devices per Hub | Hub maintains runtime behavior within validated capacity |
| Max scenes | Supported scene count operates correctly |
| Max automations | Supported automation count operates correctly |
| MQTT throughput | Message rate and latency meet acceptance criteria |
| Event latency | Source-to-action time meets expected requirement |
| Storage limits | Storage behavior follows defined retention and overflow rules |
| Vision stream limits | Vision streams operate within validated limits |
| Edge processing limits | Edge inference and processing remain within validated boundaries |

## **中文表**

| **容量測試項目**     | **預期驗證**                        |
|----------------------|-------------------------------------|
| 最大併發設備連接數   | 總活躍設備在明確負載下保持穩定      |
| 每個 Gate 最大設備數 | Gate 在已驗證容量內維持通訊         |
| 每個 Hub 最大設備數  | Hub 在已驗證容量內維持 Runtime 行為 |
| 最大場景數           | 支援場景數量正確運作                |
| 最大自動化數         | 支援自動化數量正確運作              |
| MQTT 吞吐量          | 消息速率與延遲符合驗收標準          |
| 事件延遲             | 從來源到動作的時間符合預期要求      |
| 儲存限制             | 儲存行為遵循已定義保留與溢出規則    |
| Vision 視頻流限制    | Vision 視頻流在已驗證限制內運作     |
| Edge 處理限制        | Edge 推理與處理保持在已驗證邊界內   |

## **17.8 Stress Test**

## **17.8 壓力測試**

**EN  
**Stress Test verifies long-duration operation and system behavior under
sustained or peak load. It should test device connections, message rate,
automation triggers, scene execution, cloud synchronization, Edge
processing, storage growth, network congestion, and recovery behavior.

Stress testing should identify system degradation, overload behavior,
memory growth, service instability, message delay, connection loss, and
recovery behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**壓力測試驗證長時間運作與系統在持續或峰值負載下的行為。它應測試設備連接、消息速率、自動化觸發、場景執行、雲端同步、Edge
處理、儲存增長、網路擁塞與恢復行為。

壓力測試應識別系統降級、過載行為、記憶體增長、服務不穩定、消息延遲、連接丟失與恢復行為。

## **English Table**

| **Stress Test Item** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Long-duration runtime | System remains stable over defined test duration |
| High event rate | Runtime processes peak event load |
| High device count | System remains stable with defined device count |
| Repeated scene execution | Scenes execute repeatedly without abnormal behavior |
| Repeated automation triggers | Automations execute under frequent trigger conditions |
| Cloud sync load | Synchronization remains stable or degrades as defined |
| Edge processing load | Edge behavior remains within defined limits |
| Storage growth | Storage behavior follows retention and overflow policy |
| Network congestion | System degrades according to defined behavior |

## **中文表**

| **壓力測試項目** | **預期驗證**                 |
|------------------|------------------------------|
| 長時間 Runtime   | 系統在明確測試時長內保持穩定 |
| 高事件速率       | Runtime 能處理峰值事件負載   |
| 高設備數量       | 系統在明確設備數量下保持穩定 |
| 重複場景執行     | 場景反覆執行無異常行為       |
| 重複自動化觸發   | 自動化在高頻觸發條件下執行   |
| 雲端同步負載     | 同步保持穩定或按定義降級     |
| Edge 處理負載    | Edge 行為保持在已定義限制內  |
| 儲存增長         | 儲存行為遵循保留與溢出策略   |
| 網路擁塞         | 系統依已定義行為降級         |

## **17.9 Failover Test**

## **17.9 故障切換測試**

**EN  
**Failover Test verifies how the system behaves when cloud, Internet,
Hub, Gate, devices, Edge, App, power, local network, or storage becomes
unavailable or degraded.

Failover testing should verify expected degraded operation, supported
local continuation, unavailable functions, recovery behavior, status
reporting, alert behavior, and command handling.

**ZH-TW  
**故障切換測試驗證當雲端、Internet、Hub、Gate、設備、Edge、App、電力、本地網路或儲存不可用或降級時，系統如何運作。

故障切換測試應驗證預期降級運作、受支援本地延續、不可用功能、恢復行為、狀態回報、警報行為與指令處理。

## **English Table**

| **Failover Scenario** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Cloud unavailable | Local supported functions continue where applicable |
| Internet unavailable | Local network behavior continues where configured |
| Hub unavailable | Hub-dependent runtime behavior stops or degrades as defined |
| Gate unavailable | Gate-dependent device access degrades as defined |
| Device offline | Device is marked offline and commands follow defined behavior |
| Edge unavailable | Edge-assisted functions stop or degrade while non-edge runtime continues |
| App unavailable | Physical controls and local automation continue where supported |
| Power failure | Recovery follows defined startup and state behavior |
| Network congestion | System degrades according to capacity and priority rules |

## **中文表**

| **故障切換場景** | **預期驗證**                                  |
|------------------|-----------------------------------------------|
| 雲端不可用       | 適用時受支援本地功能繼續                      |
| Internet 不可用  | 已配置條件下本地網路行為繼續                  |
| Hub 不可用       | Hub 依賴 Runtime 行為按定義停止或降級         |
| Gate 不可用      | 依賴 Gate 的設備接入按定義降級                |
| 設備離線         | 設備被標記離線，指令遵循已定義行為            |
| Edge 不可用      | Edge 輔助功能停止或降級，非 Edge Runtime 繼續 |
| App 不可用       | 支援條件下實體控制與本地自動化繼續            |
| 電力故障         | 恢復遵循已定義啟動與狀態行為                  |
| 網路擁塞         | 系統依容量與優先級規則降級                    |

## **17.10 Security Test**

## **17.10 安全測試**

**EN  
**Security Test verifies device identity, account binding, local access
control, remote access control, secure MQTT, firmware update security,
role-based access control, audit logs, and security-sensitive failure
behavior.

Security testing must verify both allowed behavior and rejected
behavior. Unauthorized access, invalid binding, invalid command,
unsupported device participation, invalid firmware, permission
violation, and insecure communication behavior must be tested where
applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**安全測試驗證設備身份、帳號綁定、本地存取控制、遠端存取控制、安全
MQTT、韌體更新安全、角色權限控制、審計日誌與安全敏感故障行為。

安全測試必須同時驗證允許行為與拒絕行為。未授權存取、無效綁定、無效指令、未支援設備參與、無效韌體、權限違反與不安全通訊行為，均應在適用條件下測試。

## **English Table**

| **Security Test Item** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Device identity | Device identity is verified before participation |
| Account binding | Binding follows permission and security rules |
| Local access control | Local commands follow permission rules |
| Remote access control | Remote access requires valid authentication and authorization |
| Secure MQTT | MQTT authentication and protection work where implemented |
| Firmware update security | Invalid or unauthorized updates are rejected |
| Role-based access control | Roles limit access as defined |
| Audit logs | Security-sensitive events are recorded where supported |
| Unauthorized access | Unauthorized behavior is rejected or blocked |

## **中文表**

| **安全測試項目** | **預期驗證**                     |
|------------------|----------------------------------|
| 設備身份         | 設備參與前完成身份驗證           |
| 帳號綁定         | 綁定遵循權限與安全規則           |
| 本地存取控制     | 本地指令遵循權限規則             |
| 遠端存取控制     | 遠端存取需要有效身份認證與授權   |
| 安全 MQTT        | 已實作條件下 MQTT 認證與保護正常 |
| 韌體更新安全     | 無效或未授權更新被拒絕           |
| 角色權限控制     | 角色依定義限制存取               |
| 審計日誌         | 支援條件下安全敏感事件被記錄     |
| 未授權存取       | 未授權行為被拒絕或阻止           |

## **17.11 Privacy Test**

## **17.11 隱私測試**

**EN  
**Privacy Test verifies data collection, storage, processing,
synchronization, retention, deletion, access permission, Vision data
behavior, cloud data policy, and Edge processing boundary.

Privacy testing should confirm that sensitive data behavior follows user
permission, privacy settings, storage rules, cloud synchronization
rules, Edge processing rules, and documented data policies.

**ZH-TW  
**隱私測試驗證數據收集、儲存、處理、同步、保留、刪除、存取權限、Vision
數據行為、雲端數據政策與 Edge 處理邊界。

隱私測試應確認敏感數據行為符合用戶權限、隱私設定、儲存規則、雲端同步規則、Edge
處理規則與已記錄數據政策。

## **English Table**

| **Privacy Test Item** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Data collection | Only defined data is collected |
| Data storage | Data is stored according to policy |
| Data retention | Retention follows defined duration and rules |
| Data deletion | Deletion or removal behavior works where supported |
| Vision privacy | Recording, storage, access, and sync follow privacy settings |
| Cloud data behavior | Cloud storage and use follow documented policy |
| Edge processing boundary | Edge processing follows local and privacy configuration |
| Access permission | Users can access only permitted data |
| Privacy restriction | Restricted data is not processed or shared outside defined rules |

## **中文表**

| **隱私測試項目** | **預期驗證**                       |
|------------------|------------------------------------|
| 數據收集         | 僅收集已定義數據                   |
| 數據儲存         | 數據依政策儲存                     |
| 數據保留         | 保留遵循已定義時長與規則           |
| 數據刪除         | 支援條件下刪除或移除行為正常       |
| Vision 隱私      | 錄影、儲存、存取與同步遵循隱私設定 |
| 雲端數據行為     | 雲端儲存與使用遵循已記錄政策       |
| Edge 處理邊界    | Edge 處理遵循本地與隱私配置        |
| 存取權限         | 用戶只能存取被允許數據             |
| 隱私限制         | 受限制數據不在規則之外被處理或共享 |

## **17.12 Compatibility Test**

## **17.12 相容性測試**

**EN  
**Compatibility Test verifies interoperability between supported
devices, firmware versions, hardware versions, software versions, App
versions, Hub versions, Gate versions, Cloud services, Edge services,
and deployment models.

Compatibility testing must confirm supported combinations and identify
unsupported combinations. Any compatibility claim must be backed by
validated product-system mapping evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**相容性測試驗證受支援設備、韌體版本、硬體版本、軟體版本、App 版本、Hub
版本、Gate 版本、Cloud 服務、Edge 服務與部署模型之間的互操作性。

相容性測試必須確認受支援組合，並識別不支援組合。任何相容性宣稱都必須具備已驗證產品—系統映射證據支持。

## **English Table**

| **Compatibility Test Item** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Product compatibility | Supported Artibird products operate together |
| Firmware compatibility | Firmware versions interoperate as expected |
| Hardware compatibility | Hardware revisions remain within supported behavior |
| App compatibility | App version works with supported system versions |
| Hub / Gate compatibility | Hub and Gate operate correctly together |
| Cloud compatibility | Cloud services support required product versions |
| Edge compatibility | Edge integrates with supported Vision, Sense, and runtime data |
| Deployment compatibility | Product combinations fit target deployment model |

## **中文表**

| **相容性測試項目** | **預期驗證**                                    |
|--------------------|-------------------------------------------------|
| 產品相容性         | 受支援 Artibird 產品可共同運作                  |
| 韌體相容性         | 韌體版本按預期互操作                            |
| 硬體相容性         | 硬體修訂保持在受支援行為內                      |
| App 相容性         | App 版本可與受支援系統版本協同                  |
| Hub / Gate 相容性  | Hub 與 Gate 正確共同運作                        |
| 雲端相容性         | 雲端服務支援所需產品版本                        |
| Edge 相容性        | Edge 與受支援 Vision、Sense 與 Runtime 數據整合 |
| 部署相容性         | 產品組合符合目標部署模型                        |

## **17.13 Deployment Test**

## **17.13 部署測試**

**EN  
**Deployment Test verifies scenario-specific system behavior across
residential, classroom, office, building, campus, energy management,
vision-aware security, agriculture, and infrastructure deployments.

Deployment testing must verify component placement, network topology,
device count, local runtime behavior, cloud behavior, Edge behavior,
failure behavior, and expected user operation under real or
representative site conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**部署測試驗證系統在住宅、教室、辦公、建築、校園、能源管理、視覺感知安全、農業與基礎設施部署中的特定場景行為。

部署測試必須在真實或代表性場地條件下，驗證組件佈置、網路拓撲、設備數量、本地
Runtime 行為、雲端行為、Edge 行為、故障行為與預期用戶操作。

## **English Table**

| **Deployment Test Item** | **Expected Verification** |
|----|----|
| Residential deployment | Home local control, scenes, automation, and remote access where supported |
| Smart classroom | Classroom control, energy, climate, AV, and panel behavior |
| Smart office | Meeting room, workspace, and shared area coordination |
| Smart building | Multi-room or multi-zone operation |
| Smart campus | Multi-building or multi-site operation |
| Energy management | Energy measurement, reporting, alerts, and control where supported |
| Vision-aware security | Vision event, Edge analysis, cloud alert, and privacy behavior |
| Agriculture / infrastructure | Outdoor or facility-oriented sensing and execution behavior |

## **中文表**

| **部署測試項目** | **預期驗證**                                   |
|------------------|------------------------------------------------|
| 住宅部署         | 支援條件下家庭本地控制、場景、自動化與遠端存取 |
| 智慧教室         | 教室控制、能源、空調、影音與面板行為           |
| 智慧辦公         | 會議室、工位區與共享區域協同                   |
| 智慧建築         | 多房間或多區域運作                             |
| 智慧校園         | 多建築或多站點運作                             |
| 能源管理         | 支援條件下能源計量、報告、警報與控制           |
| 視覺感知安全     | Vision 事件、Edge 分析、雲端警報與隱私行為     |
| 農業 / 基礎設施  | 戶外或設施導向感知與執行行為                   |

## **17.14 Test Evidence Requirements**

## **17.14 測試證據要求**

**EN  
**Test evidence must be recorded for any system claim. Evidence should
include test scope, test condition, product type, hardware version,
firmware version, software version, network topology, device count,
cloud condition, Edge condition, expected result, observed result,
failure behavior, and acceptance criteria.

Test evidence should be traceable to the system function, product
specification, deployment scenario, and commercial claim where
applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**任何系統宣稱都必須記錄測試證據。證據應包含測試範圍、測試條件、產品類型、硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、網路拓撲、設備數量、雲端條件、Edge
條件、預期結果、觀察結果、故障行為與驗收標準。

測試證據應可追溯至適用的系統功能、產品規格書、部署場景與商業宣稱。

## **English Table**

| **Evidence Item** | **Required Content** |
|----|----|
| Test ID | Unique test identifier |
| Test category | Functional, runtime, connectivity, capacity, stress, failover, security, privacy, compatibility, deployment |
| Test objective | What the test verifies |
| Test condition | Defined hardware, firmware, software, network, cloud, edge, and deployment condition |
| Product mix | Products and versions used in the test |
| Device count | Number and type of devices under test |
| Expected result | Required behavior |
| Observed result | Actual result |
| Pass / fail status | Final test result |
| Evidence record | Logs, screenshots, reports, measurements, or videos where applicable |

## **中文表**

| **證據項目** | **必須內容** |
|----|----|
| 測試 ID | 唯一測試識別碼 |
| 測試類別 | 功能、Runtime、連接、容量、壓力、故障切換、安全、隱私、相容性、部署 |
| 測試目標 | 測試驗證的內容 |
| 測試條件 | 明確硬體、韌體、軟體、網路、雲端、Edge 與部署條件 |
| 產品組合 | 測試中使用的產品與版本 |
| 設備數量 | 測試中的設備數量與類型 |
| 預期結果 | 所需行為 |
| 觀察結果 | 實際結果 |
| 通過 / 失敗狀態 | 最終測試結果 |
| 證據記錄 | 適用時日誌、截圖、報告、量測數據或視頻 |

## **17.15 Testing Boundary**

## **17.15 測試邊界**

**EN  
**Testing and validation must be described according to defined test
conditions. A successful test under one hardware version, firmware
version, software version, network topology, device count, deployment
model, or cloud / edge condition does not automatically validate all
other conditions.

Testing results must not be generalized beyond the tested scope unless
additional validation evidence is available.

**ZH-TW  
**測試與驗證必須依明確測試條件描述。在某一硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、網路拓撲、設備數量、部署模型或雲端
/ Edge 條件下測試成功，不自動代表其他所有條件已完成驗證。

除非具備額外驗證證據，否則測試結果不得超出已測範圍進行泛化。

## **17.16 Validation Requirements**

## **17.16 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any claim involving system function, runtime behavior, connectivity,
capacity, reliability, security, privacy, compatibility, deployment,
cloud participation, edge participation, AI-assisted behavior, offline
behavior, or commercial positioning must be supported by validation
evidence under defined conditions.

Validation must be reviewed before the claim is used in engineering
documents, commercial specifications, product catalogs, websites,
channel documents, installation guides, or sales materials.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及系統功能、Runtime
行為、連接、容量、可靠性、安全、隱私、相容性、部署、雲端參與、Edge
參與、AI
輔助行為、離線行為或商業定位的宣稱，都必須在明確條件下具備驗證證據支持。

在工程文件、商業規格書、產品型錄、網站、渠道文件、安裝指南或銷售資料中使用相關宣稱之前，必須先完成驗證審查。

## **17.17 Chapter Conclusion**

## **17.17 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the testing and validation structure of the
OceanAI / Artibird system. It explains how functional, runtime,
connectivity, capacity, stress, failover, security, privacy,
compatibility, and deployment tests must be performed under defined
conditions, and how validation evidence must support system,
engineering, and commercial claims.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的測試與驗證結構。它說明功能、Runtime、連接、容量、壓力、故障切換、安全、隱私、相容性與部署測試，必須如何在明確條件下執行，以及驗證證據必須如何支援系統、工程與商業宣稱。

chap 18 商業與宣稱邊界

# **chap 18 商業與宣稱邊界**

# **18. Commercial and Claim Boundaries**

# **18. 商業與宣稱邊界**

## **18.1 Purpose**

## **18.1 目的**

**EN  
**This section prevents system-level overclaims and ensures that
commercial language remains aligned with engineering validation.

**ZH-TW  
**本章防止系統級過度宣稱，並確保商業語言與工程驗證保持一致。

## **18.2 Commercial and Claim Boundaries Definition**

## **18.2 商業與宣稱邊界定義**

**EN  
**Commercial and Claim Boundaries define how the OceanAI / Artibird
system may be described in product documents, commercial specifications,
websites, product catalogs, channel materials, installation guides,
sales presentations, and customer-facing communication.

All commercial claims must remain aligned with supported system
capabilities, product specifications, engineering validation, deployment
conditions, security and privacy boundaries, certification status, and
test evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**商業與宣稱邊界定義 OceanAI / Artibird
系統可如何被描述於產品文件、商業規格書、網站、產品型錄、渠道材料、安裝指南、銷售簡報與面向客戶的溝通內容中。

所有商業宣稱都必須與受支援系統能力、產品規格書、工程驗證、部署條件、安全與隱私邊界、認證狀態與測試證據保持一致。

## **18.3 Claim Control Table**

## **18.3 宣稱管控表**

## **English Table**

| **Restricted Claim** | **Preferred Language** |
|----|----|
| Works with everything | Works with supported and validated Artibird devices |
| Fully autonomous AI system | AI-assisted coordinated system under defined conditions |
| Unlimited devices | Validated capacity under defined conditions |
| Always works offline | Supports defined local functions when required local components are present |
| Guaranteed energy savings | Supports energy-aware workflows where validated |
| Perfect AI vision detection | Supports defined visual event detection where validated |
| Certified safe | Use only after certification is complete |

## **中文表**

| **限制宣稱**     | **建議語言**                             |
|------------------|------------------------------------------|
| 支援所有設備     | 支援受支援且已驗證的 Artibird 設備       |
| 完全自主 AI 系統 | 在明確條件下的 AI 輔助協同系統           |
| 無限制設備       | 在明確條件下的已驗證容量                 |
| 永遠離線可用     | 當所需本地元件具備時，支援已定義本地功能 |
| 保證節能         | 在已驗證條件下支援能源感知工作流         |
| 完美 AI 視覺偵測 | 在已驗證條件下支援明確視覺事件偵測       |
| 已認證安全       | 僅在認證完成後使用                       |

## **18.4 System-Level Claim Principle**

## **18.4 系統級宣稱原則**

**EN  
**System-level claims must describe the OceanAI / Artibird system
according to actual supported architecture, runtime behavior, product
capability, local-first operation, cloud-enhanced behavior,
edge-assisted intelligence, validated capacity, and defined deployment
conditions.

Commercial language may simplify technical content for readability, but
it must not create unsupported assumptions about compatibility,
capacity, reliability, AI capability, offline behavior, security,
privacy, certification, or deployment scale.

**ZH-TW  
**系統級宣稱必須依據實際受支援架構、Runtime
行為、產品能力、本地優先運作、雲端增強行為、Edge
輔助智慧、已驗證容量與已定義部署條件來描述 OceanAI / Artibird 系統。

商業語言可以為了可讀性簡化技術內容，但不得造成對相容性、容量、可靠性、AI
能力、離線行為、安全、隱私、認證或部署規模的未支援假設。

## **18.5 Product Compatibility Claims**

## **18.5 產品相容性宣稱**

**EN  
**Product compatibility claims must be limited to supported and
validated Artibird products, versions, communication paths, firmware
versions, software versions, and deployment models.

The system must not be described as universally compatible with all
third-party devices, all smart home platforms, all protocols, all
appliances, all routers, all electrical loads, or all installation
environments unless such compatibility has been validated and
documented.

**ZH-TW  
**產品相容性宣稱必須限制於受支援且已驗證的 Artibird
產品、版本、通訊路徑、韌體版本、軟體版本與部署模型。

除非相關相容性已完成驗證並形成文件，否則不得將系統描述為與所有第三方設備、所有智慧家居平台、所有協議、所有家電、所有路由器、所有電氣負載或所有安裝環境通用相容。

## **English Table**

| **Claim Area** | **Acceptable Claim Boundary** |
|----|----|
| Artibird compatibility | Supported and validated Artibird products |
| Third-party device compatibility | Only where tested and documented |
| Protocol compatibility | Only supported protocols and versions |
| Appliance compatibility | Only supported appliance categories and models where validated |
| Router compatibility | General router use may be stated only within tested network conditions |
| Platform compatibility | Only integrated and validated platforms |
| Electrical load compatibility | Only supported load types and ratings defined by product specifications |

## **中文表**

| **宣稱領域**     | **可接受宣稱邊界**                         |
|------------------|--------------------------------------------|
| Artibird 相容性  | 受支援且已驗證的 Artibird 產品             |
| 第三方設備相容性 | 僅限已測試並記錄的情況                     |
| 協議相容性       | 僅限受支援協議與版本                       |
| 家電相容性       | 僅限已驗證的受支援家電類別與型號           |
| 路由器相容性     | 僅可在已測網路條件內描述一般路由器使用     |
| 平台相容性       | 僅限已整合且已驗證平台                     |
| 電氣負載相容性   | 僅限產品規格書定義的受支援負載類型與額定值 |

## **18.6 Capacity Claims**

## **18.6 容量宣稱**

**EN  
**Capacity claims must be based on validated test reports under defined
hardware, firmware, software, network, cloud, edge, and deployment
conditions.

Any statement involving concurrent device connections, devices per Gate,
devices per Hub, MQTT throughput, event latency, number of scenes,
number of automations, Vision stream count, Edge processing load, users,
rooms, spaces, or sites must include or reference validated conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**容量宣稱必須基於明確硬體、韌體、軟體、網路、雲端、Edge
與部署條件下的已驗證測試報告。

任何涉及併發設備連接、每個 Gate 設備數、每個 Hub 設備數、MQTT
吞吐量、事件延遲、場景數、自動化數、Vision 視頻流數量、Edge
處理負載、用戶、房間、空間或站點的表述，都必須包含或引用已驗證條件。

## **English Table**

| **Capacity Claim Type** | **Required Boundary** |
|----|----|
| Max concurrent devices | Must state validated device count and test condition |
| Max devices per Gate | Must state Gate model, firmware version, protocol, and test condition |
| Max devices per Hub | Must state Hub hardware, service load, and test condition |
| MQTT throughput | Must state message rate, latency, and load condition |
| Event latency | Must state source, target, network path, and load condition |
| Vision streams | Must state Vision device count, stream type, storage, network, and processing condition |
| Edge processing | Must state hardware platform, model version, input type, and load condition |

## **中文表**

| **容量宣稱類型** | **必須邊界** |
|----|----|
| 最大併發設備數 | 必須說明已驗證設備數與測試條件 |
| 每個 Gate 最大設備數 | 必須說明 Gate 型號、韌體版本、協議與測試條件 |
| 每個 Hub 最大設備數 | 必須說明 Hub 硬體、服務負載與測試條件 |
| MQTT 吞吐量 | 必須說明消息速率、延遲與負載條件 |
| 事件延遲 | 必須說明來源、目標、網路路徑與負載條件 |
| Vision 視頻流 | 必須說明 Vision 設備數、視頻流類型、儲存、網路與處理條件 |
| Edge 處理 | 必須說明硬體平台、模型版本、輸入類型與負載條件 |

## **18.7 Local-First and Offline Claims**

## **18.7 本地優先與離線宣稱**

**EN  
**Local-first and offline claims must clearly define which functions
operate locally and which functions require cloud services.

The system may be described as local-first only when the statement
refers to supported local functions under required local component
conditions. It must not be described as fully offline for all functions
unless all referenced functions have been validated without Internet or
cloud access.

**ZH-TW  
**本地優先與離線宣稱必須清楚定義哪些功能可本地運作，哪些功能需要雲端服務。

只有當表述指向在所需本地元件條件下受支援本地功能時，才可將系統描述為本地優先。除非所引用的全部功能都已在無
Internet
或無雲端存取條件下完成驗證，否則不得描述為所有功能完全離線可用。

## **English Table**

| **Claim Type** | **Required Boundary** |
|----|----|
| Local-first control | Must define required local components |
| Offline scene execution | Must define local scene configuration and required devices |
| Offline automation | Must define local automation rules and input / output devices |
| Offline App control | Must define local network, App version, Hub availability, and permission condition |
| Cloud-independent behavior | Must specify which behavior does not require cloud |
| Remote access | Must be described as cloud-required |
| Cloud synchronization | Must be described as unavailable or delayed when cloud is unavailable |

## **中文表**

| **宣稱類型**   | **必須邊界**                                     |
|----------------|--------------------------------------------------|
| 本地優先控制   | 必須定義所需本地組件                             |
| 離線場景執行   | 必須定義本地場景配置與所需設備                   |
| 離線自動化     | 必須定義本地自動化規則與輸入 / 輸出設備          |
| 離線 App 控制  | 必須定義本地網路、App 版本、Hub 可用性與權限條件 |
| 不依賴雲端行為 | 必須說明哪些行為不需要雲端                       |
| 遠端存取       | 必須描述為需要雲端                               |
| 雲端同步       | 必須描述為雲端不可用時不可用或延遲               |

## **18.8 Cloud Claims**

## **18.8 雲端宣稱**

**EN  
**Cloud claims must be limited to implemented and supported OceanAI
Cloud services. Cloud services may include remote access,
synchronization, account services, alerts, lifecycle management,
historical data, analytics, multi-site management, and commercial
service plans where supported.

Cloud claims must not imply guaranteed cloud availability, unlimited
storage, unrestricted remote access, unsupported service levels, or
undefined data use.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端宣稱必須限制於已實作且受支援的 OceanAI Cloud
服務。雲端服務可在支援條件下包括遠端存取、同步、帳號服務、警報、生命週期管理、歷史數據、分析、多站點管理與商業服務方案。

雲端宣稱不得暗示保證雲端可用、無限制儲存、不受限制遠端存取、未支援服務等級或未定義數據使用。

## **English Table**

| **Cloud Claim Type** | **Required Boundary** |
|----|----|
| Remote access | Requires Internet, account binding, permission, and cloud availability |
| Cloud synchronization | Requires supported data type and cloud availability |
| Alerts | Requires supported event type, App permission, and notification condition |
| Historical data | Requires enabled service, storage policy, and retention rule |
| Multi-site management | Requires supported account or organization structure |
| Firmware lifecycle | Requires supported product, version, and update path |
| Cloud analytics | Requires supported data source and policy-defined data use |

## **中文表**

| **雲端宣稱類型** | **必須邊界**                              |
|------------------|-------------------------------------------|
| 遠端存取         | 需要 Internet、帳號綁定、權限與雲端可用性 |
| 雲端同步         | 需要受支援數據類型與雲端可用性            |
| 警報             | 需要受支援事件類型、App 權限與通知條件    |
| 歷史數據         | 需要已啟用服務、儲存政策與保留規則        |
| 多站點管理       | 需要受支援帳號或組織結構                  |
| 韌體生命週期     | 需要受支援產品、版本與更新路徑            |
| 雲端分析         | 需要受支援數據來源與政策定義數據使用      |

## **18.9 Edge and AI Claims**

## **18.9 Edge 與 AI 宣稱**

**EN  
**Edge and AI claims must be described as AI-assisted behavior under
defined conditions. Claims involving SLM, VLM, visual understanding,
sensor fusion, optimization, energy behavior, security interpretation,
or automation support must state the supported model, input type,
deployment condition, privacy boundary, and validation requirement.

The system must not be described as fully autonomous, perfectly
accurate, universally intelligent, or capable of unrestricted control
unless such behavior is explicitly implemented, validated, and bounded
by safety, permission, and runtime rules.

**ZH-TW  
**Edge 與 AI 宣稱必須描述為在明確條件下的 AI 輔助行為。任何涉及
SLM、VLM、視覺理解、感測融合、優化、能源行為、安全解讀或自動化支援的宣稱，都必須說明受支援模型、輸入類型、部署條件、隱私邊界與驗證要求。

不得將系統描述為完全自主、完美準確、通用智慧或可不受限制控制，除非此類行為已明確實作、驗證，並受到安全、權限與
Runtime 規則約束。

## **English Table**

| **Restricted AI Claim** | **Preferred Language** |
|----|----|
| Fully autonomous AI control | AI-assisted runtime support under defined conditions |
| Perfect visual understanding | Supports defined visual interpretation where validated |
| Guaranteed optimization | Provides AI-assisted optimization suggestions where validated |
| Understands every environment | Interprets supported input data under validated deployment conditions |
| Replaces user decisions | Assists runtime behavior while following permissions and control boundaries |
| Always improves energy efficiency | Supports energy-aware workflows where validated |
| Fully private AI by default | Privacy behavior follows configuration, policy, and validated processing boundary |

## **中文表**

| **限制 AI 宣稱** | **建議語言**                            |
|------------------|-----------------------------------------|
| 完全自主 AI 控制 | 在明確條件下提供 AI 輔助 Runtime 支援   |
| 完美視覺理解     | 在已驗證條件下支援明確視覺解讀          |
| 保證優化         | 在已驗證條件下提供 AI 輔助優化建議      |
| 理解所有環境     | 在已驗證部署條件下解讀受支援輸入數據    |
| 取代用戶決策     | 在遵循權限與控制邊界下輔助 Runtime 行為 |
| 永遠提升能源效率 | 在已驗證條件下支援能源感知工作流        |
| 預設完全私有 AI  | 隱私行為遵循配置、政策與已驗證處理邊界  |

## **18.10 Security and Privacy Claims**

## **18.10 安全與隱私宣稱**

**EN  
**Security and privacy claims must match implemented behavior,
documented data policies, permission rules, and validation evidence.

The system must not be described as absolutely secure, impossible to
breach, fully private under all conditions, or compliant with every
external regulation unless such claims are legally reviewed, technically
validated, and supported by proper documentation.

**ZH-TW  
**安全與隱私宣稱必須符合已實作行為、已記錄數據政策、權限規則與驗證證據。

除非此類宣稱已完成法律審查、技術驗證並具備適當文件支持，否則不得將系統描述為絕對安全、無法被攻破、所有條件下完全私密，或符合所有外部法規。

## **English Table**

| **Security / Privacy Claim** | **Required Boundary** |
|----|----|
| Secure device access | Must state implemented authentication and access control |
| Secure MQTT | Must state where authentication and encryption are implemented |
| Privacy protection | Must follow documented privacy settings and data policy |
| Vision privacy | Must define recording, storage, access, sync, and retention behavior |
| Edge privacy | Must define local processing and cloud sync boundary |
| Cloud data protection | Must follow cloud data storage, access, and retention policy |
| Role-based access | Must define supported roles and permission model |
| Audit logging | Must state supported log types and retention behavior |

## **中文表**

| **安全 / 隱私宣稱** | **必須邊界**                             |
|---------------------|------------------------------------------|
| 安全設備存取        | 必須說明已實作身份認證與存取控制         |
| 安全 MQTT           | 必須說明哪些條件下實作身份認證與加密     |
| 隱私保護            | 必須遵循已記錄隱私設定與數據政策         |
| Vision 隱私         | 必須定義錄影、儲存、存取、同步與保留行為 |
| Edge 隱私           | 必須定義本地處理與雲端同步邊界           |
| 雲端數據保護        | 必須遵循雲端數據儲存、存取與保留政策     |
| 角色權限            | 必須定義受支援角色與權限模型             |
| 審計日誌            | 必須說明受支援日誌類型與保留行為         |

## **18.11 Reliability Claims**

## **18.11 可靠性宣稱**

**EN  
**Reliability claims must be based on tested failure behavior, recovery
behavior, degraded operation, offline behavior, and capacity boundaries.

The system must not be described as never failing, never disconnecting,
always online, always cloud-available, or always functioning under all
network, power, product, and deployment conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**可靠性宣稱必須基於已測試故障行為、恢復行為、降級運作、離線行為與容量邊界。

不得將系統描述為永不故障、永不斷線、永遠在線、雲端永遠可用，或在所有網路、電力、產品與部署條件下永遠正常運作。

## **English Table**

| **Restricted Reliability Claim** | **Preferred Language** |
|----|----|
| Never disconnects | Designed for stable operation under validated conditions |
| Always online | Supports defined online and offline behavior |
| Always works during Internet outage | Supports defined local functions when required local components are present |
| No failure | Includes defined failure, degraded, and recovery behavior |
| Always recovers automatically | Recovery behavior depends on product, network, power, and system condition |
| Works in all environments | Works under supported deployment and environmental conditions |

## **中文表**

| **限制可靠性宣稱**      | **建議語言**                             |
|-------------------------|------------------------------------------|
| 永不斷線                | 在已驗證條件下設計用於穩定運作           |
| 永遠在線                | 支援已定義在線與離線行為                 |
| Internet 中斷時永遠可用 | 當所需本地元件具備時，支援已定義本地功能 |
| 無故障                  | 包含已定義故障、降級與恢復行為           |
| 永遠自動恢復            | 恢復行為取決於產品、網路、電力與系統條件 |
| 適用所有環境            | 在受支援部署與環境條件下運作             |

## **18.12 Energy Claims**

## **18.12 能源宣稱**

**EN  
**Energy-related claims must be based on validated measurement,
supported Act-E or energy-capable devices, supported data sources,
defined deployment conditions, and documented calculation method.

The system may be described as supporting energy-aware workflows where
validated. It must not be described as guaranteeing energy savings
unless supported by controlled test evidence and clearly defined
conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**能源相關宣稱必須基於已驗證量測、受支援 Act-E
或具備能源能力的設備、受支援數據來源、明確部署條件與已記錄計算方法。

在已驗證條件下，系統可描述為支援能源感知工作流。除非具備受控測試證據與明確條件，否則不得描述為保證節能。

## **English Table**

| **Energy Claim Type** | **Required Boundary** |
|----|----|
| Energy monitoring | Requires supported energy measurement device |
| Energy report | Requires defined data source and calculation method |
| Energy optimization | Must be described as assisted or rule-based unless validated otherwise |
| Energy saving | Must include tested scenario, baseline, method, and result |
| Load control | Must follow supported load type and rating |
| Energy alert | Requires supported threshold, measurement, and notification path |

## **中文表**

| **能源宣稱類型** | **必須邊界**                           |
|------------------|----------------------------------------|
| 能源監測         | 需要受支援能源計量設備                 |
| 能源報告         | 需要已定義數據來源與計算方法           |
| 能源優化         | 除非另有驗證，必須描述為輔助或基於規則 |
| 節能             | 必須包含已測場景、基準、方法與結果     |
| 負載控制         | 必須遵循受支援負載類型與額定值         |
| 能源警報         | 需要受支援閾值、量測與通知路徑         |

## **18.13 Certification Claims**

## **18.13 認證宣稱**

**EN  
**Certification claims must only be used after certification is complete
and supported by official documentation.

Product documents may state certification targets, certification
planning, or certification readiness only if the language clearly
indicates that certification is not yet complete. Certification claims
must not imply UL, ETL, FCC, CE, or other certification status before
approval is granted.

**ZH-TW  
**認證宣稱只能在認證完成並具備官方文件支持後使用。

如果認證尚未完成，產品文件可描述認證目標、認證規劃或認證準備狀態，但語言必須清楚表明認證尚未完成。在獲得核准之前，不得暗示已具備
UL、ETL、FCC、CE 或其他認證狀態。

## **English Table**

| **Certification Language** | **Usage Condition** |
|----|----|
| Certified | Use only after certification is complete |
| Listed | Use only when listing is officially granted |
| Compliant | Use only where compliance is verified and legally appropriate |
| Designed for certification | May be used for design intention if not misleading |
| Certification target | May be used when clearly identified as a target |
| Certification pending | May be used only if actually in process |
| Certification ready | Use carefully and only when supported by internal review |

## **中文表**

| **認證語言** | **使用條件**                       |
|--------------|------------------------------------|
| 已認證       | 僅在認證完成後使用                 |
| Listed       | 僅在官方 Listing 獲准後使用        |
| 符合         | 僅在合規性已驗證且法律上適當時使用 |
| 為認證而設計 | 在不造成誤導時，可用於描述設計意圖 |
| 認證目標     | 明確標示為目標時可使用             |
| 認證進行中   | 僅在實際進行中時使用               |
| 認證準備就緒 | 需謹慎使用，且必須有內部審查支持   |

## **18.14 Commercial Document Alignment**

## **18.14 商業文件對齊**

**EN  
**Commercial documents must remain aligned with this system
specification and related product engineering specifications. This
includes commercial specifications, product catalogs, website copy,
Amazon listings, channel materials, sales presentations, partner guides,
installation overview documents, and training materials.

If a commercial statement depends on engineering validation, the
validation condition must be documented before the statement is used
externally.

**ZH-TW  
**商業文件必須與本系統規格書及相關產品工程規格書保持一致。這包括商業規格書、產品型錄、網站文案、Amazon
上架文案、渠道材料、銷售簡報、合作夥伴指南、安裝概覽文件與培訓材料。

如果某一商業表述依賴工程驗證，則在對外使用之前，必須記錄其驗證條件。

## **English Table**

| **Commercial Document** | **Alignment Requirement** |
|----|----|
| Commercial specification | Must reflect supported product and system capabilities |
| Product catalog | Must not overstate compatibility, capacity, or deployment scope |
| Website copy | Must remain consistent with validated system behavior |
| Amazon listing | Must avoid unsupported claims and certification misuse |
| Channel material | Must define target use cases and supported conditions |
| Sales presentation | Must distinguish current capability, roadmap, and target plan |
| Partner guide | Must align with deployment, support, and validation boundaries |
| Training material | Must describe supported operation and limitations clearly |

## **中文表**

| **商業文件**    | **對齊要求**                       |
|-----------------|------------------------------------|
| 商業規格書      | 必須反映受支援產品與系統能力       |
| 產品型錄        | 不得誇大相容性、容量或部署範圍     |
| 網站文案        | 必須與已驗證系統行為一致           |
| Amazon 上架文案 | 必須避免未支援宣稱與認證誤用       |
| 渠道材料        | 必須定義目標使用場景與受支援條件   |
| 銷售簡報        | 必須區分當前能力、路線圖與目標計劃 |
| 合作夥伴指南    | 必須與部署、支援與驗證邊界一致     |
| 培訓材料        | 必須清楚描述受支援運作與限制       |

## **18.15 Claim Review Requirement**

## **18.15 宣稱審查要求**

**EN  
**System-level claims should be reviewed before publication. Review
should include engineering, product, testing, certification, security,
privacy, and commercial stakeholders where applicable.

Claims involving capacity, AI, security, privacy, certification,
reliability, deployment, energy, or compatibility require validation
evidence before external use.

**ZH-TW  
**系統級宣稱在發布前應完成審查。審查應在適用條件下包含工程、產品、測試、認證、安全、隱私與商業相關人員。

涉及容量、AI、安全、隱私、認證、可靠性、部署、能源或相容性的宣稱，在對外使用前必須具備驗證證據。

## **English Table**

| **Claim Review Item** | **Required Reviewer** |
|----|----|
| Capacity claim | Engineering and testing |
| AI / Edge claim | Edge, AI, product, and testing |
| Security claim | Security and engineering |
| Privacy claim | Privacy, product, and legal / policy review where applicable |
| Certification claim | Certification and legal / compliance review where applicable |
| Reliability claim | Engineering and testing |
| Deployment claim | Product, engineering, and field validation |
| Energy claim | Engineering, testing, and data validation |
| Compatibility claim | Product, engineering, and testing |
| Commercial positioning | Product and commercial teams |

## **中文表**

| **宣稱審查項目** | **必要審查方**                    |
|------------------|-----------------------------------|
| 容量宣稱         | 工程與測試                        |
| AI / Edge 宣稱   | Edge、AI、產品與測試              |
| 安全宣稱         | 安全與工程                        |
| 隱私宣稱         | 適用時隱私、產品與法律 / 政策審查 |
| 認證宣稱         | 適用時認證與法律 / 合規審查       |
| 可靠性宣稱       | 工程與測試                        |
| 部署宣稱         | 產品、工程與現場驗證              |
| 能源宣稱         | 工程、測試與數據驗證              |
| 相容性宣稱       | 產品、工程與測試                  |
| 商業定位         | 產品與商業團隊                    |

## **18.16 Claim Boundary**

## **18.16 宣稱邊界**

**EN  
**Commercial and claim language must be described according to
implemented system capability, supported product type, validated
performance, security and privacy policy, certification status,
deployment condition, and testing evidence.

Claim boundaries do not prevent commercial communication. They ensure
that commercial communication remains accurate, supportable, and aligned
with system engineering reality.

**ZH-TW  
**商業與宣稱語言必須依據已實作系統能力、受支援產品類型、已驗證性能、安全與隱私政策、認證狀態、部署條件與測試證據進行描述。

宣稱邊界不是限制商業溝通，而是確保商業溝通保持準確、可支持，並與系統工程實際情況一致。

## **18.17 Validation Requirements**

## **18.17 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any commercial claim involving system function, product compatibility,
capacity, local-first behavior, offline operation, cloud services, Edge
/ AI behavior, security, privacy, reliability, deployment, energy,
certification, or commercial service plans must be supported by
validation evidence or clearly described as a target, planned
capability, or future roadmap item where appropriate.

Validation should include the claim text, supporting system function,
product type, test evidence, condition statement, limitation statement,
and approval record.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及系統功能、產品相容性、容量、本地優先行為、離線運作、雲端服務、Edge
/ AI
行為、安全、隱私、可靠性、部署、能源、認證或商業服務方案的商業宣稱，都必須具備驗證證據支持；若尚未完成驗證，應在適當情況下清楚描述為目標、計劃能力或未來路線圖項目。

驗證應包含宣稱文本、支援系統功能、產品類型、測試證據、條件聲明、限制聲明與核准記錄。

## **18.18 Chapter Conclusion**

## **18.18 章節結論**

**EN  
**This chapter defines the commercial and claim boundaries of the
OceanAI / Artibird system. It explains how product compatibility,
capacity, local-first behavior, cloud services, Edge and AI behavior,
security, privacy, reliability, energy, certification, and commercial
documents must remain aligned with engineering validation, supported
capabilities, deployment conditions, and documented evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**本章定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的商業與宣稱邊界。它說明產品相容性、容量、本地優先行為、雲端服務、Edge
與 AI
行為、安全、隱私、可靠性、能源、認證與商業文件，必須如何與工程驗證、受支援能力、部署條件與已記錄證據保持一致。

chap 19 版本記錄

# **chap 19 版本記錄**

# **19. Revision History**

# **19. 版本記錄**

## **19.1 Purpose**

## **19.1 目的**

**EN  
This section defines the revision history of the OceanAI / Artibird
System Specification. It records version changes, release dates,
document status, and the scope of each revision.**

**ZH-TW  
本章定義《OceanAI / Artibird
系統規格書》的版本記錄。它記錄版本變更、發布日期、文件狀態與每次修訂的範圍。**

## **19.2 Revision History Definition**

## **19.2 版本記錄定義**

**EN  
Revision History provides a formal record of how this system
specification changes over time. It helps architecture, product,
firmware, backend, App, testing, certification, commercial, and system
integration teams understand which version should be used as the current
system-level reference.**

**Each revision should include the version number, date, description,
change scope, and approval status where applicable.**

**ZH-TW  
版本記錄提供本系統規格書如何隨時間變更的正式記錄。它幫助架構、產品、韌體、後端、App、測試、認證、商業與系統整合團隊理解應使用哪一個版本作為當前系統級參考文件。**

**每次修訂應在適用條件下包含版本號、日期、說明、變更範圍與核准狀態。**

## **19.3 Revision History Table**

## **19.3 版本記錄表**

## **English Table**

| **Version** | **Date** | **Description** |
|----|----|----|
| **v1.0** | **2026-05-08** | **Initial OceanAI / Artibird System Specification Template** |
| **v1.0-Final** | **2026-05-08** | **Finalized foundational system specification template for OceanAI / Artibird system-level documentation** |
| **v1.0 Draft** | **2026-05-08** | **Formal system specification drafted based on v1.0-Final template** |
| **v1.0-Final** | **\[To be confirmed\]** | **Finalized OceanAI / Artibird System Specification after review and consistency alignment** |

## **中文表**

| **版本** | **日期** | **說明** |
|----|----|----|
| **v1.0** | **2026-05-08** | **建立 OceanAI / Artibird 系統規格書標準模板初始版本** |
| **v1.0-Final** | **2026-05-08** | **完成 OceanAI / Artibird 系統級文件的基礎系統規格書標準模板定稿** |
| **v1.0 Draft** | **2026-05-08** | **基於 v1.0-Final 模板撰寫正式系統規格書草案** |
| **v1.0-Final** | **\[待確認\]** | **經審查與一致性校準後，完成 OceanAI / Artibird 系統規格書定稿** |

## **19.4 Version Control Principle**

## **19.4 版本控制原則**

**EN  
Each version of this document must be assigned a clear version number.
Version changes should be used only when the document structure, system
definition, component relationship, runtime behavior, capacity boundary,
validation requirement, or claim boundary changes.**

**Minor wording corrections may be recorded without changing the major
version. Structural changes, new system capabilities, revised
architecture relationships, or updated validation boundaries should
trigger a new version or revision suffix.**

**ZH-TW  
本文件的每一個版本都必須分配清楚的版本號。只有當文件結構、系統定義、組件關係、Runtime
行為、容量邊界、驗證要求或宣稱邊界發生變化時，才應使用版本變更。**

**小幅文字修正可記錄而不改變主版本。結構變更、新系統能力、架構關係修訂或驗證邊界更新，應觸發新版本或修訂後綴。**

## **English Table**

| **Version Type** | **Usage** |
|----|----|
| **v1.0** | **Initial formal version** |
| **v1.0-Final** | **Finalized version after review** |
| **v1.0.1** | **Minor correction or clarification** |
| **v1.1** | **Structural improvement or extended system architecture version** |
| **v2.0** | **Major architecture, runtime, product, or platform change** |
| **R1 / R2** | **Review or revision sequence before final release** |
| **Draft** | **Working version before approval** |
| **Final** | **Approved reference version** |

## **中文表**

| **版本類型**   | **使用方式**                          |
|----------------|---------------------------------------|
| **v1.0**       | **初始正式版本**                      |
| **v1.0-Final** | **審查後定稿版本**                    |
| **v1.0.1**     | **小幅修正或澄清**                    |
| **v1.1**       | **結構優化或擴展系統架構版本**        |
| **v2.0**       | **重大架構、Runtime、產品或平台變更** |
| **R1 / R2**    | **定稿前審查或修訂序列**              |
| **Draft**      | **核准前工作版本**                    |
| **Final**      | **已核准參考版本**                    |

## **19.5 Change Record Requirement**

## **19.5 變更記錄要求**

**EN  
Any change to this document should be recorded in the revision history.
The change record should identify what changed, why it changed, which
sections were affected, and whether related product specifications,
commercial specifications, validation documents, or deployment documents
require updates.**

**ZH-TW  
本文件的任何變更都應記錄於版本記錄中。變更記錄應識別變更內容、變更原因、受影響章節，以及相關產品規格書、商業規格書、驗證文件或部署文件是否需要同步更新。**

## **English Table**

| **Change Record Item** | **Required Content** |
|----|----|
| **Version** | **Version number or revision suffix** |
| **Date** | **Date of revision** |
| **Changed Sections** | **Sections affected by the change** |
| **Change Type** | **Correction, clarification, addition, removal, restructuring, validation update** |
| **Reason** | **Reason for the change** |
| **Impact** | **Affected system behavior, product document, commercial claim, or validation item** |
| **Reviewer** | **Responsible reviewer or team where applicable** |
| **Approval Status** | **Draft, reviewed, approved, final** |

## **中文表**

| **變更記錄項目** | **必須內容**                                     |
|------------------|--------------------------------------------------|
| **版本**         | **版本號或修訂後綴**                             |
| **日期**         | **修訂日期**                                     |
| **變更章節**     | **受變更影響的章節**                             |
| **變更類型**     | **修正、澄清、新增、刪除、重構、驗證更新**       |
| **原因**         | **變更原因**                                     |
| **影響**         | **受影響系統行為、產品文件、商業宣稱或驗證項目** |
| **審查方**       | **適用時的責任審查方或團隊**                     |
| **核准狀態**     | **草案、已審查、已核准、最終版**                 |

## **19.6 Related Document Update Requirement**

## **19.6 關聯文件更新要求**

**EN  
When this system specification is updated, related documents should be
reviewed for consistency. Changes to system architecture, runtime
behavior, device model, connectivity, cloud participation, edge
participation, security, privacy, capacity, testing, or commercial claim
boundaries may require updates to product engineering specifications,
commercial specifications, product catalogs, website copy, installation
guides, training materials, or validation reports.**

**ZH-TW  
當本系統規格書更新時，應審查相關文件以保持一致性。若系統架構、Runtime
行為、設備模型、連接方式、雲端參與、Edge
參與、安全、隱私、容量、測試或商業宣稱邊界發生變更，可能需要同步更新產品工程規格書、商業規格書、產品型錄、網站文案、安裝指南、培訓材料或驗證報告。**

## **English Table**

| **Related Document** | **Update Trigger** |
|----|----|
| **Product Engineering Specifications** | **Product capability, hardware, firmware, connectivity, or capacity changes** |
| **Commercial Specifications** | **Positioning, claim, compatibility, cloud, AI, or deployment language changes** |
| **Product Catalog** | **Product role, feature, scenario, or compatibility changes** |
| **Website Copy** | **Public-facing system, product, or claim language changes** |
| **Installation Guides** | **Deployment, wiring, network, configuration, or safety behavior changes** |
| **Validation Reports** | **Capacity, reliability, security, privacy, or performance boundary changes** |
| **Channel Materials** | **Partner-facing positioning, supported scenario, or sales claim changes** |
| **Training Materials** | **Operational behavior, support process, or deployment guidance changes** |

## **中文表**

| **關聯文件**       | **更新觸發條件**                                 |
|--------------------|--------------------------------------------------|
| **產品工程規格書** | **產品能力、硬體、韌體、連接或容量變更**         |
| **商業規格書**     | **定位、宣稱、相容性、雲端、AI 或部署語言變更**  |
| **產品型錄**       | **產品角色、功能、場景或相容性變更**             |
| **網站文案**       | **對外系統、產品或宣稱語言變更**                 |
| **安裝指南**       | **部署、接線、網路、配置或安全行為變更**         |
| **驗證報告**       | **容量、可靠性、安全、隱私或性能邊界變更**       |
| **渠道材料**       | **面向合作夥伴的定位、受支援場景或銷售宣稱變更** |
| **培訓材料**       | **操作行為、支援流程或部署指引變更**             |

## **19.7 Approval Status**

## **19.7 核准狀態**

**EN  
Approval status defines whether a document version is still being
drafted, under review, approved for internal reference, or finalized as
the official system-level reference.**

**Only a finalized version should be used as the primary reference for
external commercial claims, formal product documents, partner documents,
or system deployment materials.**

**ZH-TW  
核准狀態定義某一文件版本是否仍在撰寫中、正在審查、已核准作為內部參考，或已定稿為正式系統級參考文件。**

**只有定稿版本應作為對外商業宣稱、正式產品文件、合作夥伴文件或系統部署材料的主要參考。**

## **English Table**

| **Approval Status** | **Description**                          |
|---------------------|------------------------------------------|
| **Draft**           | **Working version, not yet approved**    |
| **Review**          | **Under internal review**                |
| **Approved**        | **Approved for internal reference**      |
| **Final**           | **Finalized official reference version** |
| **Superseded**      | **Replaced by a newer version**          |
| **Archived**        | **Retained for historical record only**  |

## **中文表**

| **核准狀態**   | **說明**               |
|----------------|------------------------|
| **Draft**      | **工作版本，尚未核准** |
| **Review**     | **內部審查中**         |
| **Approved**   | **已核准作為內部參考** |
| **Final**      | **已定稿正式參考版本** |
| **Superseded** | **已被新版本取代**     |
| **Archived**   | **僅作為歷史記錄保留** |

## **19.8 Revision Boundary**

## **19.8 版本邊界**

**EN  
A revision history record does not automatically validate new system
behavior, product capability, cloud function, edge function, capacity
limit, security claim, privacy claim, deployment model, or commercial
claim.**

**Any revised content that introduces or changes system behavior must be
supported by appropriate validation evidence before it is used as an
external claim or implementation reference.**

**ZH-TW  
版本記錄本身不會自動驗證新的系統行為、產品能力、雲端功能、Edge
功能、容量限制、安全宣稱、隱私宣稱、部署模型或商業宣稱。**

**任何新增或修改系統行為的修訂內容，在被用作對外宣稱或實作參考之前，都必須具備適當驗證證據支持。**

## **19.9 Validation Requirements**

## **19.9 驗證要求**

**EN  
Any revision involving system architecture, runtime behavior, device
model, data and event flow, connectivity, cloud architecture, edge
intelligence, security, privacy, reliability, deployment, capacity,
testing, or commercial claim boundaries must be reviewed and validated
under defined conditions where applicable.**

**Validation should include the affected section, revised behavior,
required test evidence, affected products, affected deployment models,
affected commercial claims, and approval status.**

**ZH-TW  
任何涉及系統架構、Runtime
行為、設備模型、數據與事件流、連接、雲端架構、邊緣智慧、安全、隱私、可靠性、部署、容量、測試或商業宣稱邊界的修訂，都必須在適用條件下完成審查與驗證。**

**驗證應包含受影響章節、修訂後行為、所需測試證據、受影響產品、受影響部署模型、受影響商業宣稱與核准狀態。**

## **19.10 Chapter Conclusion**

## **19.10 章節結論**

**EN  
This chapter defines the revision history structure of the OceanAI /
Artibird System Specification. It explains how document versions, change
records, related document updates, approval status, revision boundaries,
and validation requirements should be managed to keep the system-level
reference accurate, traceable, and aligned with engineering and
commercial documentation.**

**ZH-TW  
本章定義了《OceanAI / Artibird
系統規格書》的版本記錄結構。它說明應如何管理文件版本、變更記錄、關聯文件更新、核准狀態、版本邊界與驗證要求，以保持系統級參考文件準確、可追溯，並與工程與商業文件保持一致。**

# **2. Preface**

# **2. 前言**

## **EN**

The OceanAI / Artibird System Specification v1.0 defines the
foundational system structure for the OceanAI / Artibird coordinated
intelligent environment system.

This document is not a product catalog, a marketing brochure, or a
single-device specification. It is a system-level reference document
that defines how OceanAI and Artibird components operate together across
architecture, runtime behavior, device participation, data flow,
connectivity, local-first operation, cloud enhancement, edge
intelligence, deployment, validation, and commercial claim boundaries.

OceanAI is defined in this document as the system-level coordinated
intelligence architecture. Artibird is defined as the physical product
and device layer that allows the architecture to take form within real
environments. ArtiOS provides the local runtime structure through which
devices, services, events, commands, scenes, automations, and system
states are processed.

The purpose of this specification is to establish a shared technical
foundation across product engineering, firmware development, backend
services, App design, cloud services, edge intelligence, testing,
certification, deployment planning, commercial documentation, and system
integration.

A coordinated intelligent environment cannot be defined only by
individual products. It must be defined by how components participate
together: how devices are discovered, how events move, how states are
maintained, how commands are routed, how local behavior continues, how
cloud services enhance operation, how edge intelligence assists
interpretation, and how all claims are validated under defined
conditions.

This document therefore serves as the baseline system-level reference
above individual Artibird product engineering specifications. Product
specifications define what each product is. This system specification
defines how the products operate together within the OceanAI / Artibird
system.

All future product documents, commercial specifications, deployment
plans, validation reports, website descriptions, channel materials, and
claim language should remain aligned with the boundaries and validation
principles defined in this document.

## **ZH-TW**

《OceanAI / Artibird 系統規格書 v1.0》定義 OceanAI / Artibird
協同智慧空間系統的基礎系統結構。

本文件不是產品型錄、行銷手冊，也不是單一設備規格書。它是一份系統級參考文件，用於定義
OceanAI 與 Artibird 組件如何在系統架構、Runtime
行為、設備參與、數據流、連接方式、本地優先運作、雲端增強、邊緣智慧、部署、驗證與商業宣稱邊界中共同運作。

在本文件中，OceanAI 被定義為系統級協同智慧架構。Artibird
被定義為使該架構能夠在真實環境中成形的實體產品與設備層。ArtiOS
則提供本地 Runtime
結構，用於處理設備、服務、事件、指令、場景、自動化與系統狀態。

本規格書的目的，是在產品工程、韌體開發、後端服務、App
設計、雲端服務、邊緣智慧、測試、認證、部署規劃、商業文件與系統整合之間，建立共同的技術基準。

一個協同智慧空間不能只由單一產品來定義，而必須由各組件如何共同參與來定義：設備如何被發現，事件如何流動，狀態如何維護，指令如何路由，本地行為如何延續，雲端服務如何增強運作，邊緣智慧如何輔助解讀，以及所有宣稱如何在明確條件下完成驗證。

因此，本文件作為高於各個 Artibird
單品工程規格書之上的基礎系統級參考文件。產品規格書定義每個產品是什麼；本系統規格書定義這些產品如何在
OceanAI / Artibird 系統中共同運作。

未來所有產品文件、商業規格書、部署方案、驗證報告、網站描述、渠道材料與宣稱語言，都應與本文件所定義的邊界與驗證原則保持一致。

# **3. Document Purpose**

# **3. 文件目的**

## **EN**

This document defines the baseline system architecture, runtime
behavior, component relationships, device model, data and event flow,
connectivity structure, local-first operation, cloud-enhanced
capabilities, edge intelligence participation, security and privacy
requirements, reliability behavior, deployment models, capacity
boundaries, testing requirements, commercial claim boundaries, revision
control, terminology, product-system mapping, validation checklist, and
deployment reference models of the OceanAI / Artibird system.

It is intended to serve as the master system-level reference for all
related engineering, product, commercial, validation, deployment, and
documentation work.

## **ZH-TW**

本文件定義 OceanAI / Artibird 系統的基礎系統架構、Runtime
行為、組件關係、設備模型、數據與事件流、連接結構、本地優先運作、雲端增強能力、邊緣智慧參與、安全與隱私要求、可靠性行為、部署模型、容量邊界、測試要求、商業宣稱邊界、版本控制、術語、產品—系統映射、驗證清單與部署參考模型。

本文件旨在作為所有相關工程、產品、商業、驗證、部署與文件工作的最高層級系統參考。

## **English Table**

| **Purpose Area** | **Description** |
|----|----|
| System Architecture | Define the layered structure of OceanAI / Artibird |
| Runtime Behavior | Define how the system operates during active use |
| Component Relationship | Define how Cloud, Edge, Hub, Gate, App, and Artibird devices relate |
| Device Model | Define how supported devices are represented in the system |
| Data and Event Flow | Define how events, commands, states, telemetry, and synchronization data move |
| Connectivity | Define supported networking paths and communication boundaries |
| Local-First Operation | Define what can operate locally when required local components are present |
| Cloud Enhancement | Define how OceanAI Cloud extends remote access, sync, lifecycle, and analytics |
| Edge Intelligence | Define how OceanAI Edge provides AI-assisted interpretation where deployed |
| Security and Privacy | Define security, access, data, privacy, and control boundaries |
| Reliability | Define failure, degraded, offline, and recovery behavior |
| Deployment | Define supported deployment models and planning requirements |
| Capacity | Define measurable system limits and validation requirements |
| Testing and Validation | Define test categories and required validation evidence |
| Commercial Claim Control | Prevent unsupported overclaims and align commercial language with engineering evidence |

## **中文表**

| **目的領域** | **說明** |
|----|----|
| 系統架構 | 定義 OceanAI / Artibird 的分層結構 |
| Runtime 行為 | 定義系統在實際運行期間如何工作 |
| 組件關係 | 定義 Cloud、Edge、Hub、Gate、App 與 Artibird 設備之間的關係 |
| 設備模型 | 定義受支援設備在系統中如何表示 |
| 數據與事件流 | 定義事件、指令、狀態、遙測與同步數據如何流動 |
| 連接方式 | 定義受支援網路路徑與通訊邊界 |
| 本地優先運作 | 定義所需本地元件具備時哪些功能可本地運作 |
| 雲端增強 | 定義 OceanAI Cloud 如何擴展遠端存取、同步、生命週期與分析能力 |
| 邊緣智慧 | 定義 OceanAI Edge 如何在部署條件下提供 AI 輔助解讀 |
| 安全與隱私 | 定義安全、存取、數據、隱私與控制邊界 |
| 可靠性 | 定義故障、降級、離線與恢復行為 |
| 部署 | 定義受支援部署模型與規劃要求 |
| 容量 | 定義可量測系統限制與驗證要求 |
| 測試與驗證 | 定義測試類別與所需驗證證據 |
| 商業宣稱管控 | 防止未支援過度宣稱，並使商業語言與工程證據對齊 |

# **4. Document Scope**

# **4. 文件範圍**

## **EN**

This document applies to the OceanAI / Artibird coordinated intelligent
environment system and its supported system components.

It defines system-level structure and behavior. It does not replace
individual product engineering specifications, certification documents,
installation manuals, privacy policies, commercial product catalogs, or
validation reports. Instead, it provides the system-level foundation
that those documents should reference.

## **ZH-TW**

本文件適用於 OceanAI / Artibird 協同智慧空間系統及其受支援系統組件。

本文件定義系統級結構與行為。它不取代各單品工程規格書、認證文件、安裝手冊、隱私政策、商業產品型錄或驗證報告，而是為這些文件提供應共同參照的系統級基礎。

## **English Table**

| **In Scope** | **Out of Scope / Boundary** |
|----|----|
| OceanAI / Artibird system architecture | Detailed PCB design for each device |
| ArtiOS runtime behavior | Full firmware implementation details |
| Component roles and relationships | Manufacturing process documents |
| Product-system mapping | Certification reports themselves |
| Local, cloud, and edge participation | Legal privacy policy text |
| Data and event flow | Final commercial brochure copy |
| Connectivity and capacity boundaries | Unvalidated third-party platform support |
| Deployment reference models | Project-specific construction drawings |
| Validation checklist | Actual test report data unless separately produced |
| Commercial claim boundaries | Unsupported marketing claims |

## **中文表**

| **包含範圍**                | **不包含 / 邊界**                        |
|-----------------------------|------------------------------------------|
| OceanAI / Artibird 系統架構 | 各設備詳細 PCB 設計                      |
| ArtiOS Runtime 行為         | 完整韌體實作細節                         |
| 組件角色與關係              | 製造流程文件                             |
| 產品—系統映射               | 認證報告本身                             |
| 本地、雲端與 Edge 參與      | 法律版隱私政策文本                       |
| 數據與事件流                | 最終商業宣傳冊文案                       |
| 連接與容量邊界              | 未驗證第三方平台支援                     |
| 部署參考模型                | 項目專用施工圖                           |
| 驗證清單                    | 除非另行產出，否則不包含實際測試報告數據 |
| 商業宣稱邊界                | 未支援行銷宣稱                           |

# **5. Intended Audience**

# **5. 適用對象**

## **EN**

This document is intended for internal and partner-facing teams that
need to understand, design, develop, validate, deploy, describe, or
support the OceanAI / Artibird system.

## **ZH-TW**

本文件適用於需要理解、設計、開發、驗證、部署、描述或支援 OceanAI /
Artibird 系統的內部團隊與合作夥伴團隊。

## **English Table**

| **Audience** | **Intended Use** |
|----|----|
| Architecture Team | Define and maintain system architecture and component relationships |
| Product Team | Align product definitions with system roles and system boundaries |
| Firmware Team | Develop device behavior according to runtime, connectivity, and validation requirements |
| Backend Team | Align cloud services with system architecture and data flow |
| App Team | Align setup, control, state display, local access, and remote access behavior |
| Edge / AI Team | Align Edge-assisted interpretation with runtime, privacy, and validation boundaries |
| Testing Team | Use system-level test categories and validation checklist |
| Certification Team | Understand safety, certification, security, and claim boundaries |
| Commercial Team | Align sales language, product catalogs, and commercial claims |
| Channel Partners | Understand supported deployment models and product-system mapping |
| System Integrators | Plan deployments according to component roles, capacity, and validation requirements |
| Support Team | Understand expected behavior, failure behavior, and recovery boundaries |

## **中文表**

| **適用對象**   | **預期用途**                                     |
|----------------|--------------------------------------------------|
| 架構團隊       | 定義與維護系統架構及組件關係                     |
| 產品團隊       | 使產品定義與系統角色及系統邊界對齊               |
| 韌體團隊       | 依 Runtime、連接與驗證要求開發設備行為           |
| 後端團隊       | 使雲端服務與系統架構及數據流對齊                 |
| App 團隊       | 對齊設定、控制、狀態顯示、本地存取與遠端存取行為 |
| Edge / AI 團隊 | 使 Edge 輔助解讀與 Runtime、隱私與驗證邊界對齊   |
| 測試團隊       | 使用系統級測試類別與驗證清單                     |
| 認證團隊       | 理解安全、認證、資安與宣稱邊界                   |
| 商業團隊       | 對齊銷售語言、產品型錄與商業宣稱                 |
| 渠道合作夥伴   | 理解受支援部署模型與產品—系統映射                |
| 系統整合商     | 依組件角色、容量與驗證要求規劃部署               |
| 支援團隊       | 理解預期行為、故障行為與恢復邊界                 |

# **6. How to Use This Document**

# **6. 如何使用本文件**

## **EN**

This document should be used as the primary system-level reference
before creating, updating, or reviewing related product, engineering,
commercial, deployment, validation, or support documents.

Product engineering specifications should use this document to align
product roles, runtime participation, device model, connectivity,
capacity, and validation requirements.

Commercial specifications, product catalogs, websites, and channel
materials should use this document to avoid unsupported claims and
ensure that product language remains aligned with engineering evidence.

Deployment plans should use this document to identify required
components, system layers, local runtime needs, cloud requirements, edge
requirements, capacity boundaries, security requirements, privacy
requirements, and validation requirements.

Testing and validation work should use Chapter 17 and Appendix C as the
baseline reference for test categories, validation evidence, and
acceptance logic.

## **ZH-TW**

在建立、更新或審查相關產品、工程、商業、部署、驗證或支援文件之前，本文件應作為主要系統級參考。

產品工程規格書應使用本文件來對齊產品角色、Runtime
參與、設備模型、連接方式、容量與驗證要求。

商業規格書、產品型錄、網站與渠道材料應使用本文件來避免未支援宣稱，並確保產品語言與工程證據保持一致。

部署方案應使用本文件來識別所需組件、系統層級、本地 Runtime
需求、雲端要求、Edge 要求、容量邊界、安全要求、隱私要求與驗證要求。

測試與驗證工作應使用 Chapter 17 與 Appendix C
作為測試類別、驗證證據與驗收邏輯的基礎參考。
