# **7. Document Hierarchy**

# **7. 文件層級**

## **EN**

This system specification sits above individual product engineering
specifications and commercial specifications. It defines the
system-level logic that all downstream documents should reference.

## **ZH-TW**

本系統規格書位於各單品工程規格書與商業規格書之上。它定義所有下游文件應共同參照的系統級邏輯。

## **English Table**

| **Document Level** | **Document Type** | **Role** |
|----|----|----|
| Level 1 | OceanAI / Artibird System Specification | Defines system architecture, runtime, integration, capacity, validation, and claim boundaries |
| Level 2 | Product Engineering Specifications | Define product-level hardware, firmware, software, connectivity, and engineering behavior |
| Level 3 | Commercial Specifications | Define customer-facing product positioning, benefits, use cases, and channel language |
| Level 4 | Product Catalogs | Present product family, product roles, scenarios, and simplified product information |
| Level 5 | Deployment Plans | Define project-specific installation, network, component placement, and validation scope |
| Level 6 | Test and Validation Reports | Provide evidence for claims, capacity, reliability, security, privacy, and deployment behavior |
| Level 7 | Website / Channel / Sales Materials | Communicate validated system and product value externally |

## **中文表**

| **文件層級** | **文件類型** | **角色** |
|----|----|----|
| Level 1 | OceanAI / Artibird 系統規格書 | 定義系統架構、Runtime、整合、容量、驗證與宣稱邊界 |
| Level 2 | 產品工程規格書 | 定義產品級硬體、韌體、軟體、連接與工程行為 |
| Level 3 | 商業規格書 | 定義面向客戶的產品定位、收益、使用場景與渠道語言 |
| Level 4 | 產品型錄 | 呈現產品家族、產品角色、場景與簡化產品資訊 |
| Level 5 | 部署方案 | 定義項目專用安裝、網路、組件佈置與驗證範圍 |
| Level 6 | 測試與驗證報告 | 為宣稱、容量、可靠性、安全、隱私與部署行為提供證據 |
| Level 7 | 網站 / 渠道 / 銷售材料 | 對外傳達已驗證系統與產品價值 |

# **9. 前置文件完成聲明**

## **EN**

This Front Matter Package v1.0 completes the introductory structure of
the OceanAI / Artibird System Specification v1.0.

Together with Chapter 1–19, Appendix A–D, and Document End, it forms a
complete system-level specification structure suitable for internal
reference, product alignment, engineering planning, deployment

## **ZH-TW**

本《前置文件套件 v1.0》完成了《OceanAI / Artibird 系統規格書
v1.0》的導入結構。

它與 Chapter 1–19、Appendix A–D 以及 Document End
共同構成一份完整的系統級規格書結構，可用於內部參考、產品對齊、工程規劃、部署準備、驗證規劃與商業宣稱管控。

附錄

按照你確認的 **《OceanAI / Artibird System Specification Template
v1.0-Final》**，正式章節到：

**19. Revision History｜19. 版本記錄**

之後不再有 **第 20 章**。

接下來應進入附錄：

# **Appendix A — Terminology**

# **Appendix A — 術語表**

也就是說，正確順序是：

| **順序**     | **章節**                                         |
|--------------|--------------------------------------------------|
| 1–19         | 正文章節                                         |
| Appendix A   | Terminology｜術語表                              |
| Appendix B   | Product-System Mapping Matrix｜產品—系統映射矩陣 |
| Appendix C   | System Validation Checklist｜系統驗證清單        |
| Appendix D   | Deployment Reference Models｜部署參考模型        |
| Document End | 文件結束                                         |

所以，為了不偏離 v1.0-Final，不應新增「第 20 章」。

下一步應寫：

**Appendix A — Terminology  
Appendix A — 術語表**

A — 術語表

# **A — 術語表**

# **Appendix A — Terminology**

# **Appendix A — 術語表**

## **A.1 Purpose**

## **A.1 目的**

**EN  
**This appendix defines key terminology used in the OceanAI / Artibird
System Specification. It provides a shared vocabulary for architecture,
product, firmware, backend, App, testing, certification, commercial, and
system integration teams.

**ZH-TW  
**本附錄定義《OceanAI / Artibird
系統規格書》中使用的核心術語。它為架構、產品、韌體、後端、App、測試、認證、商業與系統整合團隊提供一致的共用詞彙。

## **A.2 Terminology Table**

## **A.2 術語表**

## **English Table**

| **Term** | **Definition** |
|----|----|
| OceanAI | System-level coordinated intelligence architecture |
| Artibird | Product and physical device layer of the OceanAI system |
| ArtiOS | Local runtime platform for coordination, state, scenes, automation, and local services |
| Hub | Local runtime center |
| Gate | Device access gateway |
| Sync | IR / RF appliance synchronization node |
| Switch | Smart switch, event node, and relay-control variant family |
| Panel | Room-level control and interaction interface |
| Act | Electrical execution node |
| Sense | Environmental sensing and context node |
| Vision | Visual context and AI vision node |
| Cloud | Remote management, synchronization, account, and lifecycle services |
| Edge | Local AI-assisted intelligence and perception layer |
| Runtime | Active system operation layer where events, commands, state, and automation are processed |

## **中文表**

| **術語** | **定義**                                                  |
|----------|-----------------------------------------------------------|
| OceanAI  | 系統級協同智慧架構                                        |
| Artibird | OceanAI 系統中的產品與實體設備層                          |
| ArtiOS   | 用於協同、狀態、場景、自動化與本地服務的本地 Runtime 平台 |
| Hub      | 本地 Runtime 中心                                         |
| Gate     | 設備接入網關                                              |
| Sync     | IR / RF 家電同步節點                                      |
| Switch   | 智慧開關、事件節點與繼電器控制版本家族                    |
| Panel    | 房間級控制與互動介面                                      |
| Act      | 電力執行節點                                              |
| Sense    | 環境感知與上下文節點                                      |
| Vision   | 視覺上下文與 AI 視覺節點                                  |
| Cloud    | 遠端管理、同步、帳號與生命週期服務                        |
| Edge     | 本地 AI 輔助智慧與感知層                                  |
| Runtime  | 處理事件、指令、狀態與自動化的系統運行層                  |

## **A.3 System and Architecture Terms**

## **A.3 系統與架構術語**

## **English Table**

| **Term** | **Definition** |
|----|----|
| Coordinated Intelligent Environment | A supported physical environment where devices, runtime services, cloud services, edge intelligence, sensing, execution, and user interfaces operate as one coordinated system |
| System Architecture | The layered structure defining how cloud, edge, local runtime, device access, interaction, sensing, execution, and device layers relate to each other |
| System Layer | The architecture-level layer responsible for defining how components operate together |
| Product Layer | The physical device and product family layer represented by Artibird products |
| Local-First | A system operating principle where supported core local functions can operate when required local components are present |
| Cloud-Enhanced | A system model where cloud services extend remote access, synchronization, lifecycle management, analytics, and multi-site support |
| Edge-Assisted | A system model where local AI inference or interpretation supports runtime behavior under defined conditions |
| Runtime Participation | The way a component contributes to events, state, commands, automation, scenes, execution, sensing, or synchronization during system operation |
| System Boundary | The defined limit of supported system behavior under validated conditions |
| Engineering Boundary | The technical limit of what the system supports under defined hardware, firmware, software, network, and deployment conditions |

## **中文表**

| **術語** | **定義** |
|----|----|
| 協同智慧空間 | 受支援實體環境中，設備、Runtime 服務、雲端服務、邊緣智慧、感知、執行與用戶介面作為一個協同系統共同運作的空間 |
| 系統架構 | 定義雲端、邊緣、本地 Runtime、設備接入、互動、感知、執行與設備層之間關係的分層結構 |
| 系統層 | 負責定義各組件如何共同運作的架構級層級 |
| 產品層 | 由 Artibird 產品代表的實體設備與產品家族層 |
| 本地優先 | 當所需本地元件具備時，受支援核心本地功能可運作的系統運作原則 |
| 雲端增強 | 由雲端服務擴展遠端存取、同步、生命週期管理、分析與多站點支援的系統模型 |
| Edge 輔助 | 在明確條件下，由本地 AI 推理或解讀支援 Runtime 行為的系統模型 |
| Runtime 參與 | 組件在系統運行期間，對事件、狀態、指令、自動化、場景、執行、感知或同步所作的貢獻方式 |
| 系統邊界 | 在已驗證條件下，受支援系統行為的明確限制 |
| 工程邊界 | 系統在明確硬體、韌體、軟體、網路與部署條件下可支援能力的技術限制 |

## **A.4 Component Terms**

## **A.4 組件術語**

## **English Table**

| **Term** | **Definition** |
|----|----|
| OceanAI Cloud | Cloud service layer providing remote access, synchronization, account services, lifecycle services, alerts, analytics, and multi-site support where supported |
| OceanAI Edge | Local AI-assisted intelligence layer, typically based on deployed edge hardware, providing local inference, vision analysis, sensor fusion, and optimization where supported |
| Artibird Hub | Local runtime center hosting local services, MQTT broker, state management, automation, web services, and ArtiOS modules |
| Artibird Gate | ESP32-C6-based device access gateway providing supported device onboarding, local communication, network participation, and gateway communication |
| Artibird Sync | Appliance synchronization node providing supported IR / RF control and synchronization for selected appliances |
| Artibird Switch | Interaction and event node providing touch events, scene triggers, and relay control depending on product variant |
| Artibird Panel | Room-level interface for scene control, device group interaction, status display, and shared user interaction |
| Artibird Act | Electrical execution node providing relay control, plug control, load control, and optional energy measurement depending on product variant |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental context node providing temperature, humidity, light, occupancy, and related environmental signals where supported |
| Artibird Vision | Visual perception node providing visual events, local recording, security awareness, and AI-assisted visual context where supported |
| Artibird App | User access interface for setup, configuration, local control, remote control, device management, scene management, and automation configuration |

## **中文表**

| **術語** | **定義** |
|----|----|
| OceanAI Cloud | 雲端服務層，在支援條件下提供遠端存取、同步、帳號服務、生命週期服務、警報、分析與多站點支援 |
| OceanAI Edge | 本地 AI 輔助智慧層，通常基於已部署邊緣硬體，在支援條件下提供本地推理、視覺分析、感測融合與優化 |
| Artibird Hub | 本地 Runtime 中心，承載本地服務、MQTT Broker、狀態管理、自動化、Web 服務與 ArtiOS 模組 |
| Artibird Gate | 基於 ESP32-C6 的設備接入網關，提供受支援設備入網、本地通訊、網路參與與網關通訊 |
| Artibird Sync | 家電同步節點，為特定受支援家電提供 IR / RF 控制與同步 |
| Artibird Switch | 互動與事件節點，依產品版本提供觸控事件、場景觸發與繼電器控制 |
| Artibird Panel | 房間級介面，用於場景控制、設備群組互動、狀態顯示與共享用戶互動 |
| Artibird Act | 電力執行節點，依產品版本提供繼電器控制、插座控制、負載控制與可選電能計量 |
| Artibird Sense | 環境上下文節點，在支援條件下提供溫度、濕度、光照、人在與相關環境信號 |
| Artibird Vision | 視覺感知節點，在支援條件下提供視覺事件、本地錄影、安全感知與 AI 輔助視覺上下文 |
| Artibird App | 用戶存取介面，用於設定、配置、本地控制、遠端控制、設備管理、場景管理與自動化配置 |

## **A.5 Runtime and Data Terms**

## **A.5 Runtime 與數據術語**

## **English Table**

| **Term** | **Definition** |
|----|----|
| Event | A system signal generated by a device, user action, sensor, Vision node, cloud service, Edge service, or runtime service |
| Command | An instruction sent from App, Panel, Switch, Cloud, automation, scene, Edge, or runtime service to a target component or device |
| State | The current condition, value, status, or operating result of a device, room, scene, automation, service, or system component |
| Telemetry | Reported device, sensor, execution, network, energy, or diagnostic data used for monitoring, automation, or analysis |
| Scene | A predefined multi-device behavior executed by the runtime system |
| Automation | Conditional runtime logic based on time, sensor values, events, state changes, user configuration, cloud input, or Edge-assisted interpretation |
| Device Model | The structured representation of a supported device within the system |
| Device ID | Unique device identifier used by local runtime, cloud services, App interfaces, logs, and validation records |
| Capability | The supported functions of a device under defined product, firmware, hardware, connectivity, and validation conditions |
| Health Status | The operating condition of a device or system component, such as online, offline, degraded, error, updating, unbound, or disabled |
| Last Seen | The most recent communication timestamp between a device and the system |
| Sync Flow | The movement of selected state, configuration, lifecycle data, logs, historical records, or account information between Hub and Cloud |

## **中文表**

| **術語** | **定義** |
|----|----|
| 事件 | 由設備、用戶動作、感測器、Vision 節點、雲端服務、Edge 服務或 Runtime 服務產生的系統信號 |
| 指令 | 從 App、Panel、Switch、Cloud、自動化、場景、Edge 或 Runtime 服務發送至目標組件或設備的操作指令 |
| 狀態 | 設備、房間、場景、自動化、服務或系統組件的當前條件、數值、狀態或運作結果 |
| 遙測數據 | 用於監測、自動化或分析的設備、感測、執行、網路、能源或診斷上報數據 |
| 場景 | 由 Runtime 系統執行的預定義多設備行為 |
| 自動化 | 基於時間、感測值、事件、狀態變化、用戶配置、雲端輸入或 Edge 輔助解讀的條件 Runtime 邏輯 |
| 設備模型 | 受支援設備在系統中的結構化表示方式 |
| Device ID | 本地 Runtime、雲端服務、App 介面、日誌與驗證記錄使用的唯一設備識別碼 |
| 設備能力 | 設備在明確產品、韌體、硬體、連接與驗證條件下受支援的功能 |
| 健康狀態 | 設備或系統組件的運行條件，例如在線、離線、降級、錯誤、更新中、未綁定或已停用 |
| 最近通訊時間 | 設備與系統之間最近一次通訊時間戳 |
| 同步流 | 特定狀態、配置、生命週期數據、日誌、歷史記錄或帳號資訊在 Hub 與 Cloud 之間的流動 |

## **A.6 Connectivity Terms**

## **A.6 連接術語**

## **English Table**

| **Term** | **Definition** |
|----|----|
| Ethernet | Wired network connection used by supported components such as Hub, Gate, or Vision depending on product variant |
| Wi-Fi | Wireless local network connection used by supported devices and system components |
| BLE Mesh | Bluetooth Low Energy mesh communication used by supported low-power or event-node devices where implemented |
| Wi-Fi Mesh | Wi-Fi mesh communication supported only where implemented and validated |
| Local MQTT | MQTT-based local messaging structure hosted by Hub or related runtime services where implemented |
| MQTT Broker | The messaging service responsible for receiving, routing, and distributing MQTT messages |
| Topic | MQTT message address or naming path used for device, room, state, command, event, or system messages |
| Gateway Communication | Communication behavior in which Gate passes supported device events and commands between devices and Hub / ArtiOS |
| App Local Connection | Artibird App connection to the local system through supported local network paths |
| Cloud Connection | Communication path between supported local components and OceanAI Cloud |
| Offline Mode | Operating condition where Internet or cloud access is unavailable but supported local functions may continue when required local components are present |
| Max Concurrent Device Connections | Total number of supported active devices that may participate in the system at the same time under validated conditions |

## **中文表**

| **術語** | **定義** |
|----|----|
| Ethernet | 依產品版本由 Hub、Gate 或 Vision 等受支援組件使用的有線網路連接 |
| Wi-Fi | 受支援設備與系統組件使用的無線本地網路連接 |
| BLE Mesh | 在已實作條件下，由受支援低功耗或事件節點設備使用的 Bluetooth Low Energy Mesh 通訊 |
| Wi-Fi Mesh | 僅在已實作並驗證條件下支援的 Wi-Fi Mesh 通訊 |
| 本地 MQTT | 在已實作條件下，由 Hub 或相關 Runtime 服務承載的 MQTT 本地消息結構 |
| MQTT Broker | 負責接收、路由與分發 MQTT 消息的消息服務 |
| Topic | MQTT 消息地址或命名路徑，用於設備、房間、狀態、指令、事件或系統消息 |
| 網關通訊 | Gate 在設備與 Hub / ArtiOS 之間傳遞受支援設備事件與指令的通訊行為 |
| App 本地連接 | Artibird App 透過受支援本地網路路徑連接至本地系統 |
| 雲端連接 | 受支援本地組件與 OceanAI Cloud 之間的通訊路徑 |
| 離線模式 | Internet 或雲端存取不可用時，所需本地元件具備條件下受支援本地功能可繼續的運作狀態 |
| 最大併發設備連接數 | 在已驗證條件下，可同時參與系統的受支援活躍設備總數 |

## **A.7 Security and Privacy Terms**

## **A.7 安全與隱私術語**

## **English Table**

| **Term** | **Definition** |
|----|----|
| Device Identity | The unique identity and authentication basis of a supported device within the system |
| Account Binding | The secure association between a device and a user account, site, room, organization, or deployment |
| Local Access Control | Permission control for local users, devices, App interfaces, Panels, Switches, Hub services, Gate services, and runtime components |
| Remote Access Control | Permission control for users accessing supported devices, rooms, scenes, automations, sites, or cloud services outside the local environment |
| Role-Based Access Control | Access model defining what owners, admins, users, installers, guests, or organization-level roles may view, configure, control, or manage |
| Secure MQTT | MQTT communication protected by authentication, permission, encryption where implemented, message validation, and failure handling |
| Firmware Update Security | Security behavior protecting firmware updates from unauthorized modification, invalid installation, incompatible versions, or interrupted updates |
| Data Retention | Policy defining what data is stored, where it is stored, how long it is retained, who may access it, and how it may be deleted |
| Vision Data Privacy | Privacy behavior defining how Vision data is recorded, processed, accessed, stored, synchronized, retained, or deleted |
| Edge Processing Boundary | The defined limit of what data OceanAI Edge may process locally, what may remain local, and what may synchronize with cloud |
| Audit Logs | Records of security-sensitive, access-related, configuration-related, lifecycle-related, or failure-related system events |

## **中文表**

| **術語** | **定義** |
|----|----|
| 設備身份 | 受支援設備在系統中的唯一身份與身份認證基礎 |
| 帳號綁定 | 設備與用戶帳號、站點、房間、組織或部署之間的安全關聯 |
| 本地存取控制 | 對本地用戶、設備、App 介面、Panel、Switch、Hub 服務、Gate 服務與 Runtime 組件的權限控制 |
| 遠端存取控制 | 對本地環境之外存取受支援設備、房間、場景、自動化、站點或雲端服務的用戶進行權限控制 |
| 角色權限控制 | 定義 Owner、Admin、User、Installer、Guest 或組織級角色可查看、配置、控制或管理內容的存取模型 |
| 安全 MQTT | 透過身份認證、權限、已實作條件下加密、消息驗證與故障處理保護的 MQTT 通訊 |
| 韌體更新安全 | 防止韌體更新遭未授權修改、無效安裝、版本不相容或更新中斷的安全行為 |
| 數據保留 | 定義哪些數據被儲存、儲存在何處、保留多久、誰可存取以及如何刪除的政策 |
| Vision 數據隱私 | 定義 Vision 數據如何被錄製、處理、存取、儲存、同步、保留或刪除的隱私行為 |
| Edge 處理邊界 | 定義 OceanAI Edge 可在本地處理哪些數據、哪些數據保留本地、哪些數據可與雲端同步的限制 |
| 審計日誌 | 安全敏感、存取相關、配置相關、生命週期相關或故障相關系統事件的記錄 |

## **A.8 Validation and Claim Terms**

## **A.8 驗證與宣稱術語**

## **English Table**

| **Term** | **Definition** |
|----|----|
| Validation | Evidence-based confirmation that a system function, capacity, behavior, claim, or boundary is supported under defined conditions |
| Test Evidence | Recorded proof such as logs, screenshots, measurements, reports, videos, or test records supporting a system claim |
| Capacity Claim | A claim involving device count, throughput, latency, scene count, automation count, Vision stream count, Edge processing load, or other measurable system limits |
| Commercial Claim | Customer-facing statement used in commercial specifications, product catalogs, websites, Amazon listings, channel materials, sales presentations, or partner documents |
| Claim Boundary | Defined language and condition preventing unsupported overclaims |
| Certification Claim | Statement involving certification status such as UL, ETL, FCC, CE, or other regulatory / compliance status |
| Deployment Model | Defined installation and operation scenario for a supported environment such as home, classroom, office, building, campus, energy, security, agriculture, or infrastructure |
| Degraded Operation | Partial system operation when one or more components, services, or communication paths are unavailable or limited |
| Recovery Behavior | How the system returns from failure or degraded condition to supported operation |
| Failure Behavior | Defined system behavior when cloud, Internet, Hub, Gate, device, Edge, App, power, or network condition becomes unavailable or degraded |

## **中文表**

| **術語** | **定義** |
|----|----|
| 驗證 | 以證據確認某一系統功能、容量、行為、宣稱或邊界在明確條件下受支援 |
| 測試證據 | 用於支持系統宣稱的記錄證據，例如日誌、截圖、量測數據、報告、視頻或測試記錄 |
| 容量宣稱 | 涉及設備數、吞吐量、延遲、場景數、自動化數、Vision 視頻流數、Edge 處理負載或其他可量測系統限制的宣稱 |
| 商業宣稱 | 用於商業規格書、產品型錄、網站、Amazon 上架文案、渠道材料、銷售簡報或合作夥伴文件中的面向客戶表述 |
| 宣稱邊界 | 用於防止未支援過度宣稱的已定義語言與條件 |
| 認證宣稱 | 涉及 UL、ETL、FCC、CE 或其他法規 / 合規狀態的認證狀態表述 |
| 部署模型 | 面向住宅、教室、辦公、建築、校園、能源、安全、農業或基礎設施等受支援環境的已定義安裝與運作場景 |
| 降級運作 | 當一個或多個組件、服務或通訊路徑不可用或受限時，系統仍保持部分功能可用 |
| 恢復行為 | 系統如何從故障或降級狀態返回受支援運作 |
| 故障行為 | 當雲端、Internet、Hub、Gate、設備、Edge、App、電力或網路條件不可用或降級時的已定義系統行為 |

## **A.9 Appendix Conclusion**

## **A.9 附錄結論**

**EN  
**This appendix defines the core terminology used in the OceanAI /
Artibird System Specification. These terms should be used consistently
across system specifications, product engineering specifications,
commercial specifications, deployment documents, validation documents,
product catalogs, websites, channel materials, and training materials.

**ZH-TW  
**本附錄定義了《OceanAI / Artibird
系統規格書》中使用的核心術語。這些術語應在系統規格書、產品工程規格書、商業規格書、部署文件、驗證文件、產品型錄、網站、渠道材料與培訓材料中保持一致。

B — 產品—系統映射矩陣

# **B — 產品—系統映射矩陣**

# **Appendix B — Product-System Mapping Matrix**

# **Appendix B — 產品—系統映射矩陣**

## **B.1 Purpose**

## **B.1 目的**

**EN  
**This appendix defines how OceanAI and Artibird components map to
system layers, runtime responsibilities, primary functions, and
supported participation within the OceanAI / Artibird system.

**ZH-TW  
**本附錄定義 OceanAI 與 Artibird 組件如何對應至系統層級、Runtime
責任、主要功能，以及在 OceanAI / Artibird 系統中的受支援參與方式。

## **B.2 Product-System Mapping Definition**

## **B.2 產品—系統映射定義**

**EN  
**Product-System Mapping defines the relationship between each product
or platform component and its role within the overall system
architecture.

This mapping is used to prevent confusion between system architecture,
runtime services, device access, interaction, sensing, execution, cloud
services, edge intelligence, and user-facing product functions.

Each mapped component must be described according to its supported
system layer, primary function, runtime participation, dependency
boundary, and validation condition.

**ZH-TW  
**產品—系統映射定義每個產品或平台組件與整體系統架構中角色之間的關係。

此映射用於避免系統架構、Runtime
服務、設備接入、互動、感知、執行、雲端服務、邊緣智慧與面向用戶產品功能之間的混淆。

每個被映射的組件都必須依其受支援系統層級、主要功能、Runtime
參與方式、依賴邊界與驗證條件進行描述。

## **B.3 Product-System Mapping Matrix**

## **B.3 產品—系統映射矩陣**

## **English Table**

| **Product** | **System Layer** | **Primary Function** |
|----|----|----|
| Hub | Local Runtime Layer | Local coordination, services, state, automation |
| Gate | Device Access Layer | Device onboarding and gateway communication |
| Sync | Execution / Synchronization Layer | IR / RF appliance synchronization |
| Switch | Interaction / Execution Layer | Touch input, scene trigger, relay control by variant |
| Panel | Interaction Layer | Room interface and shared control |
| Act | Execution Layer | Electrical execution and optional energy data |
| Sense | Sensing Layer | Environmental context |
| Vision | Sensing / Edge Context Layer | Visual context and event awareness |
| Cloud | Cloud Layer | Remote access, sync, lifecycle |
| Edge | Edge Intelligence Layer | AI-assisted perception and optimization |
| App | Interaction / Cloud Access Layer | User control, setup, remote access |

## **中文表**

| **產品** | **系統層級**         | **主要功能**                             |
|----------|----------------------|------------------------------------------|
| Hub      | 本地 Runtime 層      | 本地協同、服務、狀態、自動化             |
| Gate     | 設備接入層           | 設備入網與網關通訊                       |
| Sync     | 執行 / 同步層        | IR / RF 家電同步                         |
| Switch   | 互動 / 執行層        | 觸控輸入、場景觸發，依版本支援繼電器控制 |
| Panel    | 互動層               | 房間介面與共享控制                       |
| Act      | 執行層               | 電力執行與可選能源數據                   |
| Sense    | 感知層               | 環境上下文                               |
| Vision   | 感知 / Edge 上下文層 | 視覺上下文與事件感知                     |
| Cloud    | 雲端層               | 遠端存取、同步、生命週期                 |
| Edge     | 邊緣智慧層           | AI 輔助感知與優化                        |
| App      | 互動 / 雲端存取層    | 用戶控制、設定、遠端存取                 |

## **B.4 System Layer Mapping**

## **B.4 系統層級映射**

**EN  
**Each product or component belongs to a defined system layer. The
system layer determines how the component participates in architecture,
runtime behavior, data flow, control flow, and validation requirements.

A component may participate in more than one layer when its function
spans multiple system responsibilities.

**ZH-TW  
**每個產品或組件都屬於已定義系統層級。系統層級決定該組件如何參與架構、Runtime
行為、數據流、控制流與驗證要求。

當某一組件的功能跨越多個系統責任時，它可參與多個層級。

## **English Table**

| **System Layer** | **Mapped Products / Components** | **Description** |
|----|----|----|
| Cloud Layer | OceanAI Cloud | Provides remote access, account services, synchronization, lifecycle services, analytics, and multi-site management where supported |
| Edge Intelligence Layer | OceanAI Edge | Provides local AI-assisted inference, vision analysis, sensor fusion, and optimization where deployed |
| Local Runtime Layer | Artibird Hub, ArtiOS | Provides local services, state management, scene execution, automation, and command routing |
| Device Access Layer | Artibird Gate | Provides device onboarding, local communication, gateway communication, and network participation |
| Interaction Layer | Artibird Switch, Artibird Panel, Artibird App | Captures user intention, scene control, room control, setup, and local / remote access |
| Sensing Layer | Artibird Sense, Artibird Vision | Provides environmental and visual context |
| Execution Layer | Artibird Act, Switch relay variants, Artibird Sync | Provides controlled physical execution, relay behavior, load control, and appliance synchronization |
| Device Layer | Supported Artibird devices | Physical devices participating in the runtime system |

## **中文表**

| **系統層級** | **對應產品 / 組件** | **說明** |
|----|----|----|
| 雲端層 | OceanAI Cloud | 在支援條件下提供遠端存取、帳號服務、同步、生命週期服務、分析與多站點管理 |
| 邊緣智慧層 | OceanAI Edge | 在部署條件下提供本地 AI 輔助推理、視覺分析、感測融合與優化 |
| 本地 Runtime 層 | Artibird Hub、ArtiOS | 提供本地服務、狀態管理、場景執行、自動化與指令路由 |
| 設備接入層 | Artibird Gate | 提供設備入網、本地通訊、網關通訊與網路參與 |
| 互動層 | Artibird Switch、Artibird Panel、Artibird App | 捕捉用戶意圖、場景控制、房間控制、設定與本地 / 遠端存取 |
| 感知層 | Artibird Sense、Artibird Vision | 提供環境與視覺上下文 |
| 執行層 | Artibird Act、Switch 繼電器版本、Artibird Sync | 提供受控實體執行、繼電器行為、負載控制與家電同步 |
| 設備層 | 受支援 Artibird 設備 | 參與 Runtime 系統的實體設備 |

## **B.5 Runtime Participation Mapping**

## **B.5 Runtime 參與映射**

**EN  
**Runtime participation defines how each component contributes to active
system operation. Components may generate events, maintain state, route
commands, execute actions, provide sensing context, synchronize data, or
support local and remote control.

**ZH-TW  
**Runtime
參與定義每個組件如何貢獻於系統實際運行。組件可產生事件、維護狀態、路由指令、執行動作、提供感知上下文、同步數據，或支援本地與遠端控制。

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Runtime Participation** |
|----|----|
| OceanAI Cloud | Provides remote commands, synchronization, account data, lifecycle updates, alerts, historical data, and multi-site support |
| OceanAI Edge | Provides AI-assisted interpretation, visual analysis, sensor fusion, optimization signals, and contextual recommendations |
| ArtiOS | Processes rules, scenes, state, events, commands, automation, and local coordination |
| Artibird Hub | Hosts runtime services, MQTT broker, state management, automation modules, web services, and local coordination |
| Artibird Gate | Passes device events and commands between supported devices and Hub / ArtiOS |
| Artibird Switch | Generates touch events, scene triggers, relay state changes, and local control inputs depending on variant |
| Artibird Panel | Generates room-level control events, scene selections, device group actions, and status display behavior |
| Artibird Act | Executes relay, plug, load-control, and optional energy measurement behavior |
| Artibird Sense | Provides temperature, humidity, light, occupancy, and environmental signals |
| Artibird Sync | Sends IR / RF commands and reports appliance synchronization results where supported |
| Artibird Vision | Provides visual events, recording status, security awareness, and visual metadata where supported |
| Artibird App | Provides setup, configuration, local commands, remote commands, room management, scene management, and automation configuration |

## **中文表**

| **組件** | **Runtime 參與方式** |
|----|----|
| OceanAI Cloud | 提供遠端指令、同步、帳號數據、生命週期更新、警報、歷史數據與多站點支援 |
| OceanAI Edge | 提供 AI 輔助解讀、視覺分析、感測融合、優化信號與上下文建議 |
| ArtiOS | 處理規則、場景、狀態、事件、指令、自動化與本地協同 |
| Artibird Hub | 承載 Runtime 服務、MQTT Broker、狀態管理、自動化模組、Web 服務與本地協同 |
| Artibird Gate | 在受支援設備與 Hub / ArtiOS 之間傳遞設備事件與指令 |
| Artibird Switch | 依版本產生觸控事件、場景觸發、繼電器狀態變化與本地控制輸入 |
| Artibird Panel | 產生房間級控制事件、場景選擇、設備群組動作與狀態顯示行為 |
| Artibird Act | 執行繼電器、插座、負載控制與可選電能計量行為 |
| Artibird Sense | 提供溫度、濕度、光照、人在與環境信號 |
| Artibird Sync | 在支援條件下發送 IR / RF 指令並回報家電同步結果 |
| Artibird Vision | 在支援條件下提供視覺事件、錄影狀態、安全感知與視覺元數據 |
| Artibird App | 提供設定、配置、本地指令、遠端指令、房間管理、場景管理與自動化配置 |

## **B.6 Product Dependency Mapping**

## **B.6 產品依賴映射**

**EN  
**Product dependency mapping defines which components are required or
optional for each product to participate in supported system behavior.

A product may operate differently depending on whether Hub, Gate, Cloud,
Edge, App, local network, or required device nodes are available.

**ZH-TW  
**產品依賴映射定義每個產品參與受支援系統行為時，哪些組件是必需或可選的。

依
Hub、Gate、Cloud、Edge、App、本地網路或所需設備節點是否可用，同一產品可能呈現不同運作方式。

## **English Table**

| **Product / Component** | **Required Dependency** | **Optional / Enhanced Dependency** |
|----|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | Power, local network, ArtiOS modules | Cloud, Edge, App, Gate |
| Artibird Gate | Power, supported network path, device protocol support | Hub, Cloud, App depending on deployment |
| Artibird Switch | Power or battery, supported communication path | Hub, Gate, Cloud depending on variant |
| Artibird Panel | Power, supported communication path | Hub, Cloud, App, device groups |
| Artibird Act | Power, supported communication path, supported load | Hub, Gate, Cloud, energy reporting where supported |
| Artibird Sense | Power or battery, supported communication path | Hub, Gate, Cloud, Edge |
| Artibird Sync | Power, supported Wi-Fi / local path, supported IR / RF device | Hub, Cloud, App |
| Artibird Vision | Power, supported network path | Hub, Cloud, Edge, local storage |
| OceanAI Edge | Power, local network, supported input data | Hub, Vision, Sense, Cloud |
| OceanAI Cloud | Internet, account service, cloud infrastructure | App, Hub, multi-site structure |
| Artibird App | Mobile device, local network or cloud account | Hub, Cloud, local discovery |

## **中文表**

| **產品 / 組件** | **必需依賴** | **可選 / 增強依賴** |
|----|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | 供電、本地網路、ArtiOS 模組 | Cloud、Edge、App、Gate |
| Artibird Gate | 供電、受支援網路路徑、設備協議支援 | 依部署可包含 Hub、Cloud、App |
| Artibird Switch | 供電或電池、受支援通訊路徑 | 依版本可包含 Hub、Gate、Cloud |
| Artibird Panel | 供電、受支援通訊路徑 | Hub、Cloud、App、設備群組 |
| Artibird Act | 供電、受支援通訊路徑、受支援負載 | Hub、Gate、Cloud、支援條件下能源報告 |
| Artibird Sense | 供電或電池、受支援通訊路徑 | Hub、Gate、Cloud、Edge |
| Artibird Sync | 供電、受支援 Wi-Fi / 本地路徑、受支援 IR / RF 設備 | Hub、Cloud、App |
| Artibird Vision | 供電、受支援網路路徑 | Hub、Cloud、Edge、本地儲存 |
| OceanAI Edge | 供電、本地網路、受支援輸入數據 | Hub、Vision、Sense、Cloud |
| OceanAI Cloud | Internet、帳號服務、雲端基礎設施 | App、Hub、多站點結構 |
| Artibird App | 行動設備、本地網路或雲端帳號 | Hub、Cloud、本地發現 |

## **B.7 產品功能映射**

**EN  
**Product function mapping defines which system functions each product
primarily supports.

This mapping helps align engineering specifications, commercial
specifications, deployment planning, validation documents, and
user-facing descriptions.

**ZH-TW  
**產品功能映射定義每個產品主要支援哪些系統功能。

此映射有助於對齊工程規格書、商業規格書、部署規劃、驗證文件與面向用戶描述。

## **English Table**
