|----|----|
| OceanAI Cloud | Remote access, synchronization, account binding, lifecycle management, alerts, history, analytics, multi-site support |
| OceanAI Edge | AI-assisted inference, visual understanding, sensor fusion, optimization, contextual interpretation |
| ArtiOS | Runtime rules, scenes, automation, state management, command routing, local coordination |
| Artibird Hub | Local service hosting, MQTT, state, automation, web services, local control |
| Artibird Gate | Device onboarding, gateway communication, network participation, BLE Mesh / Wi-Fi / Ethernet support depending on variant |
| Artibird Switch | Touch input, scene trigger, event generation, relay control by variant |
| Artibird Panel | Room interface, scene control, device group control, status display |
| Artibird Act | Electrical execution, relay control, plug control, load control, energy measurement where supported |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental sensing, context input, automation input, alert input |
| Artibird Sync | IR / RF command, appliance control, appliance synchronization |
| Artibird Vision | Visual event, local recording, security awareness, AI-assisted visual context |
| Artibird App | Setup, configuration, local control, remote control, status view, scene and automation management |

## **中文表**

| **產品 / 組件** | **支援功能類別** |
|----|----|
| OceanAI Cloud | 遠端存取、同步、帳號綁定、生命週期管理、警報、歷史、分析、多站點支援 |
| OceanAI Edge | AI 輔助推理、視覺理解、感測融合、優化、上下文解讀 |
| ArtiOS | Runtime 規則、場景、自動化、狀態管理、指令路由、本地協同 |
| Artibird Hub | 本地服務承載、MQTT、狀態、自動化、Web 服務、本地控制 |
| Artibird Gate | 設備入網、網關通訊、網路參與，依版本支援 BLE Mesh / Wi-Fi / Ethernet |
| Artibird Switch | 觸控輸入、場景觸發、事件生成，依版本支援繼電器控制 |
| Artibird Panel | 房間介面、場景控制、設備群組控制、狀態顯示 |
| Artibird Act | 電力執行、繼電器控制、插座控制、負載控制，支援條件下電能計量 |
| Artibird Sense | 環境感知、上下文輸入、自動化輸入、警報輸入 |
| Artibird Sync | IR / RF 指令、家電控制、家電同步 |
| Artibird Vision | 視覺事件、本地錄影、安全感知、AI 輔助視覺上下文 |
| Artibird App | 設定、配置、本地控制、遠端控制、狀態查看、場景與自動化管理 |

## **B.8 Local, Cloud, and Edge Mapping**

## **B.8 本地、雲端與 Edge 映射**

**EN  
**This mapping defines whether each product or component primarily
operates locally, through cloud enhancement, or with Edge-assisted
intelligence.

**ZH-TW  
**本映射定義每個產品或組件主要是以本地方式運作、透過雲端增強，或透過
Edge 輔助智慧參與。

## **English Table**

| **Product / Component** | **Local Role** | **Cloud Role** | **Edge Role** |
|----|----|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | Primary local runtime center | Synchronizes selected data where supported | Receives Edge-assisted interpretation where deployed |
| Artibird Gate | Local device access gateway | May support cloud-linked device lifecycle where supported | No primary Edge role |
| Artibird Switch | Local interaction and event node | Remote state and configuration sync where supported | No primary Edge role |
| Artibird Panel | Local room interface | Configuration or status sync where supported | May display Edge-informed status where supported |
| Artibird Act | Local execution node | Energy or status data sync where supported | May execute Edge-informed automation where supported |
| Artibird Sense | Local sensing node | Sensor data or alert sync where supported | Provides input to Edge where deployed |
| Artibird Sync | Local appliance synchronization node | Remote control and command history where supported | May execute Edge-informed appliance behavior where supported |
| Artibird Vision | Local visual node | Cloud alert or remote viewing where supported | Provides visual input to Edge where deployed |
| OceanAI Cloud | No local runtime role | Primary cloud service role | May provide historical or multi-site context where supported |
| OceanAI Edge | Local AI-assisted processing | May sync selected outputs where supported | Primary Edge intelligence role |
| Artibird App | Local setup and control where supported | Remote access and account-based control | May display Edge-assisted outputs where supported |

## **中文表**

| **產品 / 組件** | **本地角色** | **雲端角色** | **Edge 角色** |
|----|----|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | 主要本地 Runtime 中心 | 在支援條件下同步特定數據 | 部署 Edge 時接收 Edge 輔助解讀 |
| Artibird Gate | 本地設備接入網關 | 在支援條件下支援雲端關聯設備生命週期 | 無主要 Edge 角色 |
| Artibird Switch | 本地互動與事件節點 | 在支援條件下同步遠端狀態與配置 | 無主要 Edge 角色 |
| Artibird Panel | 本地房間介面 | 在支援條件下同步配置或狀態 | 在支援條件下可顯示 Edge 輔助狀態 |
| Artibird Act | 本地執行節點 | 在支援條件下同步能源或狀態數據 | 在支援條件下可執行 Edge 輔助自動化 |
| Artibird Sense | 本地感知節點 | 在支援條件下同步感測數據或警報 | 部署 Edge 時提供輸入 |
| Artibird Sync | 本地家電同步節點 | 在支援條件下支援遠端控制與指令歷史 | 在支援條件下可執行 Edge 輔助家電行為 |
| Artibird Vision | 本地視覺節點 | 在支援條件下支援雲端警報或遠端查看 | 部署 Edge 時提供視覺輸入 |
| OceanAI Cloud | 無本地 Runtime 角色 | 主要雲端服務角色 | 在支援條件下可提供歷史或多站點上下文 |
| OceanAI Edge | 本地 AI 輔助處理 | 在支援條件下可同步特定輸出 | 主要 Edge 智慧角色 |
| Artibird App | 支援條件下本地設定與控制 | 遠端存取與基於帳號的控制 | 在支援條件下可顯示 Edge 輔助輸出 |

## **B.9 Deployment Mapping**

## **B.9 部署映射**

**EN  
**Deployment mapping defines how products may be used across different
deployment models.

A deployment model should select components based on required function,
environment, local runtime need, cloud need, edge need, network
condition, power condition, and validation requirement.

**ZH-TW  
**部署映射定義產品可如何用於不同部署模型中。

部署模型應根據所需功能、環境、本地 Runtime 需求、雲端需求、Edge
需求、網路條件、供電條件與驗證要求來選擇組件。

## **English Table**

| **Deployment Model** | **Recommended Components** |
|----|----|
| Smart Home | Hub, Gate, Switch, Sense, Act, Sync |
| Smart Classroom | Hub, Gate, Panel, Switch, Sense, Act, Sync, Vision |
| Smart Office | Hub, Panel, Switch, Sense, Act, Sync |
| Smart Building | Hub, Gate, Panel, Act, Sense, Vision, Cloud |
| Smart Campus | Hub, Gate, Sense, Act, Panel, Vision, Cloud, Edge |
| Energy Management | Hub, Act-E, Sense, Cloud, Edge |
| Vision-Aware Security | Vision, Hub, Cloud, Edge, Sense, Act |
| Agriculture / Irrigation | Hub, Gate, Sense, Act, Cloud |

## **中文表**

| **部署模型** | **建議組件**                                       |
|--------------|----------------------------------------------------|
| 智慧住宅     | Hub、Gate、Switch、Sense、Act、Sync                |
| 智慧教室     | Hub、Gate、Panel、Switch、Sense、Act、Sync、Vision |
| 智慧辦公     | Hub、Panel、Switch、Sense、Act、Sync               |
| 智慧建築     | Hub、Gate、Panel、Act、Sense、Vision、Cloud        |
| 智慧校園     | Hub、Gate、Sense、Act、Panel、Vision、Cloud、Edge  |
| 能源管理     | Hub、Act-E、Sense、Cloud、Edge                     |
| 視覺感知安全 | Vision、Hub、Cloud、Edge、Sense、Act               |
| 農業 / 灌溉  | Hub、Gate、Sense、Act、Cloud                       |

## **B.10 Mapping Boundary**

## **B.10 映射邊界**

**EN  
**This product-system mapping defines supported relationships between
products and system layers. It does not imply that every product is
required in every deployment, that every product supports every
function, or that every mapped function is available under all
conditions.

Each product-system relationship must be validated according to product
type, hardware version, firmware version, software version, deployment
model, network condition, cloud availability, edge deployment status,
and system capacity boundary.

**ZH-TW  
**本產品—系統映射定義產品與系統層級之間的受支援關係。它不表示每個部署都需要所有產品，也不表示每個產品支援所有功能，或每一項映射功能在所有條件下都可用。

每個產品—系統關係都必須依產品類型、硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、部署模型、網路條件、雲端可用性、Edge
部署狀態與系統容量邊界完成驗證。

## **B.11 Appendix Conclusion**

## **B.11 附錄結論**

**EN  
**This appendix defines the product-system mapping matrix of the OceanAI
/ Artibird system. It clarifies how Hub, Gate, Sync, Switch, Panel, Act,
Sense, Vision, Cloud, Edge, App, and ArtiOS correspond to system layers,
runtime responsibilities, functional roles, dependencies, and deployment
models.

**ZH-TW  
**本附錄定義了 OceanAI / Artibird 系統的產品—系統映射矩陣。它釐清
Hub、Gate、Sync、Switch、Panel、Act、Sense、Vision、Cloud、Edge、App 與
ArtiOS 如何對應至系統層級、Runtime 責任、功能角色、依賴關係與部署模型。

C — 系統驗證清單

# **C — 系統驗證清單**

# **Appendix C — System Validation Checklist**

# **Appendix C — 系統驗證清單**

## **C.1 Purpose**

## **C.1 目的**

**EN  
**This appendix defines the system validation checklist for the OceanAI
/ Artibird system. It provides a structured checklist for verifying
local control, cloud participation, runtime behavior, device onboarding,
connection capacity, scene execution, automation execution, MQTT
communication, offline behavior, failure behavior, security, privacy,
capacity limits, and deployment models.

**ZH-TW  
**本附錄定義 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的系統驗證清單。它提供一套結構化清單，用於驗證本地控制、雲端參與、Runtime
行為、設備入網、連接容量、場景執行、自動化執行、MQTT
通訊、離線行為、故障行為、安全、隱私、容量限制與部署模型。

## **C.2 System Validation Checklist Definition**

## **C.2 系統驗證清單定義**

**EN  
**System Validation Checklist defines the minimum validation items
required before system-level functions, engineering claims, commercial
claims, deployment models, or customer-facing descriptions are used as
official references.

Each validation item must be reviewed according to supported hardware,
firmware, software, network condition, cloud availability, Edge
deployment status, product mix, deployment model, expected behavior,
observed result, and acceptance criteria.

**ZH-TW  
**系統驗證清單定義在系統級功能、工程宣稱、商業宣稱、部署模型或面向客戶描述被作為正式參考之前，至少需要完成的驗證項目。

每個驗證項目都必須依受支援硬體、韌體、軟體、網路條件、雲端可用性、Edge
部署狀態、產品組合、部署模型、預期行為、觀察結果與驗收標準進行審查。

## **C.3 System Validation Checklist**

## **C.3 系統驗證清單**

## **English Table**

| **Validation Item**               | **Required**        |
|-----------------------------------|---------------------|
| Local control verified            | Yes                 |
| Cloud remote control verified     | Yes / If applicable |
| Hub runtime behavior verified     | Yes                 |
| Gate connection capacity verified | Yes                 |
| Device onboarding verified        | Yes                 |
| Scene execution verified          | Yes                 |
| Automation execution verified     | Yes                 |
| MQTT communication verified       | Yes                 |
| Offline behavior verified         | Yes                 |
| Cloud failure behavior verified   | Yes                 |
| Edge failure behavior verified    | If applicable       |
| Security access control verified  | Yes                 |
| Vision privacy behavior verified  | If applicable       |
| Capacity limits verified          | Yes                 |
| Deployment model verified         | Yes                 |

## **中文表**

| **驗證項目**         | **是否必須** |
|----------------------|--------------|
| 本地控制驗證         | 是           |
| 雲端遠端控制驗證     | 是 / 如適用  |
| Hub Runtime 行為驗證 | 是           |
| Gate 連接容量驗證    | 是           |
| 設備入網驗證         | 是           |
| 場景執行驗證         | 是           |
| 自動化執行驗證       | 是           |
| MQTT 通訊驗證        | 是           |
| 離線行為驗證         | 是           |
| 雲端故障行為驗證     | 是           |
| Edge 故障行為驗證    | 如適用       |
| 安全存取控制驗證     | 是           |
| Vision 隱私行為驗證  | 如適用       |
| 容量限制驗證         | 是           |
| 部署模型驗證         | 是           |

## **C.4 Local Control Validation**

## **C.4 本地控制驗證**

**EN  
**Local control validation verifies that supported local control
functions operate without requiring cloud execution when required local
components are present.

This validation should include Switch control, Panel control, App local
control, Act execution, Sync command behavior, device state update,
local scene execution, and local automation where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**本地控制驗證確認當所需本地組件具備時，受支援本地控制功能可在不需要雲端執行的情況下運作。

此驗證應包含支援條件下的 Switch 控制、Panel 控制、App 本地控制、Act
執行、Sync 指令行為、設備狀態更新、本地場景執行與本地自動化。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Switch local action | Touch input triggers expected local behavior |
| Panel local action | Panel command triggers expected room or device behavior |
| App local action | App sends local command through supported local path |
| Act execution | Relay, plug, or load action executes correctly |
| Sync execution | IR / RF command is sent and reported where supported |
| Device state update | State changes are reflected in local runtime |
| Local scene | Scene executes without cloud dependency where configured |
| Local automation | Automation executes locally under defined conditions |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目**    | **必須驗證內容**                    |
|-----------------|-------------------------------------|
| Switch 本地動作 | 觸控輸入觸發預期本地行為            |
| Panel 本地動作  | Panel 指令觸發預期房間或設備行為    |
| App 本地動作    | App 透過受支援本地路徑發送本地指令  |
| Act 執行        | 繼電器、插座或負載動作正確執行      |
| Sync 執行       | 支援條件下 IR / RF 指令被發送並回報 |
| 設備狀態更新    | 狀態變化反映於本地 Runtime          |
| 本地場景        | 已配置場景在不依賴雲端條件下執行    |
| 本地自動化      | 自動化在明確條件下本地執行          |

## **C.5 Cloud Remote Control Validation**

## **C.5 雲端遠端控制驗證**

**EN  
**Cloud remote control validation verifies that supported remote control
functions operate through OceanAI Cloud under defined Internet, account,
permission, Hub, device, and cloud service conditions.

This validation applies only when remote access is implemented and
supported.

**ZH-TW  
**雲端遠端控制驗證確認在明確
Internet、帳號、權限、Hub、設備與雲端服務條件下，受支援遠端控制功能可透過
OceanAI Cloud 運作。

此驗證僅適用於已實作且受支援遠端存取的情況。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Account authentication | Remote user is authenticated |
| Permission check | User role allows requested remote action |
| Cloud command path | Cloud command reaches Hub and target device where supported |
| Remote device control | Target device executes supported remote command |
| Remote scene control | Scene executes through supported remote path |
| Remote status view | Device or site status is visible remotely |
| Cloud alert delivery | Alerts are delivered through supported notification path |
| Remote failure handling | Remote access fails safely when cloud or Internet is unavailable |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目** | **必須驗證內容**                           |
|--------------|--------------------------------------------|
| 帳號身份認證 | 遠端用戶完成身份認證                       |
| 權限檢查     | 用戶角色允許請求的遠端動作                 |
| 雲端指令路徑 | 支援條件下雲端指令到達 Hub 與目標設備      |
| 遠端設備控制 | 目標設備執行受支援遠端指令                 |
| 遠端場景控制 | 場景透過受支援遠端路徑執行                 |
| 遠端狀態查看 | 可遠端查看設備或站點狀態                   |
| 雲端警報傳送 | 警報透過受支援通知路徑傳送                 |
| 遠端故障處理 | 雲端或 Internet 不可用時，遠端存取安全失效 |

## **C.6 Hub Runtime Behavior Validation**

## **C.6 Hub Runtime 行為驗證**

**EN  
**Hub runtime behavior validation verifies that Artibird Hub and ArtiOS
correctly provide local runtime services, state management, event
handling, command routing, scene execution, automation execution, MQTT
services, and local coordination.

**ZH-TW  
**Hub Runtime 行為驗證確認 Artibird Hub 與 ArtiOS 能正確提供本地 Runtime
服務、狀態管理、事件處理、指令路由、場景執行、自動化執行、MQTT
服務與本地協同。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Local runtime service | Hub services and ArtiOS modules start and operate correctly |
| Event handling | Events are received and processed correctly |
| State management | Device and system states are maintained correctly |
| Command routing | Commands are routed to intended targets |
| Scene execution | Configured scenes execute correctly |
| Automation execution | Configured automations execute correctly |
| MQTT service | Broker and message routing operate where implemented |
| Runtime priority | Safety, local manual, automation, Edge, cloud, and background priorities apply |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目**      | **必須驗證內容**                                       |
|-------------------|--------------------------------------------------------|
| 本地 Runtime 服務 | Hub 服務與 ArtiOS 模組正確啟動並運作                   |
| 事件處理          | 事件被正確接收與處理                                   |
| 狀態管理          | 設備與系統狀態被正確維護                               |
| 指令路由          | 指令被路由至預期目標                                   |
| 場景執行          | 已配置場景正確執行                                     |
| 自動化執行        | 已配置自動化正確執行                                   |
| MQTT 服務         | 已實作條件下 Broker 與消息路由正常                     |
| Runtime 優先級    | 安全、本地手動、自動化、Edge、雲端與背景優先級正確適用 |

## **C.7 Gate Connection Capacity Validation**

## **C.7 Gate 連接容量驗證**

**EN  
**Gate connection capacity validation verifies the supported number of
devices and active connections that can be handled by Artibird Gate
under defined test conditions.

This validation must be based on system-level testing, not theoretical
chipset capability.

**ZH-TW  
**Gate 連接容量驗證確認 Artibird Gate
在明確測試條件下，可處理的受支援設備數與活躍連接數。

此驗證必須基於系統級測試，而不是理論晶片能力。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Gate model | Gate model and hardware version are recorded |
| Firmware version | Firmware version under test is recorded |
| Protocol type | Wi-Fi, Ethernet, BLE Mesh, or Wi-Fi Mesh condition is defined |
| Device count | Tested device count is recorded |
| Product mix | Connected device types are recorded |
| Event rate | Average and peak event rate are recorded |
| Stability | Gate remains stable under tested load |
| Failure behavior | Behavior beyond validated capacity is defined |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目** | **必須驗證內容**                                  |
|--------------|---------------------------------------------------|
| Gate 型號    | 記錄 Gate 型號與硬體版本                          |
| 韌體版本     | 記錄測試韌體版本                                  |
| 協議類型     | 定義 Wi-Fi、Ethernet、BLE Mesh 或 Wi-Fi Mesh 條件 |
| 設備數量     | 記錄已測設備數量                                  |
| 產品組合     | 記錄已連接設備類型                                |
| 事件速率     | 記錄平均與峰值事件速率                            |
| 穩定性       | Gate 在已測負載下保持穩定                         |
| 故障行為     | 定義超出已驗證容量後的行為                        |

## **C.8 Device Onboarding Validation**

## **C.8 設備入網驗證**

**EN  
**Device onboarding validation verifies that supported devices can be
discovered, registered, authenticated, assigned, bound, and made
available to the local runtime system.

**ZH-TW  
**設備入網驗證確認受支援設備可被發現、註冊、身份認證、分配、綁定，並可用於本地
Runtime 系統。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item**   | **Required Verification**                            |
|----------------------|------------------------------------------------------|
| Device discovery     | Device can be discovered through supported path      |
| Device registration  | Device can be registered into the system             |
| Device identity      | Device identity is verified                          |
| Account binding      | Device can be bound where required                   |
| Room assignment      | Device can be assigned to room, space, or site       |
| Capability detection | Device capability is correctly recognized            |
| State initialization | Initial device state is correctly created            |
| Onboarding failure   | Invalid or unsupported onboarding is rejected safely |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目** | **必須驗證內容**             |
|--------------|------------------------------|
| 設備發現     | 設備可透過受支援路徑被發現   |
| 設備註冊     | 設備可註冊至系統             |
| 設備身份     | 設備身份完成驗證             |
| 帳號綁定     | 需要時設備可完成綁定         |
| 房間分配     | 設備可分配至房間、空間或站點 |
| 能力識別     | 設備能力被正確識別           |
| 狀態初始化   | 初始設備狀態被正確建立       |
| 入網失敗     | 無效或未支援入網被安全拒絕   |

## **C.9 Scene Execution Validation**

## **C.9 場景執行驗證**

**EN  
**Scene execution validation verifies that configured multi-device
scenes execute expected actions under defined local or remote
conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**場景執行驗證確認已配置多設備場景可在明確本地或遠端條件下執行預期動作。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Scene configuration | Scene can be created and stored |
| Scene trigger | Scene can be triggered by supported source |
| Multi-device action | All target devices execute expected actions |
| Execution order | Action order follows defined behavior where required |
| State update | Device and scene states update after execution |
| Local scene | Scene executes locally where configured |
| Remote scene | Scene executes remotely where supported |
| Failure handling | Partial failure behavior is defined and reported where supported |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目** | **必須驗證內容**                     |
|--------------|--------------------------------------|
| 場景配置     | 場景可被建立與儲存                   |
| 場景觸發     | 場景可由受支援來源觸發               |
| 多設備動作   | 所有目標設備執行預期動作             |
| 執行順序     | 需要時動作順序遵循已定義行為         |
| 狀態更新     | 執行後設備與場景狀態更新             |
| 本地場景     | 已配置條件下場景可本地執行           |
| 遠端場景     | 支援條件下場景可遠端執行             |
| 故障處理     | 部分失敗行為被定義，支援條件下可回報 |

## **C.10 Automation Execution Validation**

## **C.10 自動化執行驗證**

**EN  
**Automation execution validation verifies that configured automation
rules execute correctly according to time, sensor value, event, state,
user configuration, cloud input, or Edge-assisted interpretation where
supported.

**ZH-TW  
**自動化執行驗證確認已配置自動化規則可依時間、感測值、事件、狀態、用戶配置、雲端輸入，或支援條件下
Edge 輔助解讀正確執行。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Automation configuration | Rule can be created and stored |
| Trigger condition | Defined trigger condition is detected |
| Rule evaluation | Rule logic evaluates correctly |
| Target action | Target device or scene executes expected action |
| Local automation | Automation executes locally where configured |
| Cloud-enhanced automation | Cloud-supported behavior works where applicable |
| Edge-assisted automation | Edge output informs automation only within defined boundary |
| Safety override | Safety and fail-safe behavior override automation where required |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目**    | **必須驗證內容**                     |
|-----------------|--------------------------------------|
| 自動化配置      | 規則可被建立與儲存                   |
| 觸發條件        | 已定義觸發條件被偵測                 |
| 規則判斷        | 規則邏輯判斷正確                     |
| 目標動作        | 目標設備或場景執行預期動作           |
| 本地自動化      | 已配置條件下自動化可本地執行         |
| 雲端增強自動化  | 適用時雲端支援行為正常               |
| Edge 輔助自動化 | Edge 輸出僅在已定義邊界內影響自動化  |
| 安全覆蓋        | 需要時安全與故障安全行為優先於自動化 |

## **C.11 MQTT Communication Validation**

## **C.11 MQTT 通訊驗證**

**EN  
**MQTT communication validation verifies that MQTT broker, topics,
authentication, message formats, publish / subscribe behavior, command
routing, state reporting, and failure handling operate correctly where
MQTT is implemented.

**ZH-TW  
**MQTT 通訊驗證確認在已實作 MQTT 的條件下，MQTT
Broker、Topic、身份認證、消息格式、發布 /
訂閱行為、指令路由、狀態上報與故障處理正常運作。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Broker availability | MQTT broker starts and remains available |
| Client authentication | Clients authenticate where required |
| Topic structure | Topics follow defined naming rules |
| Publish behavior | Messages publish correctly |
| Subscribe behavior | Clients receive expected messages |
| Command routing | Commands route to intended target |
| State reporting | Device state reports correctly |
| Failure handling | Broker, client, or network failure behavior is defined |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目**   | **必須驗證內容**                   |
|----------------|------------------------------------|
| Broker 可用性  | MQTT Broker 啟動並保持可用         |
| 客戶端身份認證 | 需要時客戶端完成身份認證           |
| Topic 結構     | Topic 遵循已定義命名規則           |
| 發布行為       | 消息正確發布                       |
| 訂閱行為       | 客戶端接收預期消息                 |
| 指令路由       | 指令路由至預期目標                 |
| 狀態上報       | 設備狀態正確上報                   |
| 故障處理       | Broker、客戶端或網路故障行為被定義 |

## **C.12 Offline Behavior Validation**

## **C.12 離線行為驗證**

**EN  
**Offline behavior validation verifies which supported functions
continue when Internet or cloud access is unavailable.

This validation must clearly distinguish between local functions,
cloud-required functions, cloud-enhanced functions, and unavailable
functions.

**ZH-TW  
**離線行為驗證確認 Internet
或雲端存取不可用時，哪些受支援功能可以繼續運作。

此驗證必須清楚區分本地功能、必須雲端功能、雲端增強功能與不可用功能。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Local device control | Continues without Internet where required local components are present |
| Local scene execution | Continues where scenes are locally configured |
| Local automation | Continues where rules and required devices are local |
| Physical control | Continues according to device design |
| App local access | Works through supported local path where implemented |
| Remote control | Stops or degrades without cloud / Internet |
| Cloud sync | Stops, delays, queues, or retries as defined |
| Offline recovery | System resumes cloud functions after reconnection where supported |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目** | **必須驗證內容**                         |
|--------------|------------------------------------------|
| 本地設備控制 | 所需本地元件具備時，無 Internet 仍可繼續 |
| 本地場景執行 | 場景已本地配置時可繼續                   |
| 本地自動化   | 規則與所需設備均在本地時可繼續           |
| 實體控制     | 依設備設計繼續運作                       |
| App 本地存取 | 已實作條件下透過受支援本地路徑運作       |
| 遠端控制     | 無雲端 / Internet 時停止或降級           |
| 雲端同步     | 依定義停止、延遲、排隊或重試             |
| 離線恢復     | 支援條件下重新連接後恢復雲端功能         |

## **C.13 Failure Behavior Validation**

## **C.13 故障行為驗證**

**EN  
**Failure behavior validation verifies how the system behaves when
cloud, Internet, Hub, Gate, devices, Edge, App, power, network, or
storage becomes unavailable or degraded.

**ZH-TW  
**故障行為驗證確認當雲端、Internet、Hub、Gate、設備、Edge、App、電力、網路或儲存不可用或降級時，系統如何運作。

## **English Table**

| **Failure Scenario** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Cloud unavailable | Local supported functions continue where applicable |
| Internet unavailable | Local network functions continue where configured |
| Hub unavailable | Hub-dependent runtime behavior stops or degrades as defined |
| Gate unavailable | Gate-dependent device access degrades as defined |
| Device offline | Device is marked offline and commands follow defined behavior |
| Edge unavailable | Edge-assisted functions stop or degrade while local runtime continues |
| App unavailable | Physical controls and local automation continue where supported |
| Power failure | Recovery follows defined startup and state behavior |
| Network congestion | System degrades according to capacity and priority rules |
| Storage unavailable | Logs, history, Vision data, or state storage follow defined behavior |

## **中文表**

| **故障場景**    | **必須驗證內容**                                |
|-----------------|-------------------------------------------------|
| 雲端不可用      | 適用時受支援本地功能繼續                        |
| Internet 不可用 | 已配置條件下本地網路功能繼續                    |
| Hub 不可用      | Hub 依賴 Runtime 行為按定義停止或降級           |
| Gate 不可用     | 依賴 Gate 的設備接入按定義降級                  |
| 設備離線        | 設備被標記離線，指令遵循已定義行為              |
| Edge 不可用     | Edge 輔助功能停止或降級，本地 Runtime 繼續      |
| App 不可用      | 支援條件下實體控制與本地自動化繼續              |
| 電力故障        | 恢復遵循已定義啟動與狀態行為                    |
| 網路擁塞        | 系統依容量與優先級規則降級                      |
| 儲存不可用      | 日誌、歷史、Vision 數據或狀態儲存遵循已定義行為 |

## **C.14 Security Access Control Validation**

## **C.14 安全存取控制驗證**

**EN  
**Security access control validation verifies device identity, account
binding, local access control, remote access control, role-based access
control, secure communication, firmware update security, and audit logs
where supported.

**ZH-TW  
**安全存取控制驗證確認設備身份、帳號綁定、本地存取控制、遠端存取控制、角色權限控制、安全通訊、韌體更新安全與支援條件下審計日誌是否正常。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Device identity | Device identity is verified before participation |
| Account binding | Binding follows security and permission rules |
| Local access control | Local commands follow user and device permission |
| Remote access control | Remote access requires valid authentication and authorization |
| Role-based access | Role permissions are correctly enforced |
| Secure communication | Implemented secure paths operate correctly |
| Firmware update security | Unauthorized or invalid firmware is rejected |
| Audit logs | Security-sensitive events are recorded where supported |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目** | **必須驗證內容**               |
|--------------|--------------------------------|
| 設備身份     | 設備參與前完成身份驗證         |
| 帳號綁定     | 綁定遵循安全與權限規則         |
| 本地存取控制 | 本地指令遵循用戶與設備權限     |
| 遠端存取控制 | 遠端存取需要有效身份認證與授權 |
| 角色權限控制 | 角色權限被正確執行             |
| 安全通訊     | 已實作安全路徑正常運作         |
| 韌體更新安全 | 未授權或無效韌體被拒絕         |
| 審計日誌     | 支援條件下安全敏感事件被記錄   |

## **C.15 Vision Privacy Behavior Validation**

## **C.15 Vision 隱私行為驗證**

**EN  
**Vision privacy behavior validation verifies how Vision data is
recorded, processed, accessed, stored, synchronized, retained, or
deleted.

This validation applies where Artibird Vision, OceanAI Edge, OceanAI
Cloud, or Vision-related alerts are deployed.

**ZH-TW  
**Vision 隱私行為驗證確認 Vision
數據如何被錄製、處理、存取、儲存、同步、保留或刪除。

此驗證適用於部署 Artibird Vision、OceanAI Edge、OceanAI Cloud 或 Vision
相關警報的情況。

## **English Table**

| **Checklist Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Recording behavior | Recording occurs only as defined |
| Local storage | Local storage follows configured rule |
| Cloud sync | Cloud sync follows permission and policy |
| Edge processing | Edge processing follows privacy boundary |
| Access permission | Only permitted users access Vision data |
| Retention rule | Vision data retention follows defined duration |
| Deletion rule | Deletion or removal behavior works where supported |
| Alert behavior | Visual alerts follow configured privacy and notification rules |

## **中文表**

| **清單項目** | **必須驗證內容**                 |
|--------------|----------------------------------|
| 錄影行為     | 錄影僅依定義發生                 |
| 本地儲存     | 本地儲存遵循已配置規則           |
| 雲端同步     | 雲端同步遵循權限與政策           |
| Edge 處理    | Edge 處理遵循隱私邊界            |
| 存取權限     | 只有被允許用戶可存取 Vision 數據 |
| 保留規則     | Vision 數據保留遵循已定義時長    |
| 刪除規則     | 支援條件下刪除或移除行為正常     |
| 警報行為     | 視覺警報遵循已配置隱私與通知規則 |

## **C.16 Capacity Limits Validation**

## **C.16 容量限制驗證**

**EN  
**Capacity limits validation verifies that measurable system limits are
tested and recorded under defined conditions.

Capacity validation must cover the actual system, not only the
theoretical capability of individual chips or components.

**ZH-TW  
**容量限制驗證確認可量測系統限制已在明確條件下完成測試並記錄。

容量驗證必須覆蓋實際系統，而不僅是單一晶片或組件的理論能力。

## **English Table**

| **Capacity Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Max concurrent device connections | Tested and recorded under defined conditions |
| Max devices per Gate | Tested with defined Gate model, firmware, protocol, and network condition |
| Max devices per Hub | Tested with defined Hub hardware, service load, and product mix |
| Max scenes | Tested under defined scene complexity |
| Max automations | Tested under defined rule complexity and trigger rate |
| MQTT throughput | Tested with defined message rate, payload, and client count |
| Event latency | Measured from event source to action execution |
| Vision stream limits | Tested with defined Vision device, stream, network, and storage condition |
| Edge processing limits | Tested with defined hardware, model, input, and load condition |

## **中文表**

| **容量項目**         | **必須驗證內容**                                   |
|----------------------|----------------------------------------------------|
| 最大併發設備連接數   | 在明確條件下測試並記錄                             |
| 每個 Gate 最大設備數 | 以明確 Gate 型號、韌體、協議與網路條件完成測試     |
| 每個 Hub 最大設備數  | 以明確 Hub 硬體、服務負載與產品組合完成測試        |
| 最大場景數           | 在明確場景複雜度下完成測試                         |
| 最大自動化數         | 在明確規則複雜度與觸發速率下完成測試               |
| MQTT 吞吐量          | 以明確消息速率、Payload 與客戶端數完成測試         |
| 事件延遲             | 從事件來源至動作執行完成量測                       |
| Vision 視頻流限制    | 以明確 Vision 設備、視頻流、網路與儲存條件完成測試 |
| Edge 處理限制        | 以明確硬體、模型、輸入與負載條件完成測試           |

## **C.17 Deployment Model Validation**

## **C.17 部署模型驗證**

**EN  
**Deployment model validation verifies that a supported deployment
scenario operates as described under representative or actual site
conditions.

This validation should cover residential, classroom, office, building,
campus, energy management, vision-aware security, agriculture, and
infrastructure deployments where applicable.

**ZH-TW  
**部署模型驗證確認受支援部署場景可在代表性或實際場地條件下按描述運作。

此驗證應在適用條件下涵蓋住宅、教室、辦公、建築、校園、能源管理、視覺感知安全、農業與基礎設施部署。

## **English Table**

| **Deployment Item** | **Required Verification** |
|----|----|
| Scenario definition | Deployment scenario is clearly defined |
| Required components | Required products and platform components are identified |
| Component placement | Placement and coverage are verified |
| Network topology | Local network, cloud path, and gateway path are verified |
| Device count | Device count is within validated capacity |
| Local runtime | Required local behavior operates correctly |
| Cloud participation | Cloud-enhanced behavior operates where supported |
| Edge participation | Edge-assisted behavior operates where deployed |
| Failure behavior | Failure and degraded operation follow defined behavior |
| Acceptance result | Deployment meets defined acceptance criteria |

## **中文表**

| **部署項目** | **必須驗證內容**                     |
|--------------|--------------------------------------|
| 場景定義     | 部署場景被清楚定義                   |
| 所需組件     | 所需產品與平台組件被識別             |
| 組件佈置     | 佈置與覆蓋完成驗證                   |
| 網路拓撲     | 本地網路、雲端路徑與網關路徑完成驗證 |
| 設備數量     | 設備數量在已驗證容量內               |
| 本地 Runtime | 所需本地行為正常運作                 |
| 雲端參與     | 支援條件下雲端增強行為正常           |
| Edge 參與    | 部署條件下 Edge 輔助行為正常         |
| 故障行為     | 故障與降級運作遵循已定義行為         |
| 驗收結果     | 部署符合已定義驗收標準               |

## **C.18 Validation Evidence Record**

## **C.18 驗證證據記錄**

**EN  
**Each validation item should be supported by a validation evidence
record. The evidence record should make the validation traceable to a
product, system function, deployment model, test condition, observed
result, and claim boundary.

**ZH-TW  
**每個驗證項目都應由驗證證據記錄支持。證據記錄應使驗證結果可追溯至產品、系統功能、部署模型、測試條件、觀察結果與宣稱邊界。

## **English Table**

| **Evidence Field** | **Required Content** |
|----|----|
| Validation ID | Unique validation identifier |
| Validation item | Item being verified |
| Related section | Related system specification section |
| Product / component | Product or component under validation |
| Hardware version | Hardware version used |
| Firmware version | Firmware version used |
| Software version | Software, App, Cloud, ArtiOS, or Edge version used |
| Network condition | Test network topology and condition |
| Cloud condition | Cloud availability and service condition |
| Edge condition | Edge deployment and model condition where applicable |
| Test condition | Defined test condition |
| Expected result | Expected behavior |
| Observed result | Actual observed behavior |
| Pass / fail | Validation result |
| Evidence attachment | Logs, screenshots, reports, measurements, or videos where applicable |
| Approval status | Draft, reviewed, approved, or final |

## **中文表**

| **證據欄位** | **必須內容**                                |
|--------------|---------------------------------------------|
| 驗證 ID      | 唯一驗證識別碼                              |
| 驗證項目     | 被驗證項目                                  |
| 關聯章節     | 關聯系統規格書章節                          |
| 產品 / 組件  | 被驗證產品或組件                            |
| 硬體版本     | 使用的硬體版本                              |
| 韌體版本     | 使用的韌體版本                              |
| 軟體版本     | 使用的軟體、App、Cloud、ArtiOS 或 Edge 版本 |
| 網路條件     | 測試網路拓撲與條件                          |
| 雲端條件     | 雲端可用性與服務條件                        |
| Edge 條件    | 適用時 Edge 部署與模型條件                  |
| 測試條件     | 明確測試條件                                |
| 預期結果     | 預期行為                                    |
| 觀察結果     | 實際觀察行為                                |
| 通過 / 失敗  | 驗證結果                                    |
| 證據附件     | 適用時日誌、截圖、報告、量測數據或視頻      |
| 核准狀態     | 草案、已審查、已核准或最終版                |

## **C.19 Checklist Boundary**

## **C.19 清單邊界**

**EN  
**This checklist defines required validation items for the OceanAI /
Artibird system. It does not automatically validate any system function,
product capability, deployment model, capacity limit, security claim,
privacy claim, or commercial claim.

Validation is complete only when the required evidence has been
collected, reviewed, and approved under defined conditions.

**ZH-TW  
**本清單定義 OceanAI / Artibird
系統所需驗證項目。它不會自動驗證任何系統功能、產品能力、部署模型、容量限制、安全宣稱、隱私宣稱或商業宣稱。

只有在明確條件下收集、審查並核准所需證據後，驗證才算完成。

## **C.20 Appendix Conclusion**

## **C.20 附錄結論**

**EN  
**This appendix defines the system validation checklist for the OceanAI
/ Artibird system. It provides the minimum validation structure required
to support system behavior, engineering claims, commercial claims,
deployment models, capacity boundaries, security behavior, privacy
behavior, cloud participation, Edge participation, and local-first
operation.

**ZH-TW  
**本附錄定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的系統驗證清單。它提供支援系統行為、工程宣稱、商業宣稱、部署模型、容量邊界、安全行為、隱私行為、雲端參與、Edge
參與與本地優先運作所需的最低驗證結構。

D — 部署參考模型

# **D — 部署參考模型**

# **Appendix D — Deployment Reference Models**

# **Appendix D — 部署參考模型**

## **D.1 Purpose**

## **D.1 目的**

**EN  
**This appendix defines deployment reference models for the OceanAI /
Artibird system. It provides reference component combinations for
supported deployment scenarios, including smart home, smart classroom,
smart office, smart building, smart campus, energy management,
vision-aware security, and agriculture / irrigation.

**ZH-TW  
**本附錄定義 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的部署參考模型。它為受支援部署場景提供參考組件組合，包括智慧住宅、智慧教室、智慧辦公、智慧建築、智慧校園、能源管理、視覺感知安全與農業
/ 灌溉。

## **D.2 Deployment Reference Model Definition**

## **D.2 部署參考模型定義**

**EN  
**Deployment Reference Models define how OceanAI and Artibird components
may be combined for typical system deployments.

These models are reference structures. They do not imply that every
listed component is required in every project, nor do they imply that
every deployment can use the same network topology, device count, power
condition, cloud configuration, Edge configuration, or validation
boundary.

Each deployment must be planned according to actual site conditions,
supported products, local runtime requirements, cloud requirements, Edge
requirements, device count, capacity limits, safety requirements,
privacy requirements, and validation evidence.

**ZH-TW  
**部署參考模型定義 OceanAI 與 Artibird
組件可如何組合，用於典型系統部署。

這些模型屬於參考結構。它們不表示每個項目都必須使用所有列出組件，也不表示每個部署都可使用相同網路拓撲、設備數量、供電條件、雲端配置、Edge
配置或驗證邊界。

每個部署都必須依據實際場地條件、受支援產品、本地 Runtime
要求、雲端要求、Edge
要求、設備數量、容量限制、安全要求、隱私要求與驗證證據進行規劃。

## **D.3 Deployment Reference Models Table**

## **D.3 部署參考模型表**

## **English Table**

| **Scenario** | **Recommended Components** |
|----|----|
| Smart Home | Hub, Gate, Switch, Sense, Act, Sync |
| Smart Classroom | Hub, Gate, Panel, Switch, Sense, Act, Sync, Vision |
| Smart Office | Hub, Panel, Switch, Sense, Act, Sync |
| Smart Building | Hub, Gate, Panel, Act, Sense, Vision, Cloud |
| Smart Campus | Hub, Gate, Sense, Act, Panel, Vision, Cloud, Edge |
| Energy Management | Hub, Act-E, Sense, Cloud, Edge |
| Vision-Aware Security | Vision, Hub, Cloud, Edge, Sense, Act |
| Agriculture / Irrigation | Hub, Gate, Sense, Act, Cloud |

## **中文表**

| **場景**     | **建議組件**                                       |
|--------------|----------------------------------------------------|
| 智慧住宅     | Hub、Gate、Switch、Sense、Act、Sync                |
| 智慧教室     | Hub、Gate、Panel、Switch、Sense、Act、Sync、Vision |
| 智慧辦公     | Hub、Panel、Switch、Sense、Act、Sync               |
| 智慧建築     | Hub、Gate、Panel、Act、Sense、Vision、Cloud        |
| 智慧校園     | Hub、Gate、Sense、Act、Panel、Vision、Cloud、Edge  |
| 能源管理     | Hub、Act-E、Sense、Cloud、Edge                     |
| 視覺感知安全 | Vision、Hub、Cloud、Edge、Sense、Act               |
| 農業 / 灌溉  | Hub、Gate、Sense、Act、Cloud                       |

## **D.4 Smart Home Reference Model**

## **D.4 智慧住宅參考模型**

**EN  
**Smart Home deployment is a residential reference model designed for
local control, room-level automation, appliance synchronization,
sensing, and optional cloud-enhanced remote access.

This model typically uses Artibird Hub as the local runtime center,
Artibird Gate as the device access gateway, and supported Artibird
devices for interaction, sensing, execution, and synchronization.

**ZH-TW  
**智慧住宅部署是一種面向住宅場景的參考模型，用於本地控制、房間級自動化、家電同步、感知，以及可選的雲端增強遠端存取。

此模型通常使用 Artibird Hub 作為本地 Runtime 中心，Artibird Gate
作為設備接入網關，並使用受支援 Artibird
設備提供互動、感知、執行與同步能力。

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Reference Role** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | Local runtime center for scenes, automation, state, and local services |
| Artibird Gate | Device access gateway for supported local devices |
| Artibird Switch | Local touch control, scene trigger, and relay control by variant |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental sensing for temperature, humidity, light, and occupancy where supported |
| Artibird Act | Electrical execution, plug control, load control, and optional energy data |
| Artibird Sync | IR / RF appliance synchronization |
| Artibird App | Setup, local control, room management, scene management, and remote access where supported |
| OceanAI Cloud | Remote access, synchronization, alerts, and lifecycle services where supported |

## **中文表**

| **組件**        | **參考角色**                                           |
|-----------------|--------------------------------------------------------|
| Artibird Hub    | 用於場景、自動化、狀態與本地服務的本地 Runtime 中心    |
| Artibird Gate   | 面向受支援本地設備的設備接入網關                       |
| Artibird Switch | 本地觸控控制、場景觸發，依版本支援繼電器控制           |
| Artibird Sense  | 支援條件下用於溫度、濕度、光照與人在的環境感知         |
| Artibird Act    | 電力執行、插座控制、負載控制與可選能源數據             |
| Artibird Sync   | IR / RF 家電同步                                       |
| Artibird App    | 設定、本地控制、房間管理、場景管理與支援條件下遠端存取 |
| OceanAI Cloud   | 支援條件下遠端存取、同步、警報與生命週期服務           |

## **D.5 Smart Classroom Reference Model**

## **D.5 智慧教室參考模型**

**EN  
**Smart Classroom deployment is a reference model for classroom
environments where lighting, climate, power, audiovisual equipment,
sensing, panel interaction, and optional visual awareness are
coordinated as one local runtime system.

This model emphasizes teacher-friendly control, local-first execution,
energy-aware behavior, classroom scene control, and optional
cloud-enhanced school-level management.

**ZH-TW  
**智慧教室部署是一種面向教室環境的參考模型，用於將照明、空調、電力、影音設備、感知、面板互動與可選視覺感知協同為一個本地
Runtime 系統。

此模型強調教師友好的控制方式、本地優先執行、能源感知行為、教室場景控制，以及可選的雲端增強校級管理。

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Reference Role** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | Classroom local runtime center |
| Artibird Gate | Device access and local communication gateway |
| Artibird Panel | Teacher-facing room control interface |
| Artibird Switch | Scene trigger, touch input, or relay control by variant |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental sensing for classroom automation |
| Artibird Act | Power control, load control, and energy-related execution |
| Artibird Sync | IR / RF control for air conditioner, projector, display, or AV equipment where supported |
| Artibird Vision | Visual event and room-state awareness where supported |
| OceanAI Cloud | Remote school management, alerts, reports, and lifecycle support where supported |
| OceanAI Edge | AI-assisted classroom context interpretation where deployed |

## **中文表**

| **組件** | **參考角色** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | 教室本地 Runtime 中心 |
| Artibird Gate | 設備接入與本地通訊網關 |
| Artibird Panel | 面向教師的房間控制介面 |
| Artibird Switch | 依版本作為場景觸發、觸控輸入或繼電器控制 |
| Artibird Sense | 用於教室自動化的環境感知 |
| Artibird Act | 電力控制、負載控制與能源相關執行 |
| Artibird Sync | 在支援條件下控制空調、投影機、顯示設備或影音設備的 IR / RF 節點 |
| Artibird Vision | 支援條件下的視覺事件與房間狀態感知 |
| OceanAI Cloud | 支援條件下遠端校級管理、警報、報告與生命週期支援 |
| OceanAI Edge | 部署條件下 AI 輔助教室上下文解讀 |

## **D.6 Smart Office Reference Model**

## **D.6 智慧辦公參考模型**

**EN  
**Smart Office deployment is a reference model for meeting rooms,
workspaces, shared areas, reception areas, and facility zones.

This model supports room interface control, lighting scenes, power
management, environmental sensing, appliance synchronization, and
optional cloud-based remote management.

**ZH-TW  
**智慧辦公部署是一種面向會議室、工位區、共享區域、接待區與設施區域的參考模型。

此模型支援房間介面控制、照明場景、電力管理、環境感知、家電同步，以及可選的雲端遠端管理。

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Reference Role** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | Local runtime center for office zones |
| Artibird Panel | Room-level shared control interface |
| Artibird Switch | Local control and scene trigger |
| Artibird Sense | Occupancy, light, temperature, and environmental input where supported |
| Artibird Act | Plug, relay, and controlled electrical execution |
| Artibird Sync | Appliance or AV synchronization where supported |
| Artibird App | Setup, control, status viewing, and configuration |
| OceanAI Cloud | Remote management and synchronization where supported |

## **中文表**

| **組件**        | **參考角色**                         |
|-----------------|--------------------------------------|
| Artibird Hub    | 辦公區域本地 Runtime 中心            |
| Artibird Panel  | 房間級共享控制介面                   |
| Artibird Switch | 本地控制與場景觸發                   |
| Artibird Sense  | 支援條件下人在、光照、溫度與環境輸入 |
| Artibird Act    | 插座、繼電器與受控電力執行           |
| Artibird Sync   | 支援條件下家電或影音同步             |
| Artibird App    | 設定、控制、狀態查看與配置           |
| OceanAI Cloud   | 支援條件下遠端管理與同步             |

## **D.7 Smart Building Reference Model**

## **D.7 智慧建築參考模型**

**EN  
**Smart Building deployment is a reference model for multi-room,
multi-zone, or multi-floor buildings.

This model requires careful planning of Hub placement, Gate placement,
network topology, device density, room / zone organization, local
runtime scope, cloud participation, capacity limits, and failure
behavior.

**ZH-TW  
**智慧建築部署是一種面向多房間、多區域或多樓層建築的參考模型。

此模型需要仔細規劃 Hub 佈置、Gate 佈置、網路拓撲、設備密度、房間 /
區域組織、本地 Runtime 範圍、雲端參與、容量限制與故障行為。

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Reference Role** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | Local runtime center for building zones or floors |
| Artibird Gate | Device access gateway for zones, floors, or device groups |
| Artibird Panel | Shared room or zone control interface |
| Artibird Act | Electrical execution and power control |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental sensing and automation input |
| Artibird Vision | Visual event and security awareness where supported |
| OceanAI Cloud | Cross-zone visibility, synchronization, alerts, reports, and lifecycle services |
| Artibird App | Setup, operation, room / zone management, and status viewing |

## **中文表**

| **組件**        | **參考角色**                                 |
|-----------------|----------------------------------------------|
| Artibird Hub    | 建築區域或樓層的本地 Runtime 中心            |
| Artibird Gate   | 面向區域、樓層或設備群組的設備接入網關       |
| Artibird Panel  | 共享房間或區域控制介面                       |
| Artibird Act    | 電力執行與電力控制                           |
| Artibird Sense  | 環境感知與自動化輸入                         |
| Artibird Vision | 支援條件下視覺事件與安全感知                 |
| OceanAI Cloud   | 跨區域可視化、同步、警報、報告與生命週期服務 |
| Artibird App    | 設定、操作、房間 / 區域管理與狀態查看        |

## **D.8 Smart Campus Reference Model**

## **D.8 智慧校園參考模型**

**EN  
**Smart Campus deployment is a reference model for multi-building,
multi-site, or institution-level environments.

This model may include classrooms, offices, public areas, outdoor areas,
energy zones, security-related areas, and central management. It
typically requires distributed Hubs, multiple Gates, supported local
runtime zones, cloud-enhanced management, and optional Edge
intelligence.

**ZH-TW  
**智慧校園部署是一種面向多建築、多站點或機構級環境的參考模型。

此模型可包含教室、辦公區、公共區域、戶外區域、能源區域、安全相關區域與中央管理。它通常需要分布式
Hub、多個 Gate、受支援本地 Runtime 區域、雲端增強管理與可選 Edge 智慧。

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Reference Role** |
|----|----|
| Multiple Artibird Hubs | Local runtime centers across buildings or zones |
| Multiple Artibird Gates | Distributed device access gateways |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental sensing across classrooms, offices, and public areas |
| Artibird Act | Electrical execution, load control, and energy behavior |
| Artibird Panel | Room, classroom, or zone control interface |
| Artibird Vision | Visual event and security awareness where supported |
| OceanAI Cloud | Multi-site management, account structure, reports, alerts, and lifecycle services |
| OceanAI Edge | AI-assisted local perception, Vision analysis, sensor fusion, and optimization where deployed |
| Artibird App | User, installer, admin, and site-level control where supported |

## **中文表**

| **組件** | **參考角色** |
|----|----|
| 多個 Artibird Hub | 跨建築或區域的本地 Runtime 中心 |
| 多個 Artibird Gate | 分布式設備接入網關 |
| Artibird Sense | 跨教室、辦公區與公共區域的環境感知 |
| Artibird Act | 電力執行、負載控制與能源行為 |
| Artibird Panel | 房間、教室或區域控制介面 |
| Artibird Vision | 支援條件下視覺事件與安全感知 |
| OceanAI Cloud | 多站點管理、帳號結構、報告、警報與生命週期服務 |
| OceanAI Edge | 部署條件下 AI 輔助本地感知、Vision 分析、感測融合與優化 |
| Artibird App | 支援條件下用戶、安裝方、管理員與站點級控制 |

## **D.9 Energy Management Reference Model**

## **D.9 能源管理參考模型**

**EN  
**Energy Management deployment is a reference model for monitoring,
controlling, reporting, and optimizing supported energy-related
behavior.

This model may use Artibird Act-E or other energy-capable execution
nodes, Artibird Sense, Artibird Hub, OceanAI Cloud, OceanAI Edge, and
Artibird App where supported.

Energy-related statements must be validated. The system should be
described as supporting energy-aware workflows unless controlled
evidence supports stronger claims.

**ZH-TW  
**能源管理部署是一種用於監測、控制、報告與優化受支援能源相關行為的參考模型。

此模型可在支援條件下使用 Artibird Act-E
或其他具備能源能力的執行節點、Artibird Sense、Artibird Hub、OceanAI
Cloud、OceanAI Edge 與 Artibird App。

能源相關表述必須完成驗證。除非具備受控證據支持更強宣稱，否則系統應描述為支援能源感知工作流。

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Reference Role** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | Local runtime and energy-related coordination |
| Artibird Act-E | Energy measurement and electrical execution where supported |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental context for energy behavior |
| OceanAI Cloud | Energy reports, historical data, alerts, and remote monitoring where supported |
| OceanAI Edge | AI-assisted energy interpretation and optimization suggestions where supported |
| Artibird App | Energy status viewing, control, alerts, and configuration |

## **中文表**

| **組件**       | **參考角色**                                 |
|----------------|----------------------------------------------|
| Artibird Hub   | 本地 Runtime 與能源相關協同                  |
| Artibird Act-E | 支援條件下電能計量與電力執行                 |
| Artibird Sense | 能源行為相關環境上下文                       |
| OceanAI Cloud  | 支援條件下能源報告、歷史數據、警報與遠端監測 |
| OceanAI Edge   | 支援條件下 AI 輔助能源解讀與優化建議         |
| Artibird App   | 能源狀態查看、控制、警報與配置               |

## **D.10 Vision-Aware Security Reference Model**

## **D.10 視覺感知安全參考模型**

**EN  
**Vision-Aware Security deployment is a reference model for supported
visual event awareness, local recording, AI-assisted visual
interpretation, alerts, remote viewing, and privacy-aware processing.

This model must be described within privacy, storage, access, retention,
and validation boundaries. It must not be described as perfect
detection, guaranteed security, or unrestricted surveillance.

**ZH-TW  
**視覺感知安全部署是一種面向受支援視覺事件感知、本地錄影、AI
輔助視覺解讀、警報、遠端查看與隱私導向處理的參考模型。

此模型必須在隱私、儲存、存取、保留與驗證邊界內描述。不得描述為完美偵測、保證安全或不受限制監控。

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Reference Role** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Vision | Visual event source, local recording, and visual context |
| Artibird Hub | Local runtime processing and alert routing |
| OceanAI Edge | AI-assisted visual interpretation where deployed |
| OceanAI Cloud | Remote alerts, remote viewing, event history, and account-based access where supported |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental context to support visual interpretation where supported |
| Artibird Act | Controlled response action where supported |
| Artibird App | Alert receiving, remote viewing, configuration, and privacy settings |

## **中文表**

| **組件**        | **參考角色**                                           |
|-----------------|--------------------------------------------------------|
| Artibird Vision | 視覺事件來源、本地錄影與視覺上下文                     |
| Artibird Hub    | 本地 Runtime 處理與警報路由                            |
| OceanAI Edge    | 部署條件下 AI 輔助視覺解讀                             |
| OceanAI Cloud   | 支援條件下遠端警報、遠端查看、事件歷史與基於帳號的存取 |
| Artibird Sense  | 支援條件下提供環境上下文以輔助視覺解讀                 |
| Artibird Act    | 支援條件下受控回應動作                                 |
| Artibird App    | 警報接收、遠端查看、配置與隱私設定                     |

## **D.11 Agriculture / Irrigation Reference Model**

## **D.11 農業 / 灌溉參考模型**

**EN  
**Agriculture / Irrigation deployment is a reference model for supported
outdoor, semi-outdoor, irrigation, environmental sensing, power control,
and remote monitoring scenarios.

This model requires careful validation of environmental protection,
power availability, communication range, network stability, device
placement, local runtime behavior, cloud participation, and
outdoor-related constraints.

**ZH-TW  
**農業 /
灌溉部署是一種面向受支援戶外、半戶外、灌溉、環境感知、電力控制與遠端監測場景的參考模型。

此模型需要仔細驗證環境防護、供電可用性、通訊距離、網路穩定性、設備佈置、本地
Runtime 行為、雲端參與與戶外相關限制。

## **English Table**

| **Component** | **Reference Role** |
|----|----|
| Artibird Hub | Local coordination where deployed |
| Artibird Gate | Device access gateway and communication path |
| Artibird Sense | Environmental sensing for soil, temperature, humidity, light, or related signals where supported |
| Artibird Act | Irrigation control, relay control, pump control, or load control where supported |
| OceanAI Cloud | Remote monitoring, alerts, history, and lifecycle services where supported |
| Artibird App | Setup, control, status viewing, and alert access |
| OceanAI Edge | AI-assisted interpretation where deployed and validated |

## **中文表**

| **組件**       | **參考角色**                                             |
|----------------|----------------------------------------------------------|
| Artibird Hub   | 部署條件下本地協同                                       |
| Artibird Gate  | 設備接入網關與通訊路徑                                   |
| Artibird Sense | 支援條件下用於土壤、溫度、濕度、光照或相關信號的環境感知 |
| Artibird Act   | 支援條件下灌溉控制、繼電器控制、水泵控制或負載控制       |
| OceanAI Cloud  | 支援條件下遠端監測、警報、歷史與生命週期服務             |
| Artibird App   | 設定、控制、狀態查看與警報存取                           |
| OceanAI Edge   | 部署且驗證條件下 AI 輔助解讀                             |

## **D.12 Deployment Planning Checklist**

## **D.12 部署規劃清單**

**EN  
**Each deployment should be planned with a clear checklist before
installation, validation, commercial proposal, or customer delivery.

**ZH-TW  
**每個部署在安裝、驗證、商業方案或客戶交付之前，都應依清楚的清單完成規劃。

## **English Table**

| **Planning Item** | **Required Definition** |
|----|----|
| Deployment scenario | Smart home, classroom, office, building, campus, energy, security, agriculture, or infrastructure |
| Required components | Hub, Gate, Switch, Panel, Act, Sense, Sync, Vision, Cloud, Edge, App where applicable |
| Site structure | Home, room, classroom, office, floor, building, campus, zone, or field |
| Network topology | Ethernet, Wi-Fi, BLE Mesh, Wi-Fi Mesh where supported, local network, cloud path |
| Power condition | Power source, backup need, battery condition, outage behavior |
| Local runtime requirement | Hub, ArtiOS, scene, automation, state, MQTT, and local service needs |
| Cloud requirement | Remote access, sync, alerts, reports, lifecycle, multi-site support |
| Edge requirement | Vision analysis, sensor fusion, AI-assisted interpretation, optimization |
| Device count | Devices per room, zone, Gate, Hub, site, or account |
| Capacity boundary | Validated device count, message rate, latency, storage, and processing limit |
| Security requirement | Account binding, access control, device identity, secure communication |
| Privacy requirement | Vision data, Edge data, cloud data, retention, access, and deletion |
| Validation requirement | Functional, runtime, connectivity, capacity, reliability, security, privacy, and deployment tests |

## **中文表**

| **規劃項目** | **必須定義內容** |
|----|----|
| 部署場景 | 智慧住宅、教室、辦公、建築、校園、能源、安全、農業或基礎設施 |
| 所需組件 | 適用時 Hub、Gate、Switch、Panel、Act、Sense、Sync、Vision、Cloud、Edge、App |
| 場地結構 | 住宅、房間、教室、辦公室、樓層、建築、校園、區域或田地 |
| 網路拓撲 | Ethernet、Wi-Fi、支援條件下 BLE Mesh / Wi-Fi Mesh、本地網路、雲端路徑 |
| 供電條件 | 電源來源、備援需求、電池條件、斷電行為 |
| 本地 Runtime 要求 | Hub、ArtiOS、場景、自動化、狀態、MQTT 與本地服務需求 |
| 雲端要求 | 遠端存取、同步、警報、報告、生命週期、多站點支援 |
| Edge 要求 | Vision 分析、感測融合、AI 輔助解讀、優化 |
| 設備數量 | 每房間、區域、Gate、Hub、站點或帳號設備數 |
| 容量邊界 | 已驗證設備數、消息速率、延遲、儲存與處理限制 |
| 安全要求 | 帳號綁定、存取控制、設備身份、安全通訊 |
| 隱私要求 | Vision 數據、Edge 數據、雲端數據、保留、存取與刪除 |
| 驗證要求 | 功能、Runtime、連接、容量、可靠性、安全、隱私與部署測試 |

## **D.13 Deployment Boundary**

## **D.13 部署邊界**

**EN  
**Deployment reference models must be interpreted as planning
references, not universal installation guarantees.

A deployment model must be validated according to actual site
conditions, supported product versions, hardware versions, firmware
versions, software versions, network topology, power condition, device
count, cloud availability, Edge deployment status, environmental
condition, privacy requirement, and capacity boundary.

**ZH-TW  
**部署參考模型應被理解為規劃參考，而不是通用安裝保證。

部署模型必須依據實際場地條件、受支援產品版本、硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、網路拓撲、供電條件、設備數量、雲端可用性、Edge
部署狀態、環境條件、隱私要求與容量邊界完成驗證。

## **D.14 Validation Requirements**

## **D.14 驗證要求**

**EN  
**Any deployment claim involving supported scenario, required
components, device count, network coverage, local runtime behavior,
cloud participation, Edge-assisted behavior, energy behavior, Vision
behavior, outdoor use, failure behavior, or acceptance result must be
validated under defined deployment conditions.

Validation should include scenario type, site condition, product mix,
hardware version, firmware version, software version, network topology,
device count, power condition, cloud condition, Edge condition,
environmental condition, expected behavior, observed result, failure
behavior, and acceptance criteria.

**ZH-TW  
**任何涉及受支援場景、所需組件、設備數量、網路覆蓋、本地 Runtime
行為、雲端參與、Edge 輔助行為、能源行為、Vision
行為、戶外使用、故障行為或驗收結果的部署宣稱，都必須在明確部署條件下完成驗證。

驗證應包含場景類型、場地條件、產品組合、硬體版本、韌體版本、軟體版本、網路拓撲、設備數量、供電條件、雲端條件、Edge
條件、環境條件、預期行為、觀察結果、故障行為與驗收標準。

## **D.15 Appendix Conclusion**

## **D.15 附錄結論**

**EN  
**This appendix defines deployment reference models for the OceanAI /
Artibird system. It explains how Smart Home, Smart Classroom, Smart
Office, Smart Building, Smart Campus, Energy Management, Vision-Aware
Security, and Agriculture / Irrigation deployments may be planned using
supported OceanAI and Artibird components within defined local, cloud,
edge, capacity, security, privacy, and validation boundaries.

**ZH-TW  
**本附錄定義了 OceanAI / Artibird
系統的部署參考模型。它說明智慧住宅、智慧教室、智慧辦公、智慧建築、智慧校園、能源管理、視覺感知安全與農業
/
灌溉部署，如何在已定義本地、雲端、Edge、容量、安全、隱私與驗證邊界內，使用受支援
OceanAI 與 Artibird 組件進行規劃。

完成聲明

# **完成聲明**

# **Document End**

# **文件結束**

## **EN**

This **OceanAI / Artibird System Specification v1.0** is now completed
as the foundational system-level reference document for the OceanAI /
Artibird coordinated intelligent environment system.

It defines the baseline structure for system architecture, runtime
behavior, component participation, device modeling, data and event flow,
networking, local-first operation, cloud enhancement, edge intelligence,
security, privacy, reliability, deployment, capacity, validation,
commercial claim boundaries, revision control, terminology,
product-system mapping, system validation, and deployment reference
models.

This document should be used as the primary system-level reference for:

- Product engineering specifications

- Commercial specifications

- Product catalogs

- Website and channel materials

- Deployment planning

- Validation reports

- Installation and training documents

- Future architecture upgrades

Any future update, product addition, deployment expansion, capacity
claim, AI-assisted function, cloud service, Edge capability, security
mechanism, privacy rule, or commercial statement should remain aligned
with the boundaries and validation principles defined in this document.

## **ZH-TW**

本 **《OceanAI / Artibird 系統規格書 v1.0》** 現已完成，作為 OceanAI /
Artibird 協同智慧空間系統的基礎系統級參考文件。

本文件定義了系統架構、Runtime
行為、組件參與、設備模型、數據與事件流、網路、本地優先運作、雲端增強、邊緣智慧、安全、隱私、可靠性、部署、容量、驗證、商業宣稱邊界、版本控制、術語、產品—系統映射、系統驗證與部署參考模型的基礎結構。

本文件應作為以下文件與工作的主要系統級參考：

- 產品工程規格書

- 商業規格書

- 產品型錄

- 網站與渠道材料

- 部署規劃

- 驗證報告

- 安裝與培訓文件

- 未來架構升級文件

任何未來更新、產品新增、部署擴展、容量宣稱、AI 輔助功能、雲端服務、Edge
能力、安全機制、隱私規則或商業表述，都應與本文件所定義的邊界與驗證原則保持一致。
